sakhījanasamāvṛtāgṛhītā balavat kubjā sā tadgṛham anādayat  Ramtataḥ subhṛśasaṃtaptas tasyāḥ sarvaḥ sakhījanaḥkruddham ājñāya śatrughnaṃ vyapalāyata sarvaśaḥ  Ramamantrayata kṛtsnaś ca tasyāḥ sarvasakhījanaḥyathāyaṃ samupakrānto niḥśeṣaṃ naḥ kariṣyati  Ramsānukrośāṃ vadānyāṃ ca dharmajñāṃ ca yaśasvinīmkausalyāṃ śaraṇaṃ yāmaḥ sā hi no stu dhruvā gatiḥ  Ramsa ca roṣeṇa tāmrākṣaḥ śatrughnaḥ śatrutāpanaḥvicakarṣa tadā kubjāṃ krośantīṃ pṛthivītale  Ramtasyā hy ākṛṣyamāṇāyā mantharāyās tatas tataḥcitraṃ bahuvidhaṃ bhāṇḍaṃ pṛthivyāṃ tad vyaśīryata  Ramtena bhāṇḍena saṃkīrṇaṃ śrīmadrājaniveśanamaśobhata tadā bhūyaḥ śāradaṃ gaganaṃ yathā  Ramsa balī balavat krodhād gṛhītvā puruṣarṣabhaḥkaikeyīm abhinirbhartsya babhāṣe paruṣaṃ vacaḥ  Ramtair vākyaiḥ paruṣair duḥkhaiḥ kaikeyī bhṛśaduḥkhitāśatrughnabhayasaṃtrastā putraṃ śaraṇam āgatā  Ramtāṃ prekṣya bharataḥ kruddhaṃ śatrughnam idam abravītavadhyāḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ pramadāḥ kṣamyatām iti  Ramhanyām aham imāṃ pāpāṃ kaikeyīṃ duṣṭacāriṇīmyadi māṃ dhārmiko rāmo nāsūyen mātṛghātakam  Ramimām api hatāṃ kubjāṃ yadi jānāti rāghavaḥtvāṃ ca māṃ caiva dharmātmā nābhibhāṣiṣyate dhruvam  Rambharatasya vacaḥ śrutvā śatrughno lakṣmaṇānujaḥnyavartata tato roṣāt tāṃ mumoca ca mantharām  Ramsā pādamūle kaikeyyā mantharā nipapāta haniḥśvasantī suduḥkhārtā kṛpaṇaṃ vilalāpa ca  Ramśatrughnavikṣepavimūḍhasaṃjñāṃ samīkṣya kubjāṃ bharatasya mātāśanaiḥ samāśvāsayad ārtarūpāṃ krauñcīṃ vilagnām iva vīkṣamāṇām  Ramtataḥ prabhātasamaye divase tha caturdaśesametya rājakartāro bharataṃ vākyam abruvan  Ramgato daśarathaḥ svargaṃ yo no gurutaro guruḥrāmaṃ pravrājya vai jyeṣṭhaṃ lakṣmaṇaṃ ca mahābalam  Ramtvam adya bhava no rājā rājaputra mahāyaśaḥsaṃgatyā nāparādhnoti rājyam etad anāyakam  Ramābhiṣecanikaṃ sarvam idam ādāya rāghavapratīkṣate tvāṃ svajanaḥ śreṇayaś ca nṛpātmaja  Ramrājyaṃ gṛhāṇa bharata pitṛpaitāmahaṃ mahatabhiṣecaya cātmānaṃ pāhi cāsmān nararṣabha  Ramābhiṣecanikaṃ bhāṇḍaṃ kṛtvā sarvaṃ pradakṣiṇambharatas taṃ janaṃ sarvaṃ pratyuvāca dhṛtavrataḥ  Ramjyeṣṭhasya rājatā nityam ucitā hi kulasya naḥnaivaṃ bhavanto māṃ vaktum arhanti kuśalā janāḥ  Ramrāmaḥ pūrvo hi no bhrātā bhaviṣyati mahīpatiḥahaṃ tv araṇye vatsyāmi varṣāṇi nava pañca ca  Ramyujyatāṃ mahatī senā caturaṅgamahābalāānayiṣyāmy ahaṃ jyeṣṭhaṃ bhrātaraṃ rāghavaṃ vanāt  Ramābhiṣecanikaṃ caiva sarvam etad upaskṛtampuraskṛtya gamiṣyāmi rāmahetor vanaṃ prati  Ramtatraiva taṃ naravyāghram abhiṣicya puraskṛtamāneṣyāmi tu vai rāmaṃ havyavāham ivādhvarāt  Ramna sakāmāṃ kariṣyāmi svām imāṃ mātṛgandhinīmvane vatsyāmy ahaṃ durge rāmo rājā bhaviṣyati  Ramkriyatāṃ śilpibhiḥ panthāḥ samāni viṣamāṇi carakṣiṇaś cānusaṃyāntu pathi durgavicārakāḥ  Ramevaṃ sambhāṣamāṇaṃ taṃ rāmahetor nṛpātmajampratyuvāca janaḥ sarvaḥ śrīmadvākyam anuttamam  Ramevaṃ te bhāṣamāṇasya padmā śrīr upatiṣṭhatāmyas tvaṃ jyeṣṭhe nṛpasute pṛthivīṃ dātum icchasi  Ramanuttamaṃ tad vacanaṃ nṛpātmaja prabhāṣitaṃ saṃśravaṇe niśamya capraharṣajās taṃ prati bāṣpabindavo nipetur āryānananetrasambhavāḥ  Ramūcus te vacanam idaṃ niśamya hṛṣṭāḥ sāmātyāḥ sapariṣado viyātaśokāḥpanthānaṃ naravarabhaktimāñ janaś ca vyādiṣṭas tava vacanāc ca śilpivargaḥ  Ramatha bhūmipradeśajñāḥ sūtrakarmaviśāradāḥsvakarmābhiratāḥ śūrāḥ khanakā yantrakās tathā  Ramkarmāntikāḥ sthapatayaḥ puruṣā yantrakovidāḥtathā vardhakayaś caiva mārgiṇo vṛkṣatakṣakāḥ  Ramkūpakārāḥ sudhākārā vaṃśakarmakṛtas tathāsamarthā ye ca draṣṭāraḥ puratas te pratasthire  Ramsa tu harṣāt tam uddeśaṃ janaugho vipulaḥ prayānaśobhata mahāvegaḥ sāgarasyeva parvaṇi  Ramte svavāraṃ samāsthāya vartmakarmāṇi kovidāḥkaraṇair vividhopetaiḥ purastāt sampratasthire  Ramlatāvallīś ca gulmāṃś ca sthāṇūn aśmana eva cajanās te cakrire mārgaṃ chindanto vividhān drumān  Ramavṛkṣeṣu ca deśeṣu kecid vṛkṣān aropayankecit kuṭhāraiṣ ṭaṅkaiś ca dātraiś chindan kvacit kvacit  Ramapare vīraṇastambān balino balavattarāḥvidhamanti sma durgāṇi sthalāni ca tatas tataḥ  Ramapare pūrayan kūpān pāṃsubhiḥ śvabhram āyatamnimnabhāgāṃs tathā kecit samāṃś cakruḥ samantataḥ  Rambabandhur bandhanīyāṃś ca kṣodyān saṃcukṣudus tadābibhidur bhedanīyāṃś ca tāṃs tān deśān narās tadā  Ramacireṇaiva kālena parivāhān bahūdakāncakrur bahuvidhākārān sāgarapratimān bahūnudapānān bahuvidhān vedikāparimaṇḍitān  Ramsa sudhākuṭṭimatalaḥ prapuṣpitamahīruhaḥmattodghuṣṭadvijagaṇaḥ patākābhir alaṃkṛtaḥ  Ramcandanodakasaṃsikto nānākusumabhūṣitaḥbahv aśobhata senāyāḥ panthāḥ svargapathopamaḥ  Ramājñāpyātha yathājñapti yuktās te dhikṛtā narāḥramaṇīyeṣu deśeṣu bahusvāduphaleṣu ca  Ramyo niveśas tv abhipreto bharatasya mahātmanaḥbhūyas taṃ śobhayāmāsur bhūṣābhir bhūṣaṇopamam  Ramnakṣatreṣu praśasteṣu muhūrteṣu ca tadvidaḥniveśaṃ sthāpayāmāsur bharatasya mahātmanaḥ  Rambahupāṃsucayāś cāpi parikhāparivāritāḥtatrendrakīlapratimāḥ pratolīvaraśobhitāḥ  Ramprāsādamālāsaṃyuktāḥ saudhaprākārasaṃvṛtāḥpatākāśobhitāḥ sarve sunirmitamahāpathāḥ  Ramvisarpadbhir ivākāśe viṭaṅkāgravimānakaiḥsamucchritair niveśās te babhuḥ śakrapuropamāḥ  Ramjāhnavīṃ tu samāsādya vividhadrumakānanāmśītalāmalapānīyāṃ mahāmīnasamākulām  Ramsacandratārāgaṇamaṇḍitaṃ yathā nabhaḥ kṣapāyām amalaṃ virājatenarendramārgaḥ sa tathā vyarājata krameṇa ramyaḥ śubhaśilpinirmitaḥ  Ramtato nāndīmukhīṃ rātriṃ bharataṃ sūtamāgadhāḥtuṣṭuvur vāgviśeṣajñāḥ stavair maṅgalasaṃhitaiḥ  Ramsuvarṇakoṇābhihataḥ prāṇadad yāmadundubhiḥdadhmuḥ śaṅkhāṃś ca śataśo vādyāṃś coccāvacasvarān  Ramsa tūryaghoṣaḥ sumahān divam āpūrayann ivabharataṃ śokasaṃtaptaṃ bhūyaḥ śokair arandhrayat  Ramtataḥ prabuddho bharatas taṃ ghoṣaṃ saṃnivartya canāhaṃ rājeti cāpy uktvā śatrughnam idam abravīt  Rampaśya śatrughna kaikeyyā lokasyāpakṛtaṃ mahatvisṛjya mayi duḥkhāni rājā daśaratho gataḥ  Ramtasyaiṣā dharmarājasya dharmamūlā mahātmanaḥparibhramati rājaśrīr naur ivākarṇikā jale  Ramity evaṃ bharataṃ prekṣya vilapantaṃ vicetanamkṛpaṇaṃ ruruduḥ sarvāḥ sasvaraṃ yoṣitas tadā  Ramtathā tasmin vilapati vasiṣṭho rājadharmavitsabhām ikṣvākunāthasya praviveśa mahāyaśāḥ  Ramśātakumbhamayīṃ ramyāṃ maṇiratnasamākulāmsudharmām iva dharmātmā sagaṇaḥ pratyapadyata  Ramsa kāñcanamayaṃ pīṭhaṃ parārdhyāstaraṇāvṛtamadhyāsta sarvavedajño dūtān anuśaśāsa ca  Rambrāhmaṇān kṣatriyān yodhān amātyān gaṇavallabhānkṣipram ānayatāvyagrāḥ kṛtyam ātyayikaṃ hi naḥ  Ramtato halahalāśabdo mahān samudapadyatarathair aśvair gajaiś cāpi janānām upagacchatām  Ramtato bharatam āyāntaṃ śatakratum ivāmarāḥpratyanandan prakṛtayo yathā daśarathaṃ tathā  Ramhrada iva timināgasaṃvṛtaḥ stimitajalo maṇiśaṅkhaśarkaraḥdaśarathasutaśobhitā sabhā sadaśaratheva babhau yathā purā  Ramtām āryagaṇasampūrṇāṃ bharataḥ pragrahāṃ sabhāmdadarśa buddhisampannaḥ pūrṇacandrāṃ niśām iva  Ramāsanāni yathānyāyam āryāṇāṃ viśatāṃ tadāadṛśyata ghanāpāye pūrṇacandreva śarvarī  Ramrājñas tu prakṛtīḥ sarvāḥ samagrāḥ prekṣya dharmavitidaṃ purohito vākyaṃ bharataṃ mṛdu cābravīt  Ramtāta rājā daśarathaḥ svargato dharmam ācarandhanadhānyavatīṃ sphītāṃ pradāya pṛthivīṃ tava  Ramrāmas tathā satyadhṛtiḥ satāṃ dharmam anusmarannājahāt pitur ādeśaṃ śaśī jyotsnām ivoditaḥ  Rampitrā bhrātrā ca te dattaṃ rājyaṃ nihatakaṇṭakamtad bhuṅkṣva muditāmātyaḥ kṣipram evābhiṣecaya  Ramudīcyāś ca pratīcyāś ca dākṣiṇātyāś ca kevalāḥkoṭyāparāntāḥ sāmudrā ratnāny abhiharantu te  Ramtac chrutvā bharato vākyaṃ śokenābhipariplutaḥjagāma manasā rāmaṃ dharmajño dharmakāṅkṣayā  Ramsa bāṣpakalayā vācā kalahaṃsasvaro yuvāvilalāpa sabhāmadhye jagarhe ca purohitam  Ramcaritabrahmacaryasya vidyā snātasya dhīmataḥdharme prayatamānasya ko rājyaṃ madvidho haret  Ramkathaṃ daśarathāj jāto bhaved rājyāpahārakaḥrājyaṃ cāhaṃ ca rāmasya dharmaṃ vaktum ihārhasi  Ramjyeṣṭhaḥ śreṣṭhaś ca dharmātmā dilīpanahuṣopamaḥlabdhum arhati kākutstho rājyaṃ daśaratho yathā  Ramanāryajuṣṭam asvargyaṃ kuryāṃ pāpam ahaṃ yadiikṣvākūṇām ahaṃ loke bhaveyaṃ kulapāṃsanaḥ  Ramyaddhi mātrā kṛtaṃ pāpaṃ nāhaṃ tad abhirocayeihastho vanadurgasthaṃ namasyāmi kṛtāñjaliḥ  Ramrāmam evānugacchāmi sa rājā dvipadāṃ varaḥtrayāṇām api lokānāṃ rāghavo rājyam arhati  Ramtad vākyaṃ dharmasaṃyuktaṃ śrutvā sarve sabhāsadaḥharṣān mumucur aśrūṇi rāme nihitacetasaḥ  Ramyadi tv āryaṃ na śakṣyāmi vinivartayituṃ vanātvane tatraiva vatsyāmi yathāryo lakṣmaṇas tathā  Ramsarvopāyaṃ tu vartiṣye vinivartayituṃ balātsamakṣam āryamiśrāṇāṃ sādhūnāṃ guṇavartinām  Ramevam uktvā tu dharmātmā bharato bhrātṛvatsalaḥsamīpastham uvācedaṃ sumantraṃ mantrakovidam  Ramtūrṇam utthāya gaccha tvaṃ sumantra mama śāsanātyātrām ājñāpaya kṣipraṃ balaṃ caiva samānaya  Ramevam uktaḥ sumantras tu bharatena mahātmanāprahṛṣṭaḥ so diśat sarvaṃ yathā saṃdiṣṭam iṣṭavat  Ramtāḥ prahṛṣṭāḥ prakṛtayo balādhyakṣā balasya caśrutvā yātrāṃ samājñaptāṃ rāghavasya nivartane  Ramtato yodhāṅganāḥ sarvā bhartṝn sarvān gṛhe gṛheyātrāgamanam ājñāya tvarayanti sma harṣitāḥ  Ramte hayair gorathaiḥ śīghraiḥ syandanaiś ca manojavaiḥsaha yodhair balādhyakṣā balaṃ sarvam acodayan  Ramsajjaṃ tu tad balaṃ dṛṣṭvā bharato gurusaṃnidhaurathaṃ me tvarayasveti sumantraṃ pārśvato bravīt  Rambharatasya tu tasyājñāṃ pratigṛhya praharṣitaḥrathaṃ gṛhītvā prayayau yuktaṃ paramavājibhiḥ  Ramsa rāghavaḥ satyadhṛtiḥ pratāpavān bruvan suyuktaṃ dṛḍhasatyavikramaḥguruṃ mahāraṇyagataṃ yaśasvinaṃ prasādayiṣyan bharato bravīt tadā  Ramtūrṇaṃ samutthāya sumantra gaccha balasya yogāya balapradhānānānetum icchāmi hi taṃ vanasthaṃ prasādya rāmaṃ jagato hitāya  Ramsa sūtaputro bharatena samyag ājñāpitaḥ saṃparipūrṇakāmaḥśaśāsa sarvān prakṛtipradhānān balasya mukhyāṃś ca suhṛjjanaṃ ca  Ramtataḥ samutthāya kule kule te rājanyavaiśyā vṛṣalāś ca viprāḥayūyujann uṣṭrarathān kharāṃś ca nāgān hayāṃś caiva kulaprasūtān  Ramtataḥ samutthitaḥ kālyam āsthāya syandanottamamprayayau bharataḥ śīghraṃ rāmadarśanakāṅkṣayā  Ramagrataḥ prayayus tasya sarve mantripurodhasaḥadhiruhya hayair yuktān rathān sūryarathopamān  Ramnavanāgasahasrāṇi kalpitāni yathāvidhianvayur bharataṃ yāntam ikṣvākukulanandanam  Ramṣaṣṭhī rathasahasrāṇi dhanvino vividhāyudhāḥanvayur bharataṃ yāntaṃ rājaputraṃ yaśasvinam  Ramśataṃ sahasrāṇy aśvānāṃ samārūḍhāni rāghavamanvayur bharataṃ yāntaṃ rājaputraṃ yaśasvinam  Ramkaikeyī ca sumitrā ca kausalyā ca yaśasvinīrāmānayanasaṃhṛṣṭā yayur yānena bhāsvatā  Ramprayātāś cāryasaṃghātā rāmaṃ draṣṭuṃ salakṣmaṇamtasyaiva ca kathāś citrāḥ kurvāṇā hṛṣṭamānasāḥ  Rammeghaśyāmaṃ mahābāhuṃ sthirasattvaṃ dṛḍhavratamkadā drakṣyāmahe rāmaṃ jagataḥ śokanāśanam  Ramdṛṣṭa eva hi naḥ śokam apaneṣyati rāghavaḥtamaḥ sarvasya lokasya samudyann iva bhāskaraḥ  Ramity evaṃ kathayantas te samprahṛṣṭāḥ kathāḥ śubhāḥpariṣvajānāś cānyonyaṃ yayur nāgarikās tadā  Ramye ca tatrāpare sarve saṃmatā ye ca naigamāḥrāmaṃ prati yayur hṛṣṭāḥ sarvāḥ prakṛtayas tadā  Rammaṇikārāś ca ye kecit kumbhakārāś ca śobhanāḥsūtrakarmakṛtaś caiva ye ca śastropajīvinaḥ  Rammāyūrakāḥ krākacikā rocakā vedhakās tathādantakārāḥ sudhākārās tathā gandhopajīvinaḥ  Ramsuvarṇakārāḥ prakhyātās tathā kambaladhāvakāḥsnāpakācchādakā vaidyā dhūpakāḥ śauṇḍikās tathā  Ramrajakās tunnavāyāś ca grāmaghoṣamahattarāḥśailūṣāś ca saha strībhir yānti kaivartakās tathā  Ramsamāhitā vedavido brāhmaṇā vṛttasaṃmatāḥgorathair bharataṃ yāntam anujagmuḥ sahasraśaḥ  Ramsuveṣāḥ śuddhavasanās tāmramṛṣṭānulepanāḥsarve te vividhair yānaiḥ śanair bharatam anvayuḥ  Ramprahṛṣṭamuditā senā sānvayāt kaikayīsutamvyavātiṣṭhata sā senā bharatasyānuyāyinī  Ramnirīkṣyānugatāṃ senāṃ tāṃ ca gaṅgāṃ śivodakāmbharataḥ sacivān sarvān abravīd vākyakovidaḥ  Ramniveśayata me sainyam abhiprāyeṇa sarvaśaḥviśrāntāḥ pratariṣyāmaḥ śva idānīṃ mahānadīm  Ramdātuṃ ca tāvad icchāmi svar gatasya mahīpateḥaurdhvadehanimittārtham avatīryodakaṃ nadīm  Ramtasyaivaṃ bruvato mātyās tathety uktvā samāhitāḥnyaveśayaṃs tāṃś chandena svena svena pṛthakpṛthak  Ramniveśya gaṅgām anu tāṃ mahānadīṃ camūṃ vidhānaiḥ paribarhaśobhinīmuvāsa rāmasya tadā mahātmano vicintayāno bharato nivartanam  Ramtato niviṣṭāṃ dhvajinīṃ gaṅgām anvāśritāṃ nadīmniṣādarājo dṛṣṭvaiva jñātīn saṃtvarito bravīt  Rammahatīyam ataḥ senā sāgarābhā pradṛśyatenāsyāntam avagacchāmi manasāpi vicintayan  Ramsa eṣa hi mahākāyaḥ kovidāradhvajo rathebandhayiṣyati vā dāśān atha vāsmān vadhiṣyati  Ramatha dāśarathiṃ rāmaṃ pitrā rājyād vivāsitambharataḥ kaikeyīputro hantuṃ samadhigacchati  Rambhartā caiva sakhā caiva rāmo dāśarathir mamatasyārthakāmāḥ saṃnaddhā gaṅgānūpe tra tiṣṭhata  Ramtiṣṭhantu sarvadāśāś ca gaṅgām anvāśritā nadīmbalayuktā nadīrakṣā māṃsamūlaphalāśanāḥ  Ramnāvāṃ śatānāṃ pañcānāṃ kaivartānāṃ śataṃ śatamsaṃnaddhānāṃ tathā yūnāṃ tiṣṭhantv ity abhyacodayat  Ramyadā tuṣṭas tu bharato rāmasyeha bhaviṣyatiseyaṃ svastimayī senā gaṅgām adya tariṣyati  Ramity uktvopāyanaṃ gṛhya matsyamāṃsamadhūni caabhicakrāma bharataṃ niṣādādhipatir guhaḥ  Ramtam āyāntaṃ tu samprekṣya sūtaputraḥ pratāpavānbharatāyācacakṣe tha vinayajño vinītavat  Rameṣa jñātisahasreṇa sthapatiḥ parivāritaḥkuśalo daṇḍakāraṇye vṛddho bhrātuś ca te sakhā  Ramtasmāt paśyatu kākutstha tvāṃ niṣādādhipo guhaḥasaṃśayaṃ vijānīte yatra tau rāmalakṣmaṇau  Rametat tu vacanaṃ śrutvā sumantrād bharataḥ śubhamuvāca vacanaṃ śīghraṃ guhaḥ paśyatu mām iti  Ramlabdhvābhyanujñāṃ saṃhṛṣṭo jñātibhiḥ parivāritaḥāgamya bharataṃ prahvo guho vacanam abravīt  Ramniṣkuṭaś caiva deśo yaṃ vañcitāś cāpi te vayamnivedayāmas te sarve svake dāśakule vasa  Ramasti mūlaṃ phalaṃ caiva niṣādaiḥ samupāhṛtamārdraṃ ca māṃsaṃ śuṣkaṃ ca vanyaṃ coccāvacaṃ mahat  Ramāśaṃse svāśitā senā vatsyatīmāṃ vibhāvarīmarcito vividhaiḥ kāmaiḥ śvaḥ sasainyo gamiṣyasi  Ramevam uktas tu bharato niṣādādhipatiṃ guhampratyuvāca mahāprājño vākyaṃ hetvarthasaṃhitam  Ramūrjitaḥ khalu te kāmaḥ kṛto mama guroḥ sakheyo me tvam īdṛśīṃ senām eko bhyarcitum icchasi  Ramity uktvā tu mahātejā guhaṃ vacanam uttamamabravīd bharataḥ śrīmān niṣādādhipatiṃ punaḥ  Ramkatareṇa gamiṣyāmi bharadvājāśramaṃ guhagahano yaṃ bhṛśaṃ deśo gaṅgānūpo duratyayaḥ  Ramtasya tadvacanaṃ śrutvā rājaputrasya dhīmataḥabravīt prāñjalir vākyaṃ guho gahanagocaraḥ  Ramdāśās tv anugamiṣyanti dhanvinaḥ susamāhitāḥahaṃ cānugamiṣyāmi rājaputra mahāyaśaḥ  Ramkaccin na duṣṭo vrajasi rāmasyākliṣṭakarmaṇaḥiyaṃ te mahatī senā śaṅkāṃ janayatīva me  Ramtam evam abhibhāṣantam ākāśa iva nirmalaḥbharataḥ ślakṣṇayā vācā guhaṃ vacanam abravīt  Rammā bhūt sa kālo yat kaṣṭaṃ na māṃ śaṅkitum arhasirāghavaḥ sa hi me bhrātā jyeṣṭhaḥ pitṛsamo mama  Ramtaṃ nivartayituṃ yāmi kākutsthaṃ vanavāsinambuddhir anyā na te kāryā guha satyaṃ bravīmi te  Ramsa tu saṃhṛṣṭavadanaḥ śrutvā bharatabhāṣitampunar evābravīd vākyaṃ bharataṃ prati harṣitaḥ  Ramdhanyas tvaṃ na tvayā tulyaṃ paśyāmi jagatītaleayatnād āgataṃ rājyaṃ yas tvaṃ tyaktum ihecchasi  Ramśāśvatī khalu te kīrtir lokān anucariṣyatiyas tvaṃ kṛcchragataṃ rāmaṃ pratyānayitum icchasi  Ramevaṃ sambhāṣamāṇasya guhasya bharataṃ tadābabhau naṣṭaprabhaḥ sūryo rajanī cābhyavartata  Ramsaṃniveśya sa tāṃ senāṃ guhena paritoṣitaḥśatrughnena saha śrīmāñ śayanaṃ punar āgamat  Ramrāmacintāmayaḥ śoko bharatasya mahātmanaḥupasthito hy anarhasya dharmaprekṣasya tādṛśaḥ  Ramantardāhena dahanaḥ saṃtāpayati rāghavamvanadāhābhisaṃtaptaṃ gūḍho gnir iva pādapam  Ramprasrutaḥ sarvagātrebhyaḥ svedaḥ śokāgnisambhavaḥyathā sūryāṃśusaṃtapto himavān prasruto himam  Ramdhyānanirdaraśailena viniḥśvasitadhātunādainyapādapasaṃghena śokāyāsādhiśṛṅgiṇā  Rampramohānantasattvena saṃtāpauṣadhiveṇunāākrānto duḥkhaśailena mahatā kaikayīsutaḥ  Ramguhena sārdhaṃ bharataḥ samāgato mahānubhāvaḥ sajanaḥ samāhitaḥsudurmanās taṃ bharataṃ tadā punar guhaḥ samāśvāsayad agrajaṃ prati  Ramācacakṣe tha sadbhāvaṃ lakṣmaṇasya mahātmanaḥbharatāyāprameyāya guho gahanagocaraḥ  Ramtaṃ jāgrataṃ guṇair yuktaṃ varacāpeṣudhāriṇambhrātṛguptyartham atyantam ahaṃ lakṣmaṇam abruvam  Ramiyaṃ tāta sukhā śayyā tvadartham upakalpitāpratyāśvasihi śeṣvāsyāṃ sukhaṃ rāghavanandana  Ramucito yaṃ janaḥ sarvo duḥkhānāṃ tvaṃ sukhocitaḥdharmātmaṃs tasya guptyarthaṃ jāgariṣyāmahe vayam  Ramna hi rāmāt priyataro mamāsti bhuvi kaścanamotsuko bhūr bravīmy etad apy asatyaṃ tavāgrataḥ  Ramasya prasādād āśaṃse loke smin sumahad yaśaḥdharmāvāptiṃ ca vipulām arthāvāptiṃ ca kevalām  Ramso haṃ priyasakhaṃ rāmaṃ śayānaṃ saha sītayārakṣiṣyāmi dhanuṣpāṇiḥ sarvaiḥ svair jñātibhiḥ saha  Ramna hi me viditaṃ kiṃcid vane smiṃś carataḥ sadācaturaṅgaṃ hy api balaṃ prasahema vayaṃ yudhi  Ramevam asmābhir uktena lakṣmaṇena mahātmanāanunītā vayaṃ sarve dharmam evānupaśyatā  Ramkathaṃ dāśarathau bhūmau śayāne saha sītayāśakyā nidrā mayā labdhuṃ jīvitaṃ vā sukhāni vā  Ramyo na devāsuraiḥ sarvaiḥ śakyaḥ prasahituṃ yudhitaṃ paśya guha saṃviṣṭaṃ tṛṇeṣu saha sītayā  Rammahatā tapasā labdho vividhaiś ca pariśramaiḥeko daśarathasyaiṣa putraḥ sadṛśalakṣaṇaḥ  Ramasmin pravrājite rājā na ciraṃ vartayiṣyatividhavā medinī nūnaṃ kṣipram eva bhaviṣyati  Ramvinadya sumahānādaṃ śrameṇoparatāḥ striyaḥnirghoṣoparataṃ nūnam adya rājaniveśanam  Ramkausalyā caiva rājā ca tathaiva jananī mamanāśaṃse yadi te sarve jīveyuḥ śarvarīm imām  Ramjīved api hi me mātā śatrughnasyānvavekṣayāduḥkhitā yā tu kausalyā vīrasūr vinaśiṣyati  Ramatikrāntam atikrāntam anavāpya manorathamrājye rāmam anikṣipya pitā me vinaśiṣyati  Ramsiddhārthāḥ pitaraṃ vṛttaṃ tasmin kāle hy upasthitepretakāryeṣu sarveṣu saṃskariṣyanti bhūmipam  Ramramyacatvarasaṃsthānāṃ suvibhaktamahāpathāmharmyaprāsādasampannāṃ sarvaratnavibhūṣitām  Ramgajāśvarathasambādhāṃ tūryanādavināditāmsarvakalyāṇasampūrṇāṃ hṛṣṭapuṣṭajanākulām  Ramārāmodyānasampūrṇāṃ samājotsavaśālinīmsukhitā vicariṣyanti rājadhānīṃ pitur mama  Ramapi satyapratijñena sārdhaṃ kuśalinā vayamnivṛtte samaye hy asmin sukhitāḥ praviśemahi  Ramparidevayamānasya tasyaivaṃ sumahātmanaḥtiṣṭhato rājaputrasya śarvarī sātyavartata  Ramprabhāte vimale sūrye kārayitvā jaṭā ubhauasmin bhāgīrathītīre sukhaṃ saṃtāritau mayā  Ramjaṭādharau tau drumacīravāsasau mahābalau kuñjarayūthapopamauvareṣucāpāsidharau paraṃtapau vyavekṣamāṇau saha sītayā gatau  Ramguhasya vacanaṃ śrutvā bharato bhṛśam apriyamdhyānaṃ jagāma tatraiva yatra tac chrutam apriyam  Ramsukumāro mahāsattvaḥ siṃhaskandho mahābhujaḥpuṇḍarīkaviśālākṣas taruṇaḥ priyadarśanaḥ  Rampratyāśvasya muhūrtaṃ tu kālaṃ paramadurmanāḥpapāta sahasā totrair hṛdi viddha iva dvipaḥ  Ramtadavasthaṃ tu bharataṃ śatrughno nantarasthitaḥpariṣvajya rurodoccair visaṃjñaḥ śokakarśitaḥ  Ramtataḥ sarvāḥ samāpetur mātaro bharatasya tāḥupavāsakṛśā dīnā bhartṛvyasanakarśitāḥ  Ramtāś ca taṃ patitaṃ bhūmau rudantyaḥ paryavārayankausalyā tv anusṛtyainaṃ durmanāḥ pariṣasvaje  Ramvatsalā svaṃ yathā vatsam upagūhya tapasvinīparipapraccha bharataṃ rudantī śokalālasā  Ramputra vyādhir na te kaccic charīraṃ paribādhateadya rājakulasyāsya tvadadhīnaṃ hi jīvitam  Ramtvāṃ dṛṣṭvā putra jīvāmi rāme sabhrātṛke gatevṛtte daśarathe rājñi nātha ekas tvam adya naḥ  Ramkaccin na lakṣmaṇe putra śrutaṃ te kiṃcid apriyamputra vā hy ekaputrāyāḥ sahabhārye vanaṃ gate  Ramsa muhūrtaṃ samāśvasya rudann eva mahāyaśāḥkausalyāṃ parisāntvyedaṃ guhaṃ vacanam abravīt  Rambhrātā me kvāvasad rātriṃ kva sītā kva ca lakṣmaṇaḥasvapac chayane kasmin kiṃ bhuktvā guha śaṃsa me  Ramso bravīd bharataṃ pṛṣṭo niṣādādhipatir guhaḥyadvidhaṃ pratipede ca rāme priyahite tithau  Ramannam uccāvacaṃ bhakṣāḥ phalāni vividhāni carāmāyābhyavahārārthaṃ bahu copahṛtaṃ mayā  Ramtat sarvaṃ pratyanujñāsīd rāmaḥ satyaparākramaḥna hi tat pratyagṛhṇāt sa kṣatradharmam anusmaran  Ramna hy asmābhiḥ pratigrāhyaṃ sakhe deyaṃ tu sarvadāiti tena vayaṃ rājann anunītā mahātmanā  Ramlakṣmaṇena samānītaṃ pītvā vāri mahāyaśāḥaupavāsyaṃ tadākārṣīd rāghavaḥ saha sītayā  Ramtatas tu jalaśeṣeṇa lakṣmaṇo py akarot tadāvāgyatās te trayaḥ saṃdhyām upāsata samāhitāḥ  Ramsaumitris tu tataḥ paścād akarot svāstaraṃ śubhamsvayam ānīya barhīṃṣi kṣipraṃ rāghavakāraṇāt  Ramtasmin samāviśad rāmaḥ svāstare saha sītayāprakṣālya ca tayoḥ pādāv apacakrāma lakṣmaṇaḥ  Rametat tad iṅgudīmūlam idam eva ca tat tṛṇamyasmin rāmaś ca sītā ca rātriṃ tāṃ śayitāv ubhau  Ramniyamya pṛṣṭhe tu talāṅgulitravāñ śaraiḥ supūrṇāv iṣudhī paraṃtapaḥmahad dhanuḥ sajyam upohya lakṣmaṇo niśām atiṣṭhat parito sya kevalam  Ramtatas tv ahaṃ cottamabāṇacāpadhṛk sthito bhavaṃ tatra sa yatra lakṣmaṇaḥatandribhir jñātibhir āttakārmukair mahendrakalpaṃ paripālayaṃs tadā  Ramtac chrutvā nipuṇaṃ sarvaṃ bharataḥ saha mantribhiḥiṅgudīmūlam āgamya rāmaśayyām avekṣya tām  Ramabravīj jananīḥ sarvā iha tena mahātmanāśarvarī śayitā bhūmāv idam asya vimarditam  Rammahābhāgakulīnena mahābhāgena dhīmatājāto daśarathenorvyāṃ na rāmaḥ svaptum arhati  Ramajinottarasaṃstīrṇe varāstaraṇasaṃcayeśayitvā puruṣavyāghraḥ kathaṃ śete mahītale  Ramprāsādāgravimāneṣu valabhīṣu ca sarvadāhaimarājatabhaumeṣu varāstaraṇaśāliṣu  Rampuṣpasaṃcayacitreṣu candanāgarugandhiṣupāṇḍurābhraprakāśeṣu śukasaṃgharuteṣu ca  Ramgītavāditranirghoṣair varābharaṇaniḥsvanaiḥmṛdaṅgavaraśabdaiś ca satataṃ pratibodhitaḥ  Rambandibhir vanditaḥ kāle bahubhiḥ sūtamāgadhaiḥgāthābhir anurūpābhiḥ stutibhiś ca paraṃtapaḥ  Ramaśraddheyam idaṃ loke na satyaṃ pratibhāti māmuhyate khalu me bhāvaḥ svapno yam iti me matiḥ  Ramna nūnaṃ daivataṃ kiṃcit kālena balavattaramyatra dāśarathī rāmo bhūmāv evaṃ śayīta saḥ  Ramvideharājasya sutā sītā ca priyadarśanādayitā śayitā bhūmau snuṣā daśarathasya ca  Ramiyaṃ śayyā mama bhrātur idaṃ hi parivartitamsthaṇḍile kaṭhine sarvaṃ gātrair vimṛditaṃ tṛṇam  Rammanye sābharaṇā suptā sītāsmiñ śayane tadātatra tatra hi dṛśyante saktāḥ kanakabindavaḥ  Ramuttarīyam ihāsaktaṃ suvyaktaṃ sītayā tadātathā hy ete prakāśante saktāḥ kauśeyatantavaḥ  Rammanye bhartuḥ sukhā śayyā yena bālā tapasvinīsukumārī satī duḥkhaṃ na vijānāti maithilī  Ramsārvabhaumakule jātaḥ sarvalokasukhāvahaḥsarvalokapriyas tyaktvā rājyaṃ priyam anuttamam  Ramkatham indīvaraśyāmo raktākṣaḥ priyadarśanaḥsukhabhāgī ca duḥkhārhaḥ śayito bhuvi rāghavaḥ  Ramsiddhārthā khalu vaidehī patiṃ yānugatā vanamvayaṃ saṃśayitāḥ sarve hīnās tena mahātmanā  Ramakarṇadhārā pṛthivī śūnyeva pratibhāti māgate daśarathe svarge rāme cāraṇyam āśrite  Ramna ca prārthayate kaścin manasāpi vasuṃdharāmvane pi vasatas tasya bāhuvīryābhirakṣitām  Ramśūnyasaṃvaraṇārakṣām ayantritahayadvipāmapāvṛtapuradvārāṃ rājadhānīm arakṣitām  Ramaprahṛṣṭabalāṃ nyūnāṃ viṣamasthām anāvṛtāmśatravo nābhimanyante bhakṣān viṣakṛtān iva  Ramadya prabhṛti bhūmau tu śayiṣye haṃ tṛṇeṣu vāphalamūlāśano nityaṃ jaṭācīrāṇi dhārayan  Ramtasyārtham uttaraṃ kālaṃ nivatsyāmi sukhaṃ vanetaṃ pratiśravam āmucya nāsya mithyā bhaviṣyati  Ramvasantaṃ bhrātur arthāya śatrughno mānuvatsyatilakṣmaṇena saha tv āryo ayodhyāṃ pālayiṣyati  Ramabhiṣekṣyanti kākutstham ayodhyāyāṃ dvijātayaḥapi me devatāḥ kuryur imaṃ satyaṃ manoratham  Ramprasādyamānaḥ śirasā mayā svayaṃ bahuprakāraṃ yadi na prapatsyatetato nuvatsyāmi cirāya rāghavaṃ vane vasan nārhati mām upekṣitum  Ramvyuṣya rātriṃ tu tatraiva gaṅgākūle sa rāghavaḥbharataḥ kālyam utthāya śatrughnam idam abravīt  Ramśatrughottiṣṭha kiṃ śeṣe niṣādādhipatiṃ guhamśīghram ānaya bhadraṃ te tārayiṣyati vāhinīm  Ramjāgarmi nāhaṃ svapimi tathaivāryaṃ vicintayanity evam abravīd bhrātrā śatrughno pi pracoditaḥ  Ramiti saṃvadator evam anyonyaṃ narasiṃhayoḥāgamya prāñjaliḥ kāle guho bharatam abravīt  Ramkaccit sukhaṃ nadītīre vātsīḥ kākutstha śarvarīmkaccic ca saha sainyasya tava sarvam anāmayam  Ramguhasya tat tu vacanaṃ śrutvā snehād udīritamrāmasyānuvaśo vākyaṃ bharato pīdam abravīt  Ramsukhā naḥ śarvarī rājan pūjitāś cāpi te vayamgaṅgāṃ tu naubhir bahvībhir dāśāḥ saṃtārayantu naḥ  Ramtato guhaḥ saṃtvaritaḥ śrutvā bharataśāsanampratipraviśya nagaraṃ taṃ jñātijanam abravīt  Ramuttiṣṭhata prabudhyadhvaṃ bhadram astu hi vaḥ sadānāvaḥ samanukarṣadhvaṃ tārayiṣyāma vāhinīm  Ramte tathoktāḥ samutthāya tvaritā rājaśāsanātpañca nāvāṃ śatāny eva samāninyuḥ samantataḥ  Ramanyāḥ svastikavijñeyā mahāghaṇṭādharā varāḥśobhamānāḥ patākinyo yuktavātāḥ susaṃhatāḥ  Ramtataḥ svastikavijñeyāṃ pāṇḍukambalasaṃvṛtāmsanandighoṣāṃ kalyāṇīṃ guho nāvam upāharat  Ramtām āruroha bharataḥ śatrughnaś ca mahābalaḥkausalyā ca sumitrā ca yāś cānyā rājayoṣitaḥ  Rampurohitaś ca tat pūrvaṃ gurave brāhmaṇāś ca yeanantaraṃ rājadārās tathaiva śakaṭāpaṇāḥ  Ramāvāsam ādīpayatāṃ tīrthaṃ cāpy avagāhatāmbhāṇḍāni cādadānānāṃ ghoṣas tridivam aspṛśat  Rampatākinyas tu tā nāvaḥ svayaṃ dāśair adhiṣṭhitāḥvahantyo janam ārūḍhaṃ tadā saṃpetur āśugāḥ  Ramnārīṇām abhipūrṇās tu kāścit kāścit tu vājināmkaścit tatra vahanti sma yānayugyaṃ mahādhanam  Ramtāḥ sma gatvā paraṃ tīram avaropya ca taṃ janamnivṛttāḥ kāṇḍacitrāṇi kriyante dāśabandhubhiḥ  Ramsavaijayantās tu gajā gajārohaiḥ pracoditāḥtarantaḥ sma prakāśante sadhvajā iva parvatāḥ  Ramnāvaś cāruruhus tv anye plavais terus tathāpareanye kumbhaghaṭais terur anye teruś ca bāhubhiḥ  Ramsā puṇyā dhvajinī gaṅgāṃ dāśaiḥ saṃtāritā svayammaitre muhūrte prayayau prayāgavanam uttamam  Ramāśvāsayitvā ca camūṃ mahātmā niveśayitvā ca yathopajoṣamdraṣṭuṃ bharadvājam ṛṣipravaryam ṛtvigvṛtaḥ san bharataḥ pratasthe  Rambharadvājāśramaṃ dṛṣṭvā krośād eva nararṣabhaḥbalaṃ sarvam avasthāpya jagāma saha mantribhiḥ  Rampadbhyām eva hi dharmajño nyastaśastraparicchadaḥvasāno vāsasī kṣaume purodhāya purohitam  Ramtataḥ saṃdarśane tasya bharadvājasya rāghavaḥmantriṇas tān avasthāpya jagāmānu purohitam  Ramvasiṣṭham atha dṛṣṭvaiva bharadvājo mahātapāḥsaṃcacālāsanāt tūrṇaṃ śiṣyān arghyam iti bruvan  Ramsamāgamya vasiṣṭhena bharatenābhivāditaḥabudhyata mahātejāḥ sutaṃ daśarathasya tam  Ramtābhyām arghyaṃ ca pādyaṃ ca dattvā paścāt phalāni caānupūrvyāc ca dharmajñaḥ papraccha kuśalaṃ kule  Ramayodhyāyāṃ bale kośe mitreṣv api ca mantriṣujānan daśarathaṃ vṛttaṃ na rājānam udāharat  Ramvasiṣṭho bharataś cainaṃ papracchatur anāmayamśarīre gniṣu vṛkṣeṣu śiṣyeṣu mṛgapakṣiṣu  Ramtatheti ca pratijñāya bharadvājo mahātapāḥbharataṃ pratyuvācedaṃ rāghavasnehabandhanāt  Ramkim ihāgamane kāryaṃ tava rājyaṃ praśāsataḥetad ācakṣva me sarvaṃ na hi me śudhyate manaḥ  Ramsuṣuve yamamitraghnaṃ kausalyānandavardhanambhrātrā saha sabhāryo yaś ciraṃ pravrājito vanam  Ramniyuktaḥ strīniyuktena pitrā yo sau mahāyaśāḥvanavāsī bhavetīha samāḥ kila caturdaśa  Ramkaccin na tasyāpāpasya pāpaṃ kartum ihecchasiakaṇṭakaṃ bhoktumanā rājyaṃ tasyānujasya ca  Ramevam ukto bharadvājaṃ bharataḥ pratyuvāca haparyaśrunayano duḥkhād vācā saṃsajjamānayā  Ramhato smi yadi mām evaṃ bhagavān api manyatematto na doṣam āśaṅker naivaṃ mām anuśādhi hi  Ramna caitad iṣṭaṃ mātā me yad avocan madantarenāham etena tuṣṭaś ca na tad vacanam ādade  Ramahaṃ tu taṃ naravyāghram upayātaḥ prasādakaḥpratinetum ayodhyāṃ ca pādau tasyābhivanditum  Ramtvaṃ mām evaṃ gataṃ matvā prasādaṃ kartum arhasiśaṃsa me bhagavan rāmaḥ kva samprati mahīpatiḥ  Ramuvāca taṃ bharadvājaḥ prasādād bharataṃ vacaḥtvayy etat puruṣavyāghra yuktaṃ rāghavavaṃśajeguruvṛttir damaś caiva sādhūnāṃ cānuyāyitā  Ramjāne caitan manaḥsthaṃ te dṛḍhīkaraṇam astv itiapṛcchaṃ tvāṃ tavātyarthaṃ kīrtiṃ samabhivardhayan  Ramasau vasati te bhrātā citrakūṭe mahāgirauśvas tu gantāsi taṃ deśaṃ vasādya saha mantribhiḥetaṃ me kuru suprājña kāmaṃ kāmārthakovida  Ramtatas tathety evam udāradarśanaḥ pratītarūpo bharato bravīd vacaḥcakāra buddhiṃ ca tadā mahāśrame niśānivāsāya narādhipātmajaḥ  Ramkṛtabuddhiṃ nivāsāya tathaiva sa munis tadābharataṃ kaikayīputram ātithyena nyamantrayat  Ramabravīd bharatas tv enaṃ nanv idaṃ bhavatā kṛtampādyam arghyaṃ tathātithyaṃ vane yad upapadyate  Ramathovāca bharadvājo bharataṃ prahasann ivajāne tvāṃ prītisaṃyuktaṃ tuṣyes tvaṃ yena kenacit  Ramsenāyās tu tavaitasyāḥ kartum icchāmi bhojanammama prītir yathārūpā tvam arho manujarṣabha  Ramkimarthaṃ cāpi nikṣipya dūre balam ihāgataḥkasmān nehopayāto si sabalaḥ puruṣarṣabha  Rambharataḥ pratyuvācedaṃ prāñjalis taṃ tapodhanamsasainyo nopayāto smi bhagavan bhagavadbhayāt  Ramvājimukhyā manuṣyāś ca mattāś ca varavāraṇāḥpracchādya mahatīṃ bhūmiṃ bhagavann anuyānti mām  Ramte vṛkṣān udakaṃ bhūmim āśrameṣūṭajāṃs tathāna hiṃsyur iti tenāham eka evāgatas tataḥ  Ramānīyatām itaḥ senety ājñaptaḥ paramarṣiṇātathā tu cakre bharataḥ senāyāḥ samupāgamam  Ramagniśālāṃ praviśyātha pītvāpaḥ parimṛjya caātithyasya kriyāhetor viśvakarmāṇam āhvayat  Ramāhvaye viśvakarmāṇam ahaṃ tvaṣṭāram eva caātithyaṃ kartum icchāmi tatra me saṃvidhīyatām  Ramprāksrotasaś ca yā nadyaḥ pratyaksrotasa eva capṛthivyām antarikṣe ca samāyāntv adya sarvaśaḥ  Ramanyāḥ sravantu maireyaṃ surām anyāḥ suniṣṭhitāmaparāś codakaṃ śītam ikṣukāṇḍarasopamam  Ramāhvaye devagandharvān viśvāvasuhahāhuhūntathaivāpsaraso devīr gandharvīś cāpi sarvaśaḥ  Ramghṛtācīm atha viśvācīṃ miśrakeśīm alambusāmśakraṃ yāś copatiṣṭhanti brahmāṇaṃ yāś ca bhāminīḥsarvās tumburuṇā sārdham āhvaye saparicchadāḥ  Ramvanaṃ kuruṣu yad divyaṃ vāso bhūṣaṇapattravatdivyanārīphalaṃ śaśvat tat kauberam ihaiva tu  Ramiha me bhagavān somo vidhattām annam uttamambhakṣyaṃ bhojyaṃ ca coṣyaṃ ca lehyaṃ ca vividhaṃ bahu  Ramvicitrāṇi ca mālyāni pādapapracyutāni casurādīni ca peyāni māṃsāni vividhāni ca  Ramevaṃ samādhinā yuktas tejasāpratimena caśikṣāsvarasamāyuktaṃ tapasā cābravīn muniḥ  Rammanasā dhyāyatas tasya prāṅmukhasya kṛtāñjaleḥājagmus tāni sarvāṇi daivatāni pṛthakpṛthak  Rammalayaṃ darduraṃ caiva tataḥ svedanudo nilaḥupaspṛśya vavau yuktyā supriyātmā sukhaḥ śivaḥ  Ramtato bhyavartanta ghanā divyāḥ kusumavṛṣṭayaḥdevadundubhighoṣaś ca dikṣu sarvāsu śuśruve  Rampravavuś cottamā vātā nanṛtuś cāpsarogaṇāḥprajagur devagandharvā vīṇāḥ pramumucuḥ svarān  Ramsa śabdo dyāṃ ca bhūmiṃ ca prāṇināṃ śravaṇāni caviveśoccāritaḥ ślakṣṇaḥ samo layaguṇānvitaḥ  Ramtasminn uparate śabde divye śrotrasukhe nṛṇāmdadarśa bhārataṃ sainyaṃ vidhānaṃ viśvakarmaṇaḥ  Rambabhūva hi samā bhūmiḥ samantāt pañcayojanamśādvalair bahubhiś channā nīlavaiḍūryasaṃnibhaiḥ  Ramtasmin bilvāḥ kapitthāś ca panasā bījapūrakāḥāmalakyo babhūvuś ca cūtāś ca phalabhūṣaṇāḥ  Ramuttarebhyaḥ kurubhyaś ca vanaṃ divyopabhogavatājagāma nadī divyā tīrajair bahubhir vṛtā  Ramcatuḥśālāni śubhrāṇi śālāś ca gajavājināmharmyaprāsādasaṃghātās toraṇāni śubhāni ca  Ramsitameghanibhaṃ cāpi rājaveśma sutoraṇamśuklamālyakṛtākāraṃ divyagandhasamukṣitam  Ramcaturasram asaṃbādhaṃ śayanāsanayānavatdivyaiḥ sarvarasair yuktaṃ divyabhojanavastravat  Ramupakalpitasarvānnaṃ dhautanirmalabhājanamkḷptasarvāsanaṃ śrīmat svāstīrṇaśayanottamam  Rampraviveśa mahābāhur anujñāto maharṣiṇāveśma tad ratnasampūrṇaṃ bharataḥ kaikayīsutaḥ  Ramanujagmuś ca taṃ sarve mantriṇaḥ sapurohitāḥbabhūvuś ca mudā yuktās taṃ dṛṣṭvā veśmasaṃvidhim  Ramtatra rājāsanaṃ divyaṃ vyajanaṃ chattram eva cabharato mantribhiḥ sārdham abhyavartata rājavat  Ramāsanaṃ pūjayāmāsa rāmāyābhipraṇamya cavālavyajanam ādāya nyaṣīdat sacivāsane  Ramānupūrvyān niṣeduś ca sarve mantripurohitāḥtataḥ senāpatiḥ paścāt praśāstā ca niṣedatuḥ  Ramtatas tatra muhūrtena nadyaḥ pāyasakardamāḥupātiṣṭhanta bharataṃ bharadvājasya śāsanāt  Ramtāsām ubhayataḥ kūlaṃ pāṇḍumṛttikalepanāḥramyāś cāvasathā divyā brahmaṇas tu prasādajāḥ  Ramtenaiva ca muhūrtena divyābharaṇabhūṣitāḥāgur viṃśatisāhasrā brahmaṇā prahitāḥ striyaḥ  Ramsuvarṇamaṇimuktena pravālena ca śobhitāḥāgur viṃśatisāhasrāḥ kuberaprahitāḥ striyaḥ  Ramyābhir gṛhītaḥ puruṣaḥ sonmāda iva lakṣyateāgur viṃśatisāhasrā nandanād apsarogaṇāḥ  Ramnāradas tumburur gopaḥ parvataḥ sūryavarcasaḥete gandharvarājāno bharatasyāgrato jaguḥ  Ramalambusā miśrakeśī puṇḍarīkātha vāmanāupānṛtyaṃs tu bharataṃ bharadvājasya śāsanāt  Ramyāni mālyāni deveṣu yāni caitrarathe vaneprayāge tāny adṛśyanta bharadvājasya śāsanāt  Rambilvā mārdaṅgikā āsañ śamyāgrāhā vibhītakāḥaśvatthā nartakāś cāsan bharadvājasya tejasā  Ramtataḥ saralatālāś ca tilakā naktamālakāḥprahṛṣṭās tatra saṃpetuḥ kubjā bhūtvātha vāmanāḥ  Ramśiṃśapāmalakī jambūr yāś cānyāḥ kānane latāḥpramadāvigrahaṃ kṛtvā bharadvājāśrame vasan  Ramsurāṃ surāpāḥ pibata pāyasaṃ ca bubhukṣitāḥmāṃsāni ca sumedhyāni bhakṣyantāṃ yāvad icchatha  Ramutsādya snāpayanti sma nadītīreṣu valguṣuapy ekam ekaṃ puruṣaṃ pramadāḥ sapta cāṣṭa ca  Ramsaṃvahantyaḥ samāpetur nāryo ruciralocanāḥparimṛjya tathā nyāyaṃ pāyayanti varāṅganāḥ  Ramhayān gajān kharān uṣṭrāṃs tathaiva surabheḥ sutānikṣūṃś ca madhujālāṃś ca bhojayanti sma vāhanānikṣvākuvarayodhānāṃ codayanto mahābalāḥ  Ramnāśvabandho śvam ājānān na gajaṃ kuñjaragrahaḥmattapramattamuditā camūḥ sā tatra saṃbabhau  Ramtarpitāḥ sarvakāmais te raktacandanarūṣitāḥapsarogaṇasaṃyuktāḥ sainyā vācam udairayan  Ramnaivāyodhyāṃ gamiṣyāmo na gamiṣyāma daṇḍakānkuśalaṃ bharatasyāstu rāmasyāstu tathā sukham  Ramiti pādātayodhāś ca hastyaśvārohabandhakāḥanāthās taṃ vidhiṃ labdhvā vācam etām udairayan  Ramsamprahṛṣṭā vinedus te narās tatra sahasraśaḥbharatasyānuyātāraḥ svargo yam iti cābruvan  Ramtato bhuktavatāṃ teṣāṃ tad annam amṛtopamamdivyān udvīkṣya bhakṣyāṃs tān abhavad bhakṣaṇe matiḥ  Rampreṣyāś ceṭyaś ca vadhvaś ca pratyuvāca haaṅgāvekṣasva saumitre kasyaitāṃ manyase camūm  Ramevam uktas tu rāmeṇa lakṣmaṇo vākyam abravītdidhakṣann iva tāṃ senāṃ ruṣitaḥ pāvako yathā  Ramsampannaṃ rājyam icchaṃs tu vyaktaṃ prāpyābhiṣecanamāvāṃ hantuṃ samabhyeti kaikeyyā bharataḥ sutaḥ  Rameṣa vai sumahāñ śrīmān viṭapī saṃprakāśatevirājaty udgataskandhaḥ kovidāradhvajo rathe  Rambhajanty ete yathākāmam aśvān āruhya śīghragānete bhrājanti saṃhṛṣṭā gajān āruhya sādinaḥ  Ramgṛhītadhanuṣau cāvāṃ giriṃ vīra śrayāvaheapi nau vaśam āgacchet kovidāradhvajo raṇe  Ramapi drakṣyāmi bharataṃ yatkṛte vyasanaṃ mahattvayā rāghava samprāptaṃ sītayā ca mayā tathā  Ramyannimittaṃ bhavān rājyāc cyuto rāghava śāśvatātsamprāpto yam arir vīra bharato vadhya eva me  Rambharatasya vadhe doṣaṃ nāhaṃ paśyāmi rāghavapūrvāpakāriṇāṃ tyāge na hy adharmo vidhīyateetasmin nihate kṛtsnām anuśādhi vasuṃdharām  Ramadya putraṃ hataṃ saṃkhye kaikeyī rājyakāmukāmayā paśyet suduḥkhārtā hastibhagnam iva drumam  Ramkaikeyīṃ ca vadhiṣyāmi sānubandhāṃ sabāndhavāmkaluṣeṇādya mahatā medinī parimucyatām  Ramadyemaṃ saṃyataṃ krodham asatkāraṃ ca mānadamokṣyāmi śatrusainyeṣu kakṣeṣv iva hutāśanam  Ramadyaitac citrakūṭasya kānanaṃ niśitaiḥ śaraiḥbhindañ śatruśarīrāṇi kariṣye śoṇitokṣitam  Ramśarair nirbhinnahṛdayān kuñjarāṃs turagāṃs tathāśvāpadāḥ parikarṣantu narāṃś ca nihatān mayā  Ramśarāṇāṃ dhanuṣaś cāham anṛṇo smi mahāvanesasainyaṃ bharataṃ hatvā bhaviṣyāmi na saṃśayaḥ  Ramsusaṃrabdhaṃ tu saumitriṃ lakṣmaṇaṃ krodhamūrchitamrāmas tu parisāntvyātha vacanaṃ cedam abravīt  Ramkim atra dhanuṣā kāryam asinā vā sacarmaṇāmaheṣvāse mahāprājñe bharate svayam āgate  Ramprāptakālaṃ yad eṣo smān bharato draṣṭum icchatiasmāsu manasāpy eṣa nāhitaṃ kiṃcid ācaret  Ramvipriyaṃ kṛtapūrvaṃ te bharatena kadā na kimīdṛśaṃ vā bhayaṃ te dya bharataṃ yo tra śaṅkase  Ramna hi te niṣṭhuraṃ vācyo bharato nāpriyaṃ vacaḥahaṃ hy apriyam uktaḥ syāṃ bharatasyāpriye kṛte  Ramkathaṃ nu putrāḥ pitaraṃ hanyuḥ kasyāṃcid āpadibhrātā vā bhrātaraṃ hanyāt saumitre prāṇam ātmanaḥ  Ramyadi rājyasya hetos tvam imāṃ vācaṃ prabhāṣasevakṣyāmi bharataṃ dṛṣṭvā rājyam asmai pradīyatām  Ramucyamāno hi bharato mayā lakṣmaṇa tattvataḥrājyam asmai prayaccheti bāḍham ity eva vakṣyati  Ramtathokto dharmaśīlena bhrātrā tasya hite rataḥlakṣmaṇaḥ praviveśeva svāni gātrāṇi lajjayā  Ramvrīḍitaṃ lakṣmaṇaṃ dṛṣṭvā rāghavaḥ pratyuvāca haeṣa manye mahābāhur ihāsmān draṣṭum āgataḥ  Ramvanavāsam anudhyāya gṛhāya pratineṣyatiimāṃ vāpy eṣa vaidehīm atyantasukhasevinīm  Rametau tau saṃprakāśete gotravantau manoramauvāyuvegasamau vīra javanau turagottamau  Ramsa eṣa sumahākāyaḥ kampate vāhinīmukhenāgaḥ śatruṃjayo nāma vṛddhas tātasya dhīmataḥ  Ramavatīrya tu sālāgrāt tasmāt sa samitiṃjayaḥlakṣmaṇaḥ prāñjalir bhūtvā tasthau rāmasya pārśvataḥ  Rambharatenātha saṃdiṣṭā sammardo na bhaved itisamantāt tasya śailasya senāvāsam akalpayat  Ramadhyardham ikṣvākucamūr yojanaṃ parvatasya sāpārśve nyaviśad āvṛtya gajavājirathākulā  Ramsā citrakūṭe bharatena senā dharmaṃ puraskṛtya vidhūya darpamprasādanārthaṃ raghunandanasya virocate nītimatā praṇītā  Ramniveśya senāṃ tu vibhuḥ padbhyāṃ pādavatāṃ varaḥabhigantuṃ sa kākutstham iyeṣa guruvartakam  Ramniviṣṭamātre sainye tu yathoddeśaṃ vinītavatbharato bhrātaraṃ vākyaṃ śatrughnam idam abravīt  Ramkṣipraṃ vanam idaṃ saumya narasaṃghaiḥ samantataḥlubdhaiś ca sahitair ebhis tvam anveṣitum arhasi  Ramyāvan na rāmaṃ drakṣyāmi lakṣmaṇaṃ vā mahābalamvaidehīṃ vā mahābhāgāṃ na me śāntir bhaviṣyati  Ramyāvan na candrasaṃkāśaṃ drakṣyāmi śubham ānanambhrātuḥ padmapalāśākṣaṃ na me śāntir bhaviṣyati  Ramyāvan na caraṇau bhrātuḥ pārthivavyañjanānvitauśirasā dhārayiṣyāmi na me śāntir bhaviṣyati  Ramyāvan na rājye rājyārhaḥ pitṛpaitāmahe sthitaḥabhiṣekajalaklinno na me śāntir bhaviṣyati  Ramkṛtakṛtyā mahābhāgā vaidehī janakātmajābhartāraṃ sāgarāntāyāḥ pṛthivyā yānugacchati  Ramsubhagaś citrakūṭo sau girirājopamo giriḥyasmin vasati kākutsthaḥ kubera iva nandane  Ramkṛtakāryam idaṃ durgaṃ vanaṃ vyālaniṣevitamyad adhyāste mahātejā rāmaḥ śastrabhṛtāṃ varaḥ  Ramevam uktvā mahātejā bharataḥ puruṣarṣabhaḥpadbhyām eva mahātejāḥ praviveśa mahad vanam  Ramsa tāni drumajālāni jātāni girisānuṣupuṣpitāgrāṇi madhyena jagāma vadatāṃ varaḥ  Ramsa gireś citrakūṭasya sālam āsādya puṣpitamrāmāśramagatasyāgner dadarśa dhvajam ucchritam  Ramtaṃ dṛṣṭvā bharataḥ śrīmān mumoda sahabāndhavaḥatra rāma iti jñātvā gataḥ pāram ivāmbhasaḥ  Ramsa citrakūṭe tu girau niśāmya rāmāśramaṃ puṇyajanopapannamguhena sārdhaṃ tvarito jagāma punar niveśyaiva camūṃ mahātmā  Ramniviṣṭāyāṃ tu senāyām utsuko bharatas tadājagāma bhrātaraṃ draṣṭuṃ śatrughnam anudarśayan  Ramṛṣiṃ vasiṣṭhaṃ saṃdiśya mātṝn me śīghram ānayaiti tvaritam agre sa jagāma guruvatsalaḥ  Ramsumantras tv api śatrughnam adūrād anvapadyatarāmadarśanajas tarṣo bharatasyeva tasya ca  Ramgacchann evātha bharatas tāpasālayasaṃsthitāmbhrātuḥ parṇakuṭīṃ śrīmān uṭajaṃ ca dadarśa ha  Ramśālāyās tv agratas tasyā dadarśa bharatas tadākāṣṭhāni cāvabhagnāni puṣpāṇy avacitāni ca  Ramdadarśa ca vane tasmin mahataḥ saṃcayān kṛtānmṛgāṇāṃ mahiṣāṇāṃ ca karīṣaiḥ śītakāraṇāt  Ramgacchan eva mahābāhur dyutimān bharatas tadāśatrughnaṃ cābravīd dhṛṣṭas tān amātyāṃś ca sarvaśaḥ  Rammanye prāptāḥ sma taṃ deśaṃ bharadvājo yam abravītnātidūre hi manye haṃ nadīṃ mandākinīm itaḥ  Ramuccair baddhāni cīrāṇi lakṣmaṇena bhaved anuprāptas taṃ janaṃ cedam abravīt  Ramjagatyāṃ puruṣavyāghra āste vīrāsane rataḥjanendro nirjanaṃ prāpya dhin me janma sajīvitam  Rammatkṛte vyasanaṃ prāpto lokanātho mahādyutiḥsarvān kāmān parityajya vane vasati rāghavaḥ  Ramiti lokasamākruṣṭaḥ pādeṣv adya prasādayanrāmasya nipatiṣyāmi sītāyāś ca punaḥ punaḥ  Ramevaṃ sa vilapaṃs tasmin vane daśarathātmajaḥdadarśa mahatīṃ puṇyāṃ Ramnirīkṣya sa muhūrtaṃ tu dadarśa bharato gurumuṭaje rāmam āsīnaṃ jaṭāmaṇḍaladhāriṇam  Ramtaṃ tu kṛṣṇājinadharaṃ cīravalkalavāsasamdadarśa rāmam āsīnam abhitaḥ pāvakopamam  Ramsiṃhaskandhaṃ mahābāhuṃ yathāmbare śukrabṛhaspatibhyām  Ramtān pārthivān vāraṇayūthapābhān samāgatāṃs tatra mahaty araṇyevanaukasas te pi samīkṣya sarve py aśrūṇy amuñcan pravihāya harṣam  Ramāghrāya rāmas taṃ mūrdhni anudraṣṭā satkṛtas te purohitaḥ  Ramkaccid agniṣu te yukto vidhijño matimān ṛjuḥhutaṃ ca hoṣyamāṇaṃ ca kāle vedayate sadā  Ramiṣvastravarasampannam arthaśāstraviśāradamsudhanvānam upādhyāyaṃ kaccit śāstrakovidaiḥ  Ramkaccin nidrāvaśaṃ naiṣi kaccit kāle vibudhyasekaccic cāpararātriṣu cintayasy arthanaipuṇam  Ramkaccin mantrayase naikaḥ kaccin na bahubhiḥ sahakaccit te mantrito mantro rāṣṭraṃ na paridhāvati  Ramkaccid arthaṃ viniścitya laghumūlaṃ mahodayamkṣipram ārabhase kartuṃ na dīrghayasi rāghava  Ramkaccit tu sukṛtāny eva kṛtarūpāṇi vā punaḥvidus te sarvakāryāṇi na kartavyāni pārthivāḥ  Ramkaccin na tarkair yuktvā vā ye cāpy aparikīrtitāḥtvayā vā tava vāmātyair budhyate tāta mantritam  Ramkaccit sahasrān mūrkhāṇām ekam icchasi paṇḍitampaṇḍito hy arthakṛcchreṣu kuryān niḥśreyasaṃ mahat  Ramsahasrāṇy api mūrkhāṇāṃ yady upāste mahīpatiḥatha vāpy ayutāny eva nāsti teṣu sahāyatā  Rameko py amātyo medhāvī śūro dakṣo vicakṣaṇaḥrājānaṃ rājamātraṃ vā prāpayen mahatīṃ śriyam  Ramkaccin mukhyā mahatsv eva madhyameṣu ca madhyamāḥjaghanyāś ca jaghanyeṣu bhṛtyāḥ karmasu yojitāḥ  Ramamātyān upadhātītān pitṛpaitāmahāñ śucīnśreṣṭhāñ śreṣṭheṣu kaccit tvaṃ niyojayasi karmasu  Ramkaccit tvāṃ nāvajānanti yājakāḥ patitaṃ yathāugrapratigrahītāraṃ kāmayānam iva striyaḥ  Ramupāyakuśalaṃ vaidyaṃ bhṛtyasaṃdūṣaṇe ratamśūram aiśvaryakāmaṃ ca yo na hanti sa vadhyate  Ramkaccid dhṛṣṭaś ca śūraś ca pradhānataḥkaccit prāṇāṃs tavārtheṣu saṃtyajanti samāhitāḥ  Ramkaccij jānapado vidvān dakṣiṇaḥ pratibhānavānyathoktavādī dūtas te kṛto bharata paṇḍitaḥ  Ramkaccid aṣṭādaśāny eṣu svapakṣe daśa pañca ca surakṣitāḥkaccin na śraddadhāsyāsāṃ kaccid guhyaṃ na bhāṣase  Ramkaccin nāgavanaṃ guptaṃ kuñjarāṇāṃ ca tṛpyasikaccid darśayase nityaṃ manuṣyāṇāṃ vibhūṣitamutthāyotthāya pūrvāhṇe rājaputro mahāpathe  Ramkaccit sarvāṇi durgāṇi dhanadhānyāyudhodakaiḥyantraiś ca paripūrṇāni tathā śilpidhanurdharaiḥ  Ramāyas te vipulaḥ kaccit kaccid alpataro vyayaḥapātreṣu na te kaccit kośo gacchati rāghava  Ramdevatārthe ca pitrarthe brāhmaṇābhyāgateṣu cayodheṣu mitravargeṣu kaccid gacchati te vyayaḥ  Ramkaccid āryo viśuddhātmā kṣāritaś corakarmaṇāapṛṣṭaḥ śāstrakuśalair na lobhād badhyate śuciḥ  Ramgṛhītaś caiva pṛṣṭaś ca kāle dṛṣṭaḥ sakāraṇaḥkaccin na mucyate coro dhanalobhān nararṣabha  Ramvyasane kaccid āḍhyasya durgatasya ca rāghavaarthaṃ virāgāḥ paśyanti tavāmātyā bahuśrutāḥ  Ramyāni mithyābhiśastānāṃ patanty asrāṇi rāghavatāni putrapaśūn ghnanti prītyartham anuśāsataḥ  Ramkaccid vṛddhāṃś ca bālāṃś ca vaidyamukhyāṃś ca rāghavadānena manasā vācā tribhir etair bubhūṣase  Ramkaccid gurūṃś ca vṛddhāṃś ca tāpasān devatātithīncaityāṃś ca sarvān siddhārthān brāhmaṇāṃś ca namasyasi  Ramkaccid arthena vā dharmaṃ dharmaṃ dharmeṇa vā punaḥubhau vā prītilobhena kāmena na vibādhase  Ramkaccid arthaṃ ca dharmaṃ ca kāmaṃ ca jayatāṃ varavibhajya kāle kālajña sarvān bharata sevase  Ramkaccit te brāhmaṇāḥ śarma sarvaśāstrārthakovidāḥāśaṃsante mahāprājña paurajānapadaiḥ saha  Ramnāstikyam anṛtaṃ krodhaṃ pramādaṃ dīrghasūtratāmadarśanaṃ jñānavatām ālasyaṃ pañcavṛttitām  Ramekacintanam arthānām anarthajñaiś ca mantraṇamniścitānām anārambhaṃ mantrasyāparirakṣaṇam  Rammaṅgalasyāprayogaṃ ca pratyutthānaṃ ca sarvaśaḥkaccit tvaṃ varjayasy etān rājadoṣāṃś caturdaśa  Ramkaccit svādukṛtaṃ bhojyam eko nāśnāsi rāghavakaccid āśaṃsamānebhyo mitrebhyaḥ samprayacchasi  Ramrāmasya vacanaṃ śrutvā bharataḥ pratyuvāca hakiṃ me dharmād vihīnasya rājadharmaḥ kariṣyati  Ramśāśvato yaṃ sadā dharmaḥ sthito smāsu nararṣabhajyeṣṭhaputre sthite rājan na kanīyān bhaven nṛpaḥ  Ramsa samṛddhāṃ mayā sārdham ayodhyāṃ gaccha rāghavaabhiṣecaya cātmānaṃ kulasyāsya bhavāya naḥ  Ramrājānaṃ mānuṣaṃ prāhur devatve saṃmato mamayasya dharmārthasahitaṃ vṛttam āhur amānuṣam  Ramkekayasthe ca mayi tu tvayi cāraṇyam āśritedivam ārya gato rājā yāyajūkaḥ satāṃ mataḥ  Ramuttiṣṭha puruṣavyāghra kriyatām udakaṃ pituḥahaṃ cāyaṃ ca śatrughnaḥ pūrvam eva kṛtodakau  Rampriyeṇa kila dattaṃ hi pitṛlokeṣu rāghavaakṣayyaṃ bhavatīty āhur bhavāṃś caiva pituḥ priyaḥ  Ramtāṃ śrutvā karuṇāṃ vācaṃ pitur maraṇasaṃhitāmrāghavo bharatenoktāṃ babhūva gatacetanaḥ  Ramvāgvajraṃ bharatenoktam amanojñaṃ paraṃtapaḥpragṛhya bāhū rāmo vai puṣpitāgro yathā drumaḥvane paraśunā kṛttas tathā bhuvi papāta ha  Ramtathā hi patitaṃ rāmaṃ jagatyāṃ jagatīpatimkūlaghātapariśrāntaṃ prasuptam iva kuñjaram  Rambhrātaras te maheṣvāsaṃ sarvataḥ śokakarśitamrudantaḥ saha vaidehyā siṣicuḥ salilena vai  Ramsa tu saṃjñāṃ punar labdhvā netrābhyām āsram utsṛjanupākrāmata kākutsthaḥ kṛpaṇaṃ bahubhāṣitum  Ramkiṃ nu tasya mayā kāryaṃ durjātena mahātmanaḥyo mṛto mama śokena na mayā cāpi saṃskṛtaḥ  Ramaho bharata siddhārtho yena rājā tvayānaghaśatrugheṇa ca sarveṣu pretakṛtyeṣu satkṛtaḥ  Ramniṣpradhānām anekāgrāṃ narendreṇa vinākṛtāmnivṛttavanavāso pi nāyodhyāṃ gantum utsahe  Ramsamāptavanavāsaṃ mām ayodhyāyāṃ paraṃtapako nu śāsiṣyati punas tāte lokāntaraṃ gate  Rampurā prekṣya suvṛttaṃ māṃ pitā yāny āha sāntvayanvākyāni tāni śroṣyāmi kutaḥ karṇasukhāny aham  Ramevam uktvā sa bharataṃ bhāryām abhyetya rāghavaḥuvāca śokasaṃtaptaḥ pūrṇacandranibhānanām  Ramsīte mṛtas te śvaśuraḥ pitrā hīno si lakṣmaṇabharato duḥkham ācaṣṭe svargataṃ pṛthivīpatim  Ramsāntvayitvā tu tāṃ rāmo rudantīṃ janakātmajāmuvāca lakṣmaṇaṃ tatra duḥkhito duḥkhitaṃ vacaḥ  Ramānayeṅgudīpiṇyākaṃ cīram āhara cottaramjalakriyārthaṃ tātasya gamiṣyāmi mahātmanaḥ  Ramsītā purastād vrajatu tvam enām abhito vrajaahaṃ paścād gamiṣyāmi gatir hy eṣā sudāruṇā  Ramtato nityānugas teṣāṃ viditātmā mahāmatiḥmṛdur dāntaś ca śāntaś ca rāme ca dṛḍhabhaktimān  Ramsumantras tair nṛpasutaiḥ sārdham āśvāsya rāghavamavātārayad ālambya nadīṃ mandākinīṃ śivām  Ramte sutīrthāṃ tataḥ kṛcchrād upāgamya yaśasvinaḥnadīṃ mandākinīṃ ramyāṃ sadā puṣpitakānanām  Ramśīghrasrotasam āsādya tīrthaṃ śivam akardamamsiṣicus tūdakaṃ rājñe tata etad bhavatv iti  Rampragṛhya ca mahīpālo jalapūritam añjalimdiśaṃ yāmyām abhimukho rudan vacanam abravīt  Rametat te rājaśārdūla vimalaṃ toyam akṣayampitṛlokagatasyādya maddattam upatiṣṭhatu  Ramtato mandākinītīrāt pratyuttīrya sa rāghavaḥpituś cakāra tejasvī nivāpaṃ bhrātṛbhiḥ saha  Ramaiṅgudaṃ badarīmiśraṃ piṇyākaṃ darbhasaṃstarenyasya rāmaḥ suduḥkhārto rudan vacanam abravīt  Ramidaṃ bhuṅkṣva mahārāja prīto yadaśanā vayamyadannaḥ puruṣo bhavati tadannās tasya devatāḥ  Ramtatas tenaiva mārgeṇa pratyuttīrya nadītaṭātāruroha naravyāghro ramyasānuṃ mahīdharam  Ramtataḥ parṇakuṭīdvāram āsādya jagatīpatiḥparijagrāha pāṇibhyām ubhau bharatalakṣmaṇau  Ramteṣāṃ tu rudatāṃ śabdāt pratiśrutkābhavad giraubhrātṝṇāṃ saha vaidehyā siṃhānāṃ nardatām iva  Ramvijñāya tumulaṃ śabdaṃ trastā bharatasainikāḥabruvaṃś cāpi rāmeṇa bharataḥ saṃgato dhruvamteṣām eva mahāñ śabdaḥ śocatāṃ pitaraṃ mṛtam  Ramatha vāsān parityajya taṃ sarve bhimukhāḥ svanamapy ekamanaso jagmur yathāsthānaṃ pradhāvitāḥ  Ramhayair anye gajair anye rathair anye svalaṃkṛtaiḥsukumārās tathaivānye padbhir eva narā yayuḥ  Ramaciraproṣitaṃ rāmaṃ ciraviproṣitaṃ yathādraṣṭukāmo janaḥ sarvo jagāma sahasāśramam  Rambhrātṝṇāṃ tvaritās te tu draṣṭukāmāḥ samāgamamyayur bahuvidhair yānaiḥ khuranemisamākulaiḥ  Ramsā bhūmir bahubhir yānaiḥ khuranemisamāhatāmumoca tumulaṃ śabdaṃ dyaur ivābhrasamāgame  Ramtena vitrāsitā nāgāḥ kareṇuparivāritāḥāvāsayanto gandhena jagmur anyad vanaṃ tataḥ  Ramvarāhamṛgasiṃhāś ca mahiṣāḥ sarkṣavānarāḥvyāghragokarṇagavayā vitreṣuḥ pṛṣataiḥ saha  Ramrathāṅgasāhvā natyūhā haṃsāḥ kāraṇḍavāḥ plavāḥtathā puṃskokilāḥ krauñcā visaṃjñā bhejire diśaḥ  Ramtena śabdena vitrastair ākāśaṃ pakṣibhir vṛtammanuṣyair āvṛtā bhūmir ubhayaṃ prababhau tadā  Ramtān narān bāṣpapūrṇākṣān samīkṣyātha suduḥkhitānparyaṣvajata dharmajñaḥ pitṛvan mātṛvac ca saḥ  Ramsa tatra kāṃścit pariṣasvaje narān narāś ca kecit tu tam abhyavādayancakāra sarvān savayasyabāndhavān yathārham āsādya tadā nṛpātmajaḥ  Ramtataḥ sa teṣāṃ rudatāṃ mahātmanāṃ bhuvaṃ ca khaṃ cānuvinādayan svanaḥguhā girīṇāṃ ca diśaś ca saṃtataṃ mṛdaṅgaghoṣapratimo viśuśruve  Ramvasiṣṭhaḥ purataḥ kṛtvā dārān daśarathasya caabhicakrāma taṃ deśaṃ rāmadarśanatarṣitaḥ  Ramrājapatnyaś ca gacchantyo mandaṃ mandākinīṃ pratidadṛśus tatra tat tīrthaṃ rāmalakṣmaṇasevitam  Ramkausalyā bāṣpapūrṇena mukhena pariśuṣyatāsumitrām abravīd dīnā yāś cānyā rājayoṣitaḥ  Ramidaṃ teṣām anāthānāṃ kliṣṭam akliṣṭakarmaṇāmvane prāk kevalaṃ tīrthaṃ ye te nirviṣayīkṛtāḥ  Ramitaḥ sumitre putras te sadā jalam atandritaḥsvayaṃ harati saumitrir mama putrasya kāraṇāt  Ramdakṣiṇāgreṣu darbheṣu sā dadarśa mahītalepitur iṅgudīpiṇyākaṃ nyastam āyatalocanā  Ramtaṃ bhūmau pitur ārtena nyastaṃ rāmeṇa vīkṣya sāuvāca devī kausalyā sarvā daśarathastriyaḥ  Ramidam ikṣvākunāthasya rāghavasya mahātmanaḥrāghaveṇa pitur dattaṃ paśyataitad yathāvidhi  Ramtasya devasamānasya pārthivasya mahātmanaḥnaitad aupayikaṃ manye bhuktabhogasya bhojanam  Ramcaturantāṃ mahīṃ bhuktvā mahendrasadṛśo vibhuḥkatham iṅgudīpiṇyākaṃ sa bhuṅkte vasudhādhipaḥ  Ramato duḥkhataraṃ loke na kiṃcit pratibhāti māyatra rāmaḥ pitur dadyād iṅgudīkṣodam ṛddhimān  Ramrāmeṇeṅgudīpiṇyākaṃ pitur dattaṃ samīkṣya mekathaṃ duḥkhena hṛdayaṃ na sphoṭati sahasradhā  Ramevam ārtāṃ sapatnyas tā jagmur āśvāsya tāṃ tadādadṛśuś cāśrame rāmaṃ svargāc cyutam ivāmaram  Ramsarvabhogaiḥ parityaktaṃ rāmaṃ samprekṣya mātaraḥārtā mumucur aśrūṇi sasvaraṃ śokakarśitāḥ  Ramtāsāṃ rāmaḥ samutthāya jagrāha caraṇāñ śubhānmātṝṇāṃ manujavyāghraḥ sarvāsāṃ satyasaṃgaraḥ  Ramtāḥ pāṇibhiḥ sukhasparśair mṛdvaṅgulitalaiḥ śubhaiḥpramamārjū rajaḥ pṛṣṭhād rāmasyāyatalocanāḥ  Ramsaumitrir api tāḥ sarvā mātṝn samprekṣya duḥkhitaḥabhyavādayatāsaktaṃ śanai rāmād anantaram  Ramyathā rāme tathā tasmin sarvā vavṛtire striyaḥvṛttiṃ daśarathāj jāte lakṣmaṇe śubhalakṣaṇe  Ramsītāpi caraṇāṃs tāsām upasaṃgṛhya duḥkhitāśvaśrūṇām aśrupūrṇākṣī sā babhūvāgrataḥ sthitā  Ramtāṃ pariṣvajya duḥkhārtāṃ mātā duhitaraṃ yathāvanavāsakṛśāṃ dīnāṃ kausalyā vākyam abravīt  Ramvideharājasya sutā snuṣā daśarathasya carāmapatnī kathaṃ duḥkhaṃ samprāptā nirjane vane  Rampadmam ātapasaṃtaptaṃ parikliṣṭam ivotpalamkāñcanaṃ rajasā dhvastaṃ kliṣṭaṃ candram ivāmbudaiḥ  Rammukhaṃ te prekṣya māṃ śoko dahaty agnir ivāśrayambhṛśaṃ manasi vaidehi vyasanāraṇisambhavaḥ  Rambruvantyām evam ārtāyāṃ jananyāṃ bharatāgrajaḥpādāv āsādya jagrāha vasiṣṭhasya sa rāghavaḥ  Rampurohitasyāgnisamasya tasya vai bṛhaspater indra ivāmarādhipaḥpragṛhya pādau susamṛddhatejasaḥ sahaiva tenopaviveśa rāghavaḥ  Ramtato jaghanyaṃ sahitaiḥ sa mantribhiḥ purapradhānaiś ca sahaiva sainikaiḥjanena dharmajñatamena dharmavān upopaviṣṭo bharatas tadāgrajam  Ramupopaviṣṭas tu tadā sa vīryavāṃs tapasviveṣeṇa samīkṣya rāghavamśriyā jvalantaṃ bharataḥ kṛtāñjalir yathā mahendraḥ prayataḥ prajāpatim  Ramkim eṣa vākyaṃ bharato dya rāghavaṃ praṇamya satkṛtya ca sādhu vakṣyatiitīva tasyāryajanasya tattvato babhūva kautūhalam uttamaṃ tadā  Ramsa rāghavaḥ satyadhṛtiś ca lakṣmaṇo mahānubhāvo bharataś ca dhārmikaḥvṛtāḥ suhṛdbhiś ca virejur adhvare yathā sadasyaiḥ sahitās trayo gnayaḥ  Ramtaṃ tu rāmaḥ samāśvāsya bhrātaraṃ guruvatsalamlakṣmaṇena saha bhrātrā praṣṭuṃ samupacakrame  Ramkim etad iccheyam ahaṃ śrotuṃ pravyāhṛtaṃ tvayāyasmāt tvam āgato deśam imaṃ cīrajaṭājinī  Ramyannimittam imaṃ deśaṃ kṛṣṇājinajaṭādharaḥhitvā rājyaṃ praviṣṭas tvaṃ tat sarvaṃ vaktum arhasi  Ramity uktaḥ kekayīputraḥ kākutsthena mahātmanāpragṛhya balavad bhūyaḥ prāñjalir vākyam abravīt  Ramāryaṃ tātaḥ parityajya kṛtvā karma suduṣkaramgataḥ svargaṃ mahābāhuḥ putraśokābhipīḍitaḥ  Ramstriyā niyuktaḥ kaikeyyā mama mātrā paraṃtapacakāra sumahat pāpam idam ātmayaśoharam  Ramsā rājyaphalam aprāpya vidhavā śokakarśitāpatiṣyati mahāghore niraye jananī mama  Ramtasya me dāsabhūtasya prasādaṃ kartum arhasiabhiṣiñcasva cādyaiva rājyena maghavān iva  Ramimāḥ prakṛtayaḥ sarvā vidhavā mātaraś ca yāḥtvatsakāśam anuprāptāḥ prasādaṃ kartum arhasi  Ramtadānupūrvyā yuktaṃ ca yuktaṃ cātmani mānadarājyaṃ prāpnuhi dharmeṇa sakāmān suhṛdaḥ kuru  Rambhavatv avidhavā bhūmiḥ samagrā patinā tvayāśaśinā vimaleneva śāradī rajanī yathā  Ramebhiś ca sacivaiḥ sārdhaṃ śirasā yācito mayābhrātuḥ śiṣyasya dāsasya prasādaṃ kartum arhasi  Ramtad idaṃ śāśvataṃ pitryaṃ sarvaṃ sacivamaṇḍalampūjitaṃ puruṣavyāghra nātikramitum utsahe  Ramevam uktvā mahābāhuḥ sabāṣpaḥ kekayīsutaḥrāmasya śirasā pādau jagrāha bharataḥ punaḥ  Ramtaṃ mattam iva mātaṃgaṃ niḥśvasantaṃ punaḥ punaḥbhrātaraṃ bharataṃ rāmaḥ pariṣvajyedam abravīt  Ramkulīnaḥ sattvasampannas tejasvī caritavrataḥrājyahetoḥ kathaṃ pāpam ācaret tvadvidho janaḥ  Ramna doṣaṃ tvayi paśyāmi sūkṣmam apy arisūdanana cāpi jananīṃ bālyāt tvaṃ vigarhitum arhasi  Ramyāvat pitari dharmajña gauravaṃ lokasatkṛtetāvad dharmabhṛtāṃ śreṣṭha jananyām api gauravam  Rametābhyāṃ dharmaśīlābhyāṃ vanaṃ gaccheti rāghavamātāpitṛbhyām ukto haṃ katham anyat samācare  Ramtvayā rājyam ayodhyāyāṃ prāptavyaṃ lokasatkṛtamvastavyaṃ daṇḍakāraṇye mayā valkalavāsasā  Ramevaṃ kṛtvā mahārājo vibhāgaṃ lokasaṃnidhauvyādiśya ca mahātejā divaṃ daśaratho gataḥ  Ramsa ca pramāṇaṃ dharmātmā rājā lokagurus tavapitrā dattaṃ yathābhāgam upabhoktuṃ tvam arhasi  Ramcaturdaśa samāḥ saumya daṇḍakāraṇyam āśritaḥupabhokṣye tv ahaṃ dattaṃ bhāgaṃ pitrā mahātmanā  Ramyad abravīn māṃ naralokasatkṛtaḥ pitā mahātmā vibudhādhipopamaḥtad eva manye paramātmano hitaṃ na sarvalokeśvarabhāvam avyayam  Ramtataḥ puruṣasiṃhānāṃ vṛtānāṃ taiḥ suhṛdgaṇaiḥśocatām eva rajanī duḥkhena vyatyavartata  Ramrajanyāṃ suprabhātāyāṃ bhrātaras te suhṛdvṛtāḥmandākinyāṃ hutaṃ japyaṃ kṛtvā rāmam upāgaman  Ramtūṣṇīṃ te samupāsīnā na kaścit kiṃcid abravītbharatas tu suhṛnmadhye rāmaṃ vacanam abravīt  Ramsāntvitā māmikā mātā dattaṃ rājyam idaṃ mamatad dadāmi tavaivāhaṃ bhuṅkṣva rājyam akaṇṭakam  Rammahatevāmbuvegena bhinnaḥ setur jalāgamedurāvāraṃ tvadanyena rājyakhaṇḍam idaṃ mahat  Ramgatiṃ khara ivāśvasya tārkṣyasyeva patatriṇaḥanugantuṃ na śaktir me gatiṃ tava mahīpate  Ramsujīvaṃ nityaśas tasya yaḥ parair upajīvyaterāma tena tu durjīvaṃ yaḥ parān upajīvati  Ramyathā tu ropito vṛkṣaḥ puruṣeṇa vivardhitaḥhrasvakena durāroho rūḍhaskandho mahādrumaḥ  Ramsa yadā puṣpito bhūtvā phalāni na vidarśayetsa tāṃ nānubhavet prītiṃ yasya hetoḥ prabhāvitaḥ  Rameṣopamā mahābāho tvam arthaṃ vettum arhasiyadi tvam asmān ṛṣabho bhartā bhṛtyān na śādhi hi  Ramśreṇayas tvāṃ mahārāja paśyantv agryāś ca sarvaśaḥpratapantam ivādityaṃ rājye sthitam ariṃdamam  Ramtavānuyāne kākutstha mattā nardantu kuñjarāḥantaḥpuragatā nāryo nandantu susamāhitāḥ  Ramtasya sādhv ity amanyanta nāgarā vividhā janāḥbharatasya vacaḥ śrutvā rāmaṃ pratyanuyācataḥ  Ramtam evaṃ duḥkhitaṃ prekṣya vilapantaṃ yaśasvinamrāmaḥ kṛtātmā bharataṃ samāśvāsayad ātmavān  Ramnātmanaḥ kāmakāro sti puruṣo yam anīśvaraḥitaś cetarataś cainaṃ kṛtāntaḥ parikarṣati  Ramsarve kṣayāntā nicayāḥ patanāntāḥ samucchrayāḥsaṃyogā viprayogāntā maraṇāntaṃ ca jīvitam  Ramyathā phalānāṃ pakvānāṃ nānyatra patanād bhayamevaṃ narasya jātasya nānyatra maraṇād bhayam  Ramyathāgāraṃ dṛḍhasthūṇaṃ jīrṇaṃ bhūtvāvasīdatitathāvasīdanti narā jarāmṛtyuvaśaṃ gatāḥ  Ramahorātrāṇi gacchanti sarveṣāṃ prāṇinām ihaāyūṃṣi kṣapayanty āśu grīṣme jalam ivāṃśavaḥ  Ramātmānam anuśoca tvaṃ kim anyam anuśocasiāyus te hīyate yasya sthitasya ca gatasya ca  Ramsahaiva mṛtyur vrajati saha mṛtyur niṣīdatigatvā sudīrgham adhvānaṃ saha mṛtyur nivartate  Ramgātreṣu valayaḥ prāptāḥ śvetāś caiva śiroruhāḥjarayā puruṣo jīrṇaḥ kiṃ hi kṛtvā prabhāvayet  Ramnandanty udita āditye nandanty astam ite ravauātmano nāvabudhyante manuṣyā jīvitakṣayam  Ramhṛṣyanty ṛtumukhaṃ dṛṣṭvā navaṃ navam ihāgatamṛtūnāṃ parivartena prāṇināṃ prāṇasaṃkṣayaḥ  Ramyathā kāṣṭhaṃ ca kāṣṭhaṃ ca sameyātāṃ mahārṇavesametya ca vyapeyātāṃ kālam āsādya kaṃcana  Ramevaṃ bhāryāś ca putrāś ca jñātayaś ca vasūni casametya vyavadhāvanti dhruvo hy eṣāṃ vinābhavaḥ  Ramnātra kaścid yathā bhāvaṃ prāṇī samabhivartatetena tasmin na sāmarthyaṃ pretasyāsty anuśocataḥ  Ramyathā hi sārthaṃ gacchantaṃ brūyāt kaścit pathi sthitaḥaham apy āgamiṣyāmi pṛṣṭhato bhavatām iti  Ramevaṃ pūrvair gato mārgaḥ pitṛpaitāmaho dhruvaḥtam āpannaḥ kathaṃ śoced yasya nāsti vyatikramaḥ  Ramvayasaḥ patamānasya srotaso vānivartinaḥātmā sukhe niyoktavyaḥ sukhabhājaḥ prajāḥ smṛtāḥ  Ramdharmātmā sa śubhaiḥ kṛtsnaiḥ kratubhiś cāptadakṣiṇaiḥdhūtapāpo gataḥ svargaṃ pitā naḥ pṛthivīpatiḥ  Rambhṛtyānāṃ bharaṇāt samyak prajānāṃ paripālanātarthādānāc ca dhārmeṇa pitā nas tridivaṃ gataḥ  Ramiṣṭvā bahuvidhair yajñair bhogāṃś cāvāpya puṣkalānuttamaṃ cāyur āsādya svar gataḥ pṛthivīpatiḥ  Ramsa jīrṇaṃ mānuṣaṃ dehaṃ parityajya pitā hi naḥdaivīm ṛddhim anuprāpto brahmalokavihāriṇīm  Ramtaṃ tu naivaṃvidhaḥ kaścit prājñaḥ śocitum arhatitvadvidho yadvidhaś cāpi śrutavān buddhimattaraḥ  Ramete bahuvidhāḥ śokā vilāparudite tathāvarjanīyā hi dhīreṇa sarvāvasthāsu dhīmatā  Ramsa svastho bhava mā śoco yātvā cāvasa tāṃ purīmtathā pitrā niyukto si vaśinā vadatāṃ vara  Ramyatrāham api tenaiva niyuktaḥ puṇyakarmaṇātatraivāhaṃ kariṣyāmi pitur āryasya śāsanam  Ramna mayā śāsanaṃ tasya tyaktuṃ nyāyyam ariṃdamatat tvayāpi sadā mānyaṃ sa vai bandhuḥ sa naḥ pitā  Ramevam uktvā tu virate rāme vacanam arthavatuvāca bharataś citraṃ dhārmiko dhārmikaṃ vacaḥ  Ramko hi syād īdṛśo loke yādṛśas tvam ariṃdamana tvāṃ pravyathayed duḥkhaṃ prītir vā na praharṣayet  Ramsaṃmataś cāsi vṛddhānāṃ tāṃś ca pṛcchasi saṃśayānyathā mṛtas tathā jīvan yathāsati tathā sati  Ramyasyaiṣa buddhilābhaḥ syāt paritapyeta kena saḥsa evaṃ vyasanaṃ prāpya na viṣīditum arhati  Ramamaropamasattvas tvaṃ mahātmā satyasaṃgaraḥsarvajñaḥ sarvadarśī ca buddhimāṃś cāsi rāghava  Ramna tvām evaṃ guṇair yuktaṃ prabhavābhavakovidamaviṣahyatamaṃ duḥkham āsādayitum arhati  Ramproṣite mayi yat pāpaṃ mātrā matkāraṇāt kṛtamkṣudrayā tad aniṣṭaṃ me prasīdatu bhavān mama  Ramdharmabandhena baddho smi tenemāṃ neha mātaramhanmi tīvreṇa daṇḍena daṇḍārhāṃ pāpakāriṇīm  Ramkathaṃ daśarathāj jātaḥ śuddhābhijanakarmaṇaḥjānan dharmam adharmiṣṭhaṃ kuryāṃ karma jugupsitam  Ramguruḥ kriyāvān vṛddhaś ca rājā pretaḥ piteti catātaṃ na parigarheyaṃ daivataṃ ceti saṃsadi  Ramko hi dharmārthayor hīnam īdṛśaṃ karma kilbiṣamstriyāḥ priyacikīrṣuḥ san kuryād dharmajña dharmavit  Ramantakāle hi bhūtāni muhyantīti purāśrutiḥrājñaivaṃ kurvatā loke pratyakṣā sā śrutiḥ kṛtā  Ramsādhvartham abhisaṃdhāya krodhān mohāc ca sāhasāttātasya yad atikrāntaṃ pratyāharatu tad bhavān  Rampitur hi samatikrāntaṃ putro yaḥ sādhu manyatetad apatyaṃ mataṃ loke viparītam ato nyathā  Ramtad apatyaṃ bhavān astu mā bhavān duṣkṛtaṃ pituḥabhipattā kṛtaṃ karma loke dhīravigarhitam  Ramkaikeyīṃ māṃ ca tātaṃ ca suhṛdo bāndhavāṃś ca naḥpaurajānapadān sarvāṃs trātu sarvam idaṃ bhavān  Ramkva cāraṇyaṃ kva ca kṣātraṃ kva jaṭāḥ kva ca pālanamīdṛśaṃ vyāhataṃ karma na bhavān kartum arhati  Ramatha kleśajam eva tvaṃ dharmaṃ caritum icchasidharmeṇa caturo varṇān pālayan kleśam āpnuhi  Ramcaturṇām āśramāṇāṃ hi gārhasthyaṃ śreṣṭham āśramamāhur dharmajña dharmajñās taṃ kathaṃ tyaktum arhasi  Ramśrutena bālaḥ sthānena janmanā bhavato hy ahamsa kathaṃ pālayiṣyāmi bhūmiṃ bhavati tiṣṭhati  Ramhīnabuddhiguṇo bālo hīnaḥ sthānena cāpy ahambhavatā ca vinā bhūto na vartayitum utsahe  Ramidaṃ nikhilam avyagraṃ pitryaṃ rājyam akaṇṭakamanuśādhi svadharmeṇa dharmajña saha bāndhavaiḥ  Ramihaiva tvābhiṣiñcantu dharmajña saha bāndhavaiḥṛtvijaḥ savasiṣṭhāś ca mantravan mantrakovidāḥ  Ramabhiṣiktas tvam asmābhir ayodhyāṃ pālane vrajavijitya tarasā lokān marudbhir iva vāsavaḥ  Ramṛṇāni trīṇy apākurvan durhṛdaḥ sādhu nirdahansuhṛdas tarpayan kāmais tvam evātrānuśādhi mām  Ramadyārya muditāḥ santu suhṛdas te bhiṣecaneadya bhītāḥ pālayantāṃ durhṛdas te diśo daśa  Ramākrośaṃ mama mātuś ca pramṛjya puruṣarṣabhaadya tatra bhavantaṃ ca pitaraṃ rakṣa kilbiṣāt  Ramśirasā tvābhiyāce haṃ kuruṣva karuṇāṃ mayibāndhaveṣu ca sarveṣu bhūteṣv iva maheśvaraḥ  Ramatha vā pṛṣṭhataḥ kṛtvā vanam eva bhavān itaḥgamiṣyati gamiṣyāmi bhavatā sārdham apy aham  Ramtathāpi rāmo bharatena tāmyatā prasādyamānaḥ śirasā mahīpatiḥna caiva cakre gamanāya sattvavān matiṃ pitus tadvacane pratiṣṭhitaḥ  Ramtad adbhutaṃ sthairyam avekṣya rāghave samaṃ jano harṣam avāpa duḥkhitaḥna yāty ayodhyām iti duḥkhito bhavat sthirapratijñatvam avekṣya harṣitaḥ  Ramtam ṛtvijo naigamayūthavallabhās tathā visaṃjñāśrukalāś ca mātaraḥtathā bruvāṇaṃ bharataṃ pratuṣṭuvuḥ praṇamya rāmaṃ ca yayācire saha  Rampunar evaṃ bruvāṇaṃ tu bharataṃ lakṣmaṇāgrajaḥpratyuvāca tataḥ śrīmāñ jñātimadhye tisatkṛtaḥ  Ramupapannam idaṃ vākyaṃ yat tvam evam abhāṣathāḥjātaḥ putro daśarathāt kaikeyyāṃ rājasattamāt  Rampurā bhrātaḥ pitā naḥ sa mātaraṃ te samudvahanmātāmahe samāśrauṣīd rājyaśulkam anuttamam  Ramdevāsure ca saṃgrāme jananyai tava pārthivaḥsamprahṛṣṭo dadau rājā varam ārādhitaḥ prabhuḥ  Ramtataḥ sā saṃpratiśrāvya tava mātā yaśasvinīayācata naraśreṣṭhaṃ dvau varau varavarṇinī  Ramtava rājyaṃ naravyāghra mama pravrājanaṃ tathātac ca rājā tathā tasyai niyuktaḥ pradadau varam  Ramtena pitrāham apy atra niyuktaḥ puruṣarṣabhacaturdaśa vane vāsaṃ varṣāṇi varadānikam  Ramso haṃ vanam idaṃ prāpto nirjanaṃ lakṣmaṇānvitaḥśītayā cāpratidvandvaḥ satyavāde sthitaḥ pituḥ  Rambhavān api tathety eva pitaraṃ satyavādinamkartum arhati rājendraṃ kṣipram evābhiṣecanāt  Ramṛṇān mocaya rājānaṃ matkṛte bharata prabhumpitaraṃ trāhi dharmajña mātaraṃ cābhinandaya  Ramśrūyate hi purā tāta śrutir gītā yaśasvinīgayena yajamānena gayeṣv eva pitṝn prati  Rampuṃnāmnā narakād yasmāt pitaraṃ trāyate sutaḥtasmāt putra iti proktaḥ pitṝn yat pāti vā sutaḥ  Rameṣṭavyā bahavaḥ putrā guṇavanto bahuśrutāḥteṣāṃ vai samavetānām api kaścid gayāṃ vrajet  Ramevaṃ rājarṣayaḥ sarve pratītā rājanandanatasmāt trāhi naraśreṣṭha pitaraṃ narakāt prabho  Ramayodhyāṃ gaccha bharata prakṛtīr anurañjayaśatrughnasahito vīra saha sarvair dvijātibhiḥ  Rampravekṣye daṇḍakāraṇyam aham apy avilambayanābhyāṃ tu sahito rājan vaidehyā lakṣmaṇena ca  Ramtvaṃ rājā bhava bharata svayaṃ narāṇāṃ vanyānām aham api rājarāṇ mṛgāṇāmgaccha tvaṃ puravaram adya samprahṛṣṭaḥ saṃhṛṣṭas tv aham api daṇḍakān pravekṣye  Ramchāyāṃ te dinakarabhāḥ prabādhamānaṃ varṣatraṃ bharata karotu mūrdhni śītāmeteṣām aham api kānanadrumāṇāṃ chāyāṃ tām atiśayinīṃ sukhaṃ śrayiṣye  Ramśatrughnaḥ kuśalamatis tu te sahāyaḥ saumitrir mama viditaḥ pradhānamitramcatvāras tanayavarā vayaṃ narendraṃ satyasthaṃ bharata carāma mā viṣādam  Ramāśvāsayantaṃ bharataṃ jābālir brāhmaṇottamaḥuvāca rāmaṃ dharmajñaṃ dharmāpetam idaṃ vacaḥ  Ramsādhu rāghava mā bhūt te buddhir evaṃ nirarthakāprākṛtasya narasyeva āryabuddhes tapasvinaḥ  Ramkaḥ kasya puruṣo bandhuḥ kim āpyaṃ kasya kenacityad eko jāyate jantur eka eva vinaśyati  Ramtasmān mātā pitā ceti rāma sajjeta yo naraḥunmatta iva sa jñeyo nāsti kāciddhi kasyacit  Ramyathā grāmāntaraṃ gacchan naraḥ kaścit kvacid vasetutsṛjya ca tam āvāsaṃ pratiṣṭhetāpare hani  Ramevam eva manuṣyāṇāṃ pitā mātā gṛhaṃ vasuāvāsamātraṃ kākutstha sajjante nātra sajjanāḥ  Rampitryaṃ rājyaṃ samutsṛjya sa nārhati narottamaāsthātuṃ kāpathaṃ duḥkhaṃ viṣamaṃ bahukaṇṭakam  Ramsamṛddhāyām ayodhyāyām ātmānam abhiṣecayaekaveṇīdharā hi tvāṃ nagarī sampratīkṣate  Ramrājabhogān anubhavan mahārhān pārthivātmajavihara tvam ayodhyāyāṃ yathā śakras triviṣṭape  Ramna te kaścid daśaratas tvaṃ ca tasya na kaścanaanyo rājā tvam anyaś ca tasmāt kuru yad ucyate  Ramgataḥ sa nṛpatis tatra gantavyaṃ yatra tena vaipravṛttir eṣā martyānāṃ tvaṃ tu mithyā vihanyase  Ramarthadharmaparā ye ye tāṃs tāñ śocāmi netarānte hi duḥkham iha prāpya vināśaṃ pretya bhejire  Ramaṣṭakāpitṛdaivatyam ity ayaṃ prasṛto janaḥannasyopadravaṃ paśya mṛto hi kim aśiṣyati  Ramyadi bhuktam ihānyena deham anyasya gacchatidadyāt pravasataḥ śrāddhaṃ na tat pathy aśanaṃ bhavet  Ramdānasaṃvananā hy ete granthā medhāvibhiḥ kṛtāḥyajasva dehi dīkṣasva tapas tapyasva saṃtyaja  Ramsa nāsti param ity eva kuru buddhiṃ mahāmatepratyakṣaṃ yat tad ātiṣṭha parokṣaṃ pṛṣṭhataḥ kuru  Ramsatāṃ buddhiṃ puraskṛtya sarvalokanidarśinīmrājyaṃ tvaṃ pratigṛhṇīṣva bharatena prasāditaḥ  Ramjābāles tu vacaḥ śrutvā rāmaḥ satyātmanāṃ varaḥuvāca parayā yuktyā svabuddhyā cāvipannayā  Rambhavān me priyakāmārthaṃ vacanaṃ yad ihoktavānakāryaṃ kāryasaṃkāśam apathyaṃ pathyasaṃmitam  Ramnirmaryādas tu puruṣaḥ pāpācārasamanvitaḥmānaṃ na labhate satsu bhinnacāritradarśanaḥ  Ramkulīnam akulīnaṃ vā vīraṃ puruṣamāninamcāritram eva vyākhyāti śuciṃ vā yadi vāśucim  Ramanāryas tv āryasaṃkāśaḥ śaucāddhīnas tathā śuciḥlakṣaṇyavad alakṣaṇyo duḥśīlaḥ śīlavān iva  Ramadharmaṃ dharmaveṣeṇa yadīmaṃ lokasaṃkaramabhipatsye śubhaṃ hitvā kriyāvidhivivarjitam  Ramkaś cetayānaḥ puruṣaḥ kāryākāryavicakṣaṇaḥbahu maṃsyati māṃ loke durvṛttaṃ lokadūṣaṇam  Ramkasya yāsyāmy ahaṃ vṛttaṃ kena vā svargam āpnuyāmanayā vartamāno haṃ vṛttyā hīnapratijñayā  Ramkāmavṛttas tv ayaṃ lokaḥ kṛtsnaḥ samupavartateyadvṛttāḥ santi rājānas tadvṛttāḥ santi hi prajāḥ  Ramsatyam evānṛśaṃsyaṃ ca rājavṛttaṃ sanātanamtasmāt satyātmakaṃ rājyaṃ satye lokaḥ pratiṣṭhitaḥ  Ramṛṣayaś caiva devāś ca satyam eva hi meniresatyavādī hi loke smin paramaṃ gacchati kṣayam  Ramudvijante yathā sarpān narād anṛtavādinaḥdharmaḥ satyaṃ paro loke mūlaṃ svargasya cocyate  Ramsatyam eveśvaro loke satyaṃ padmā samāśritāsatyamūlāni sarvāṇi satyān nāsti paraṃ padam  Ramdattam iṣṭaṃ hutaṃ caiva taptāni ca tapāṃsi cavedāḥ satyapratiṣṭhānās tasmāt satyaparo bhavet  Ramekaḥ pālayate lokam ekaḥ pālayate kulammajjaty eko hi niraya ekaḥ svarge mahīyate  Ramso haṃ pitur nideśaṃ tu kimarthaṃ nānupālayesatyapratiśravaḥ satyaṃ satyena samayīkṛtaḥ  Ramnaiva lobhān na mohād vā na cājñānāt tamonvitaḥsetuṃ satyasya bhetsyāmi guroḥ satyapratiśravaḥ  Ramasatyasaṃdhasya sataś calasyāsthiracetasaḥnaiva devā na pitaraḥ pratīcchantīti naḥ śrutam  Rampratyagātmam imaṃ dharmaṃ satyaṃ paśyāmy ahaṃ svayambhāraḥ satpuruṣācīrṇas tadartham abhinandyate  Ramkṣātraṃ dharmam ahaṃ tyakṣye hy adharmaṃ dharmasaṃhitamkṣudrair nṛśaṃsair lubdhaiś ca sevitaṃ pāpakarmabhiḥ  Ramkāyena kurute pāpaṃ manasā sampradhārya caanṛtaṃ jihvayā cāha trividhaṃ karma pātakam  Rambhūmiḥ kīrtir yaśo lakṣmīḥ puruṣaṃ prārthayanti hisvargasthaṃ cānubadhnanti satyam eva bhajeta tat  Ramśreṣṭhaṃ hy anāryam eva syād yad bhavān avadhārya māmāha yuktikarair vākyair idaṃ bhadraṃ kuruṣva ha  Ramkathaṃ hy ahaṃ pratijñāya vanavāsam imaṃ guroḥbharatasya kariṣyāmi vaco hitvā guror vacaḥ  Ramsthirā mayā pratijñātā pratijñā gurusaṃnidhauprahṛṣṭamānasā devī kaikeyī cābhavat tadā  Ramvanavāsaṃ vasann evaṃ śucir niyatabhojanaḥmūlaiḥ puṣpaiḥ phalaiḥ puṇyaiḥ pitṝn devāṃś ca tarpayan  Ramsaṃtuṣṭapañcavargo haṃ lokayātrāṃ pravartayeakuhaḥ śraddadhānaḥ san kāryākāryavicakṣaṇaḥ  Ramkarmabhūmim imāṃ prāpya kartavyaṃ karma yac chubhamagnir vāyuś ca somaś ca karmaṇāṃ phalabhāginaḥ  Ramśataṃ kratūnām āhṛtya devarāṭ tridivaṃ gataḥtapāṃsy ugrāṇi cāsthāya divaṃ yātā maharṣayaḥ  Ramsatyaṃ ca dharmaṃ ca parākramaṃ ca bhūtānukampāṃ priyavāditāṃ cadvijātidevātithipūjanaṃ ca panthānam āhus tridivasya santaḥ  Ramdharme ratāḥ satpuruṣaiḥ sametās tejasvino dānaguṇapradhānāḥahiṃsakā vītamalāś ca loke bhavanti pūjyā munayaḥ pradhānāḥ  Ramkruddham ājñāya rāmaṃ tu vasiṣṭhaḥ pratyuvāca hajābālir api jānīte lokasyāsya gatāgatimnivartayitukāmas tu tvām etad vākyam abravīt  Ramimāṃ lokasamutpattiṃ lokanātha nibodha mesarvaṃ salilam evāsīt pṛthivī yatra nirmitātataḥ samabhavad brahmā svayambhūr daivataiḥ saha  Ramsa varāhas tato bhūtvā projjahāra vasuṃdharāmasṛjac ca jagat sarvaṃ saha putraiḥ kṛtātmabhiḥ  Ramākāśaprabhavo brahmā śāśvato nitya avyayaḥtasmān marīciḥ saṃjajñe marīceḥ kaśyapaḥ sutaḥ  Ramvivasvān kaśyapāj jajñe manur vaivasvataḥ smṛtaḥsa tu prajāpatiḥ pūrvam ikṣvākus tu manoḥ sutaḥ  Ramyasyeyaṃ prathamaṃ dattā samṛddhā manunā mahītam ikṣvākum ayodhyāyāṃ rājānaṃ viddhi pūrvakam  Ramikṣvākos tu sutaḥ śrīmān kukṣir eveti viśrutaḥkukṣer athātmajo vīro vikukṣir udapadyata  Ramvikukṣes tu mahātejā bāṇaḥ putraḥ pratāpavānbāṇasya tu mahābāhur anaraṇyo mahāyaśāḥ  Ramnānāvṛṣṭir babhūvāsmin na durbhikṣaṃ satāṃ vareanaraṇye mahārāje taskaro vāpi kaścana  Ramanaraṇyān mahābāhuḥ pṛthū rājā babhūva hatasmāt pṛthor mahārājas triśaṅkur udapadyatasa satyavacanād vīraḥ saśarīro divaṃ gataḥ  Ramtriśaṅkor abhavat sūnur dhundhumāro mahāyaśāḥdhundhumārān mahātejā yuvanāśvo vyajāyata  Ramyuvanāśvasutaḥ śrīmān māndhātā samapadyatamāndhātus tu mahātejāḥ susaṃdhir udapadyata  Ramsusaṃdher api putrau dvau dhruvasaṃdhiḥ prasenajityaśasvī dhruvasaṃdhes tu bharato ripusūdanaḥ  Rambharatāt tu mahābāhor asito nāma jāyatayasyaite pratirājāna udapadyanta śatravaḥhaihayās tālajaṅghāś ca śūrāś ca śaśabindavaḥ  Ramtāṃs tu sarvān prativyūhya yuddhe rājā pravāsitaḥsa ca śailavare ramye babhūvābhirato muniḥdve cāsya bhārye garbhiṇyau babhūvatur iti śrutiḥ  Rambhārgavaś cyavano nāma himavantam upāśritaḥtam ṛṣiṃ samupāgamya kālindī tv abhyavādayat  Ramsa tām abhyavadad vipro varepsuṃ putrajanmanitataḥ sā gṛham āgamya devī putraṃ vyajāyata  Ramsapatnyā tu garas tasyai datto garbhajighāṃsayāgareṇa saha tenaiva jātaḥ sa sagaro bhavat  Ramsa rājā sagaro nāma yaḥ samudram akhānayatiṣṭvā parvaṇi vegena trāsayantam imāḥ prajāḥ  Ramasamañjas tu putro bhūt sagarasyeti naḥ śrutamjīvann eva sa pitrā tu nirastaḥ pāpakarmakṛt  Ramaṃśumān iti putro bhūd asamañjasya vīryavāndilīpo ṃśumataḥ putro dilīpasya bhagīrathaḥ  Rambhagīrathāt kakutsthas tu kākutsthā yena tu smṛtāḥkakutsthasya tu putro bhūd raghur yena tu rāghavaḥ  Ramraghos tu putras tejasvī pravṛddhaḥ puruṣādakaḥkalmāṣapādaḥ saudāsa ity evaṃ prathito bhuvi  Ramkalmāṣapādaputro bhūc chaṅkhaṇas tv iti viśrutaḥyas tu tad vīryam āsādya sahaseno vyanīnaśat  Ramśaṅkhaṇasya tu putro bhūc chūraḥ śrīmān sudarśanaḥsudarśanasyāgnivarṇa agnivarṇasya śīghragaḥ  Ramśīghragasya maruḥ putro maroḥ putraḥ praśuśrukaḥpraśuśrukasya putro bhūd ambarīṣo mahādyutiḥ  Ramambarīṣasya putro bhūn nahuṣaḥ satyavikramaḥnahuṣasya ca nābhāgaḥ putraḥ paramadhārmikaḥ  Ramajaś ca suvrataś caiva nābhāgasya sutāv ubhauajasya caiva dharmātmā rājā daśarathaḥ sutaḥ  Ramtasya jyeṣṭho si dāyādo rāma ity abhiviśrutaḥtad gṛhāṇa svakaṃ rājyam avekṣasva jagan nṛpa  Ramikṣvākūṇāṃ hi sarveṣāṃ rājā bhavati pūrvajaḥpūrvajenāvaraḥ putro jyeṣṭho rājye bhiṣicyate  Ramsa rāghavāṇāṃ kuladharmam ātmanaḥ sanātanaṃ nādya vihātum arhasiprabhūtaratnām anuśādhi medinīṃ prabhūtarāṣṭrāṃ pitṛvan mahāyaśāḥ  Ramvasiṣṭhas tu tadā rāmam uktvā rājapurohitaḥabravīd dharmasaṃyuktaṃ punar evāparaṃ vacaḥ  Rampuruṣasyeha jātasya bhavanti guravas trayaḥācāryaś caiva kākutstha pitā mātā ca rāghava  Rampitā hy enaṃ janayati puruṣaṃ puruṣarṣabhaprajñāṃ dadāti cācāryas tasmāt sa gurur ucyate  Ramsa te haṃ pitur ācāryas tava caiva paraṃtapamama tvaṃ vacanaṃ kurvan nātivarteḥ satāṃ gatim  Ramimā hi te pariṣadaḥ śreṇayaś ca samāgatāḥeṣu tāta caran dharmaṃ nātivarteḥ satāṃ gatim  Ramvṛddhāyā dharmaśīlāyā mātur nārhasy avartitumasyās tu vacanaṃ kurvan nātivarteḥ satāṃ gatim  Rambharatasya vacaḥ kurvan yācamānasya rāghavaātmānaṃ nātivartes tvaṃ satyadharmaparākrama  Ramevaṃ madhuram uktas tu guruṇā rāghavaḥ svayampratyuvāca samāsīnaṃ vasiṣṭhaṃ puruṣarṣabhaḥ  Ramyan mātāpitarau vṛttaṃ tanaye kurutaḥ sadāna supratikaraṃ tat tu mātrā pitrā ca yat kṛtam  Ramyathāśakti pradānena snāpanāc chādanena canityaṃ ca priyavādena tathā saṃvardhanena ca  Ramsa hi rājā janayitā pitā daśaratho mamaājñātaṃ yan mayā tasya na tan mithyā bhaviṣyati  Ramevam uktas tu rāmeṇa bharataḥ pratyanantaramuvāca paramodāraḥ sūtaṃ paramadurmanāḥ  Ramiha me sthaṇḍile śīghraṃ kuśān āstara sāratheāryaṃ pratyupavekṣyāmi yāvan me na prasīdati  Ramanāhāro nirāloko dhanahīno yathā dvijaḥśeṣye purastāc chālāyā yāvan na pratiyāsyati  Ramsa tu rāmam avekṣantaṃ sumantraṃ prekṣya durmanāḥkuśottaram upasthāpya bhūmāv evāstarat svayam  Ramtam uvāca mahātejā rāmo rājarṣisattamāḥkiṃ māṃ bharata kurvāṇaṃ tāta pratyupavekṣyasi  Rambrāhmaṇo hy ekapārśvena narān roddhum ihārhatina tu mūrdhāvasiktānāṃ vidhiḥ pratyupaveśane  Ramuttiṣṭha naraśārdūla hitvaitad dāruṇaṃ vratampuravaryām itaḥ kṣipram ayodhyāṃ yāhi rāghava  Ramāsīnas tv eva bharataḥ paurajānapadaṃ janamuvāca sarvataḥ prekṣya kim āryaṃ nānuśāsatha  Ramte tam ūcur mahātmānaṃ paurajānapadā janāḥkākutstham abhijānīmaḥ samyag vadati rāghavaḥ  Rameṣo pi hi mahābhāgaḥ pitur vacasi tiṣṭhatiata eva na śaktāḥ smo vyāvartayitum añjasā  Ramteṣām ājñāya vacanaṃ rāmo vacanam abravītevaṃ nibodha vacanaṃ suhṛdāṃ dharmacakṣuṣām  Rametac caivobhayaṃ śrutvā samyak saṃpaśya rāghavauttiṣṭha tvaṃ mahābāho māṃ ca spṛśa tathodakam  Ramathotthāya jalaṃ spṛṣṭvā bharato vākyam abravītśṛṇvantu me pariṣado mantriṇaḥ śreṇayas tathā  Ramna yāce pitaraṃ rājyaṃ nānuśāsāmi mātaramāryaṃ paramadharmajñam abhijānāmi rāghavam  Ramyadi tv avaśyaṃ vastavyaṃ kartavyaṃ ca pitur vacaḥaham eva nivatsyāmi caturdaśa vane samāḥ  Ramdharmātmā tasya tathyena bhrātur vākyena vismitaḥuvāca rāmaḥ samprekṣya paurajānapadaṃ janam  Ramvikrītam āhitaṃ krītaṃ yat pitrā jīvatā mamana tal lopayituṃ śakyaṃ mayā vā bharatena vā  Ramupadhir na mayā kāryo vanavāse jugupsitaḥyuktam uktaṃ ca kaikeyyā pitrā me sukṛtaṃ kṛtam  Ramjānāmi bharataṃ kṣāntaṃ gurusatkārakāriṇamsarvam evātra kalyāṇaṃ satyasaṃdhe mahātmani  Ramanena dharmaśīlena vanāt pratyāgataḥ punaḥbhrātrā saha bhaviṣyāmi pṛthivyāḥ patir uttamaḥ  Ramvṛto rājā hi kaikeyyā mayā tadvacanaṃ kṛtamanṛtān mocayānena pitaraṃ taṃ mahīpatim  Ramtam apratimatejobhyāṃ bhrātṛbhyāṃ romaharṣaṇamvismitāḥ saṃgamaṃ prekṣya samavetā maharṣayaḥ  Ramantarhitās tv ṛṣigaṇāḥ siddhāś ca paramarṣayaḥtau bhrātarau mahātmānau kākutsthau praśaśaṃsire  Ramsa dhanyo yasya putrau dvau dharmajñau dharmavikramauśrutvā vayaṃ hi sambhāṣām ubhayoḥ spṛhayāmahe  Ramtatas tv ṛṣigaṇāḥ kṣipraṃ daśagrīvavadhaiṣiṇaḥbharataṃ rājaśārdūlam ity ūcuḥ saṃgatā vacaḥ  Ramkule jāta mahāprājña mahāvṛtta mahāyaśaḥgrāhyaṃ rāmasya vākyaṃ te pitaraṃ yady avekṣase  Ramsadānṛṇam imaṃ rāmaṃ vayam icchāmahe pituḥanṛṇatvāc ca kaikeyyāḥ svargaṃ daśaratho gataḥ  Rametāvad uktvā vacanaṃ gandharvāḥ samaharṣayaḥrājarṣayaś caiva tathā sarve svāṃ svāṃ gatiṃ gatāḥ  Ramhlāditas tena vākyena śubhena śubhadarśanaḥrāmaḥ saṃhṛṣṭavadanas tān ṛṣīn abhyapūjayat  Ramsrastagātras tu bharataḥ sa vācā sajjamānayākṛtāñjalir idaṃ vākyaṃ rāghavaṃ punar abravīt  Ramrājadharmam anuprekṣya kuladharmānusaṃtatimkartum arhasi kākutstha mama mātuś ca yācanām  Ramrakṣituṃ sumahad rājyam aham ekas tu notsahepaurajānapadāṃś cāpi raktān rañjayituṃ tathā  Ramjñātayaś ca hi yodhāś ca mitrāṇi suhṛdaś ca naḥtvām eva pratikāṅkṣante parjanyam iva karṣakāḥ  Ramidaṃ rājyaṃ mahāprājña sthāpaya pratipadya hiśaktimān asi kākutstha lokasya paripālane  Ramity uktvā nyapatad bhrātuḥ pādayor bharatas tadābhṛśaṃ samprārthayāmāsa rāmam evaṃ priyaṃvadaḥ  Ramtam aṅke bhrātaraṃ kṛtvā rāmo vacanam abravītśyāmaṃ nalinapattrākṣaṃ mattahaṃsasvaraṃ svayam  Ramāgatā tvām iyaṃ buddhiḥ svajā vainayikī ca yābhṛśam utsahase tāta rakṣituṃ pṛthivīm api  Ramamātyaiś ca suhṛdbhiś ca buddhimadbhiś ca mantribhiḥsarvakāryāṇi saṃmantrya sumahānty api kāraya  Ramlakṣmīś candrād apeyād vā himavān vā himaṃ tyajetatīyāt sāgaro velāṃ na pratijñām ahaṃ pituḥ  Ramkāmād vā tāta lobhād vā mātrā tubhyam idaṃ kṛtamna tan manasi kartavyaṃ vartitavyaṃ ca mātṛvat  Ramevaṃ bruvāṇaṃ bharataḥ kausalyāsutam abravīttejasādityasaṃkāśaṃ pratipaccandradarśanam  Ramadhirohārya pādābhyāṃ pāduke hemabhūṣiteete hi sarvalokasya yogakṣemaṃ vidhāsyataḥ  Ramso dhiruhya naravyāghraḥ pāduke hy avaruhya caprāyacchat sumahātejā bharatāya mahātmane  Ramsa pāduke te bharataḥ pratāpavān svalaṃkṛte samparigṛhya dharmavitpradakṣiṇaṃ caiva cakāra rāghavaṃ cakāra caivottamanāgamūrdhani  Ramathānupūrvyāt pratipūjya taṃ janaṃ gurūṃś ca mantriprakṛtīs tathānujauvyasarjayad rāghavavaṃśavardhanaḥ sthitaḥ svadharme himavān ivācalaḥ  Ramtaṃ mātaro bāṣpagṛhītakaṇṭhyo duḥkhena nāmantrayituṃ hi śekuḥsa tv eva mātṝn abhivādya sarvā rudan kuṭīṃ svāṃ praviveśa rāmaḥ  Ramtataḥ śirasi kṛtvā tu pāduke bharatas tadāāruroha rathaṃ hṛṣṭaḥ śatrughnena samanvitaḥ  Ramvasiṣṭho vāmadevaś ca jābāliś ca dṛḍhavrataḥagrataḥ prayayuḥ sarve mantriṇo mantrapūjitāḥ  Rammandākinīṃ nadīṃ ramyāṃ prāṅmukhās te yayus tadāpradakṣiṇaṃ ca kurvāṇāś citrakūṭaṃ mahāgirim  Rampaśyan dhātusahasrāṇi ramyāṇi vividhāni caprayayau tasya pārśvena sasainyo bharatas tadā  Ramadūrāc citrakūṭasya dadarśa bharatas tadāāśramaṃ yatra sa munir bharadvājaḥ kṛtālayaḥ  Ramsa tam āśramam āgamya bharadvājasya buddhimānavatīrya rathāt pādau vavande kulanandanaḥ  Ramtato hṛṣṭo bharadvājo bharataṃ vākyam abravītapi kṛtyaṃ kṛtaṃ tāta rāmeṇa ca samāgatam  Ramevam uktas tu bharato bharadvājena dhīmatāpratyuvāca bharadvājaṃ bharato dharmavatsalaḥ  Ramsa yācyamāno guruṇā mayā ca dṛḍhavikramaḥrāghavaḥ paramaprīto vasiṣṭhaṃ vākyam abravīt  Rampituḥ pratijñāṃ tām eva pālayiṣyāmi tattvataḥcaturdaśa hi varṣāṇi yā pratijñā pitur mama  Ramevam ukto mahāprājño vasiṣṭhaḥ pratyuvāca havākyajño vākyakuśalaṃ rāghavaṃ vacanaṃ mahat  Ramete prayaccha saṃhṛṣṭaḥ pāduke hemabhūṣiteayodhyāyāṃ mahāprājña yogakṣemakare tava  Ramevam ukto vasiṣṭhena rāghavaḥ prāṅmukhaḥ sthitaḥpāduke hemavikṛte mama rājyāya te dadau  Ramnivṛtto ham anujñāto rāmeṇa sumahātmanāayodhyām eva gacchāmi gṛhītvā pāduke śubhe  Rametac chrutvā śubhaṃ vākyaṃ bharatasya mahātmanaḥbharadvājaḥ śubhataraṃ munir vākyam udāharat  Ramnaitac citraṃ naravyāghra śīlavṛttavatāṃ varayad āryaṃ tvayi tiṣṭhet tu nimne vṛṣṭim ivodakam  Ramamṛtaḥ sa mahābāhuḥ pitā daśarathas tavayasya tvam īdṛśaḥ putro dharmātmā dharmavatsalaḥ  Ramtam ṛṣiṃ tu mahātmānam uktavākyaṃ kṛtāñjaliḥāmantrayitum ārebhe caraṇāv upagṛhya ca  Ramtataḥ pradakṣiṇaṃ kṛtvā bharadvājaṃ punaḥ punaḥbharatas tu yayau śrīmān ayodhyāṃ saha mantribhiḥ  Ramyānaiś ca śakaṭaiś caiva hayair nāgaiś ca sā camūḥpunar nivṛttā vistīrṇā bharatasyānuyāyinī  Ramtatas te yamunāṃ divyāṃ nadīṃ tīrtvormimālinīmdadṛśus tāṃ punaḥ sarve gaṅgāṃ śivajalāṃ nadīm  Ramtāṃ ramyajalasampūrṇāṃ saṃtīrya sahabāndhavaḥśṛṅgaverapuraṃ ramyaṃ praviveśa sasainikaḥ  Ramśṛṅgaverapurād bhūya ayodhyāṃ saṃdadarśa habharato duḥkhasaṃtaptaḥ sārathiṃ cedam abravīt  Ramsārathe paśya vidhvastā ayodhyā na prakāśatenirākārā nirānandā dīnā pratihatasvanā  Ramsnigdhagambhīraghoṣeṇa syandanenopayān prabhuḥayodhyāṃ bharataḥ kṣipraṃ praviveśa mahāyaśāḥ  Rambiḍālolūkacaritām ālīnanaravāraṇāmtimirābhyāhatāṃ kālīm aprakāśāṃ niśām iva  Ramrāhuśatroḥ priyāṃ patnīṃ śriyā prajvalitaprabhāmgraheṇābhyutthitenaikāṃ rohiṇīm iva pīḍitām  Ramalpoṣṇakṣubdhasalilāṃ gharmottaptavihaṃgamāmlīnamīnajhaṣagrāhāṃ kṛśāṃ girinadīm iva  Ramvidhūmām iva hemābhām adhvarāgnisamutthitāmhavirabhyukṣitāṃ paścāc chikhāṃ vipralayaṃ gatām  Ramvidhvastakavacāṃ rugṇagajavājirathadhvajāmhatapravīrām āpannāṃ camūm iva mahāhave  Ramsaphenāṃ sasvanāṃ bhūtvā sāgarasya samutthitāmpraśāntamārutoddhūtāṃ jalormim iva niḥsvanām  Ramtyaktāṃ yajñāyudhaiḥ sarvair abhirūpaiś ca yājakaiḥsutyākāle vinirvṛtte vediṃ gataravām iva  Ramgoṣṭhamadhye sthitām ārtām acarantīṃ navaṃ tṛṇamgovṛṣeṇa parityaktāṃ gavāṃ patnīm ivotsukām  Ramprabhākarālaiḥ susnigdhaiḥ prajvaladbhir ivottamaiḥviyuktāṃ maṇibhir jātyair navāṃ muktāvalīm iva  Ramsahasā calitāṃ sthānān mahīṃ puṇyakṣayād gatāmsaṃhṛtadyutivistārāṃ tārām iva divaś cyutām  Rampuṣpanaddhāṃ vasantānte mattabhramaraśālinīmdrutadāvāgnivipruṣṭāṃ klāntāṃ vanalatām iva  Ramsaṃmūḍhanigamāṃ sarvāṃ saṃkṣiptavipaṇāpaṇāmpracchannaśaśinakṣatrāṃ dyām ivāmbudharair vṛtām  Ramkṣīṇapānottamair bhinnaiḥ śarāvair abhisaṃvṛtāmhataśauṇḍām ivākāśe pānabhūmim asaṃskṛtām  Ramvṛkṇabhūmitalāṃ nimnāṃ vṛkṇapātraiḥ samāvṛtāmupayuktodakāṃ bhagnāṃ prapāṃ nipatitām iva  Ramvipulāṃ vitatāṃ caiva yuktapāśāṃ tarasvināmbhūmau bāṇair viniṣkṛttāṃ patitāṃ jyām ivāyudhāt  Ramsahasā yuddhaśauṇḍena hayāroheṇa vāhitāmnikṣiptabhāṇḍām utsṛṣṭāṃ kiśorīm iva durbalām  Ramprāvṛṣi pravigāḍhāyāṃ praviṣṭasyābhramaṇḍalampracchannāṃ nīlajīmūtair bhāskarasya prabhām iva  Rambharatas tu rathasthaḥ sañ śrīmān daśarathātmajaḥvāhayantaṃ rathaśreṣṭhaṃ sārathiṃ vākyam abravīt  Ramkiṃ nu khalv adya gambhīro mūrchito na niśamyateyathāpuram ayodhyāyāṃ gītavāditraniḥsvanaḥ  Ramvāruṇīmadagandhāś ca mālyagandhaś ca mūrchitaḥdhūpitāgarugandhaś ca na pravāti samantataḥ  Ramyānapravaraghoṣaś ca snigdhaś ca hayaniḥsvanaḥpramattagajanādaś ca mahāṃś ca rathaniḥsvanaḥnedānīṃ śrūyate puryām asyāṃ rāme vivāsite  Ramtaruṇaiś cāruveṣaiś ca narair unnatagāmibhiḥsaṃpatadbhir ayodhyāyāṃ na vibhānti mahāpathāḥ  Ramevaṃ bahuvidhaṃ jalpan viveśa vasatiṃ pituḥtena hīnāṃ narendreṇa siṃhahīnāṃ guhām iva  Ramtato nikṣipya mātṝn sa ayodhyāyāṃ dṛḍhavrataḥbharataḥ śokasaṃtapto gurūn idam athābravīt  Ramnandigrāmaṃ gamiṣyāmi sarvān āmantraye dya vaḥtatra duḥkham idaṃ sarvaṃ sahiṣye rāghavaṃ vinā  Ramgataś ca hi divaṃ rājā vanasthaś ca gurur mamarāmaṃ pratīkṣe rājyāya sa hi rājā mahāyaśāḥ  Rametac chrutvā śubhaṃ vākyaṃ bharatasya mahātmanaḥabruvan mantriṇaḥ sarve vasiṣṭhaś ca purohitaḥ  Ramsadṛśaṃ ślāghanīyaṃ ca yad uktaṃ bharata tvayāvacanaṃ bhrātṛvātsalyād anurūpaṃ tavaiva tat  Ramnityaṃ te bandhulubdhasya tiṣṭhato bhrātṛsauhṛdeāryamārgaṃ prapannasya nānumanyeta kaḥ pumān  Rammantriṇāṃ vacanaṃ śrutvā yathābhilaṣitaṃ priyamabravīt sārathiṃ vākyaṃ ratho me yujyatām iti  Ramprahṛṣṭavadanaḥ sarvā mātṝn samabhivādya saḥāruroha rathaṃ śrīmāñ śatrughnena samanvitaḥ  Ramāruhya tu rathaṃ śīghraṃ śatrughnabharatāv ubhauyayatuḥ paramaprītau vṛtau mantripurohitaiḥ  Ramagrato guravas tatra vasiṣṭhapramukhā dvijāḥprayayuḥ prāṅmukhāḥ sarve nandigrāmo yato bhavat  Rambalaṃ ca tad anāhūtaṃ gajāśvarathasaṃkulamprayayau bharate yāte sarve ca puravāsinaḥ  Ramrathasthaḥ sa tu dharmātmā bharato bhrātṛvatsalaḥnandigrāmaṃ yayau tūrṇaṃ śirasy ādhāya pāduke  Ramtatas tu bharataḥ kṣipraṃ nandigrāmaṃ praviśya saḥavatīrya rathāt tūrṇaṃ gurūn idam uvāca ha  Rametad rājyaṃ mama bhrātrā dattaṃ saṃnyāsavat svayamyogakṣemavahe ceme pāduke hemabhūṣitetam imaṃ pālayiṣyāmi rāghavāgamanaṃ prati  Ramkṣipraṃ saṃyojayitvā tu rāghavasya punaḥ svayamcaraṇau tau tu rāmasya drakṣyāmi sahapādukau  Ramtato nikṣiptabhāro haṃ rāghaveṇa samāgataḥnivedya gurave rājyaṃ bhajiṣye guruvṛttitām  Ramrāghavāya ca saṃnyāsaṃ dattveme varapādukerājyaṃ cedam ayodhyāṃ ca dhūtapāpo bhavāmi ca  Ramabhiṣikte tu kākutsthe prahṛṣṭamudite janeprītir mama yaśaś caiva bhaved rājyāc caturguṇam  Ramevaṃ tu vilapan dīno bharataḥ sa mahāyaśāḥnandigrāme karod rājyaṃ duḥkhito mantribhiḥ saha  Ramsa valkalajaṭādhārī muniveṣadharaḥ prabhuḥnandigrāme vasad vīraḥ sasainyo bharatas tadā
