babhūvādbhutaṃ yuddhaṃ tumulaṃ romaharṣaṇamrāmasyāsya mahāghoraṃ punas teṣāṃ ca rakṣasām  Ramtad drumāṇāṃ śilānāṃ ca varṣaṃ prāṇaharaṃ mahatpratijagrāha dharmātmā rāghavas tīkṣṇasāyakaiḥ  Rampratigṛhya ca tad varaṃ nimīlita ivarṣabhaḥrāmaḥ krodhaṃ paraṃ bheje vadhārthaṃ sarvarakṣasām  Ramtataḥ krodhasamāviṣṭaḥ pradīpta iva tejasāśarair abhyakirat sainyaṃ sarvataḥ sahadūṣaṇam  Ramtataḥ senāpatiḥ kruddho dūṣaṇaḥ śatrudūṣaṇaḥjagrāha giriśṛṅgābhaṃ parighaṃ romaharṣaṇam  Ramveṣṭitaṃ kāñcanaiḥ paṭṭair devasainyābhimardanamāyasaiḥ śaṅkubhis tīkṣṇaiḥ kīrṇaṃ paravasokṣitam  Ramvajrāśanisamasparśaṃ paragopuradāraṇamtaṃ mahoragasaṃkāśaṃ pragṛhya parighaṃ raṇedūṣaṇo bhyapatad rāmaṃ krūrakarmā niśācaraḥ  Ramtasyābhipatamānasya dūṣaṇasya sa rāghavaḥdvābhyāṃ śarābhyāṃ cicheda sahastābharaṇau bhujau  Rambhraṣṭas tasya mahākāyaḥ papāta raṇamūrdhaniparighaś chinnahastasya śakradhvaja ivāgrataḥ  Ramsa karābhyāṃ vikīrṇābhyāṃ papāta bhuvi dūṣaṇaḥviṣāṇābhyāṃ viśīrṇābhyāṃ manasvīva mahāgajaḥ  Ramdṛṣṭvā taṃ patitaṃ bhūmau dūṣaṇaṃ nihataṃ raṇesādhu sādhv iti kākutsthaṃ sarvabhūtāny apūjayan  Rametasminn antare kruddhās trayaḥ senāgrayāyinaḥsaṃhatyābhyadravan rāmaṃ mṛtyupāśāvapāśitāḥmahākapālaḥ sthūlākṣaḥ pramāthī ca mahābalaḥ  Rammahākapālo vipulaṃ śūlam udyamya rākṣasaḥsthūlākṣaḥ paṭṭiśaṃ gṛhya pramāthī ca paraśvadham  Ramdṛṣṭvaivāpatatas tāṃs tu rāghavaḥ sāyakaiḥ śitaiḥtīkṣṇāgraiḥ pratijagrāha samprāptān atithīn iva  Rammahākapālasya śiraś cicheda raghunandanaḥasaṃkhyeyais tu bāṇaughaiḥ pramamātha pramāthinam  Ramsthūlākṣasyākṣiṇī tīkṣṇaiḥ pūrayāmāsa sāyakaiḥsa papāta hato bhūmau viṭapīva mahādrumaḥ  Ramtataḥ pāvakasaṃkāśair hemavajravibhūṣitaiḥjaghanaśeṣaṃ tejasvī tasya sainyasya sāyakaiḥ  Ramte rukmapuṅkhā viśikhāḥ sadhūmā iva pāvakāḥnijaghnus tāni rakṣāṃsi vajrā iva mahādrumān  Ramrakṣasāṃ tu śataṃ rāmaḥ śatenaikena karṇināsahasraṃ ca sahasreṇa jaghāna raṇamūrdhani  Ramtair bhinnavarmābharaṇāś chinnabhinnaśarāsanāḥnipetuḥ śoṇitādigdhā dharaṇyāṃ rajanīcarāḥ  Ramtair muktakeśaiḥ samare patitaiḥ śoṇitokṣitaiḥāstīrṇā vasudhā kṛtsnā mahāvediḥ kuśair iva  Ramkṣaṇena tu mahāghoraṃ vanaṃ nihatarākṣasambabhūva nirayaprakhyaṃ māṃsaśoṇitakardamam  Ramcaturdaśa sahasrāṇi rakṣasāṃ bhīmakarmaṇāmhatāny ekena rāmeṇa mānuṣeṇa padātinā  Ramtasya sainyasya sarvasya kharaḥ śeṣo mahārathaḥrākṣasas triśirāś caiva rāmaś ca ripusūdanaḥ  Ramtatas tu tad bhīmabalaṃ mahāhave samīkṣya rāmeṇa hataṃ balīyasārathena rāmaṃ mahatā kharas tataḥ samāsasādendra ivodyatāśaniḥ  Ramkharaṃ tu rāmābhimukhaṃ prayāntaṃ vāhinīpatiḥrākṣasas triśirā nāma saṃnipatyedam abravīt  Rammāṃ niyojaya vikrānta saṃnivartasva sāhasātpaśya rāmaṃ mahābāhuṃ saṃyuge vinipātitam  Rampratijānāmi te satyam āyudhaṃ cāham ālabheyathā rāmaṃ vadhiṣyāmi vadhārhaṃ sarvarakṣasām  Ramahaṃ vāsya raṇe mṛtyur eṣa vā samare mamavinivartya raṇotsāhaṃ muhūrtaṃ prāśniko bhava  Ramprahṛṣṭo vā hate rāme janasthānaṃ prayāsyasimayi vā nihate rāmaṃ saṃyugāyopayāsyasi  Ramkharas triśirasā tena mṛtyulobhāt prasāditaḥgaccha yudhyety anujñāto rāghavābhimukho yayau  Ramtriśirāś ca rathenaiva vājiyuktena bhāsvatāabhyadravad raṇe rāmaṃ triśṛṅga iva parvataḥ  Ramśaradhārāsamūhān sa mahāmegha ivotsṛjanvyasṛjat sadṛśaṃ nādaṃ jalārdrasyeva dundubheḥ  Ramāgacchantaṃ triśirasaṃ rākṣasaṃ prekṣya rāghavaḥdhanuṣā pratijagrāha vidhunvan sāyakāñ śitān  Ramsa samprahāras tumulo rāmatriśirasor mahānbabhūvātīva balinoḥ siṃhakuñjarayor iva  Ramtatas triśirasā bāṇair lalāṭe tāḍitas tribhiḥamarṣī kupito rāmaḥ saṃrabdham idam abravīt  Ramaho vikramaśūrasya rākṣasasyedṛśaṃ balampuṣpair iva śarair yasya lalāṭe smi parikṣataḥmamāpi pratigṛhṇīṣva śarāṃś cāpaguṇacyutān  Ramevam uktvā tu saṃrabdhaḥ śarān āśīviṣopamāntriśirovakṣasi kruddho nijaghāna caturdaśa  Ramcaturbhis turagān asya śaraiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥnyapātayata tejasvī caturas tasya vājinaḥ  Ramaṣṭabhiḥ sāyakaiḥ sūtaṃ rathopasthe nyapātayatrāmaś cicheda bāṇena dhvajaṃ cāsya samucchritam  Ramtato hatarathāt tasmād utpatantaṃ niśācarambibheda rāmas taṃ bāṇair hṛdaye so bhavaj jaḍaḥ  Ramsāyakaiś cāprameyātmā sāmarṣas tasya rakṣasaḥśirāṃsy apātayat trīṇi vegavadbhis tribhiḥ śataiḥ  Ramsa bhūmau śoṇitodgārī rāmabāṇābhipīḍitaḥnyapatat patitaiḥ pūrvaṃ svaśirobhir niśācaraḥ  Ramhataśeṣās tato bhagnā rākṣasāḥ kharasaṃśrayāḥdravanti sma na tiṣṭhanti vyāghratrastā mṛgā iva  Ramtān kharo dravato dṛṣṭvā nivartya ruṣitaḥ svayamrāmam evābhidudrāva rāhuś candramasaṃ yathā  Ramnihataṃ dūṣaṇaṃ dṛṣṭvā raṇe triśirasā sahakharasyāpy abhavat trāso dṛṣṭvā rāmasya vikramam  Ramsa dṛṣṭvā rākṣasaṃ sainyam aviṣahyaṃ mahābalamhatam ekena rāmeṇa dūṣaṇas triśirā api  Ramtad balaṃ hatabhūyiṣṭhaṃ vimanāḥ prekṣya rākṣasaḥāsasāda kharo rāmaṃ namucir vāsavaṃ yathā  Ramvikṛṣya balavac cāpaṃ nārācān raktabhojanānkharaś cikṣepa rāmāya kruddhān āśīviṣān iva  Ramjyāṃ vidhunvan subahuśaḥ śikṣayāstrāṇi darśayancacāra samare mārgāñ śarai rathagataḥ kharaḥ  Ramsa sarvāś ca diśo bāṇaiḥ pradiśaś ca mahārathaḥpūrayāmāsa taṃ dṛṣṭvā rāmo pi sumahad dhanuḥ  Ramsa sāyakair durviṣahaiḥ sasphuliṅgair ivāgnibhiḥnabhaś cakārāvivaraṃ parjanya iva vṛṣṭibhiḥ  Ramtad babhūva śitair bāṇaiḥ khararāmavisarjitaiḥparyākāśam anākāśaṃ sarvataḥ śarasaṃkulam  Ramśarajālāvṛtaḥ sūryo na tadā sma prakāśateanyonyavadhasaṃrambhād ubhayoḥ samprayudhyatoḥ  Ramtato nālīkanārācais tīkṣṇāgraiś ca vikarṇibhiḥājaghāna raṇe rāmaṃ totrair iva mahādvipam  Ramtaṃ rathasthaṃ dhanuṣpāṇiṃ rākṣasaṃ paryavasthitamdadṛśuḥ sarvabhūtāni pāśahastam ivāntakam  Ramtaṃ siṃham iva vikrāntaṃ siṃhavikrāntagāminamdṛṣṭvā nodvijate rāmaḥ siṃhaḥ kṣudramṛgaṃ yathā  Ramtataḥ sūryanikāśena rathena mahatā kharaḥāsasāda raṇe rāmaṃ pataṃga iva pāvakam  Ramtato sya saśaraṃ cāpaṃ muṣṭideśe mahātmanaḥkharaś cicheda rāmasya darśayan pāṇilāghavam  Ramsa punas tv aparān sapta śarān ādāya varmaṇinijaghāna raṇe kruddhaḥ śakrāśanisamaprabhān  Ramtatas tat prahataṃ bāṇaiḥ kharamuktaiḥ suparvabhiḥpapāta kavacaṃ bhūmau rāmasyādityavarcasaḥ  Ramsa śarair arpitaḥ kruddhaḥ sarvagātreṣu rāghavaḥrarāja samare rāmo vidhūmo gnir iva jvalan  Ramtato gambhīranirhrādaṃ rāmaḥ śatrunibarhaṇaḥcakārāntāya sa ripoḥ sajyam anyan mahad dhanuḥ  Ramsumahad vaiṣṇavaṃ yat tad atisṛṣṭaṃ maharṣiṇāvaraṃ tad dhanur udyamya kharaṃ samabhidhāvata  Ramtataḥ kanakapuṅkhais tu śaraiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥcicheda rāmaḥ saṃkruddhaḥ kharasya samare dhvajam  Ramsa darśanīyo bahudhā vicchinnaḥ kāñcano dhvajaḥjagāma dharaṇīṃ sūryo devatānām ivājñayā  Ramtaṃ caturbhiḥ kharaḥ kruddho rāmaṃ gātreṣu mārgaṇaiḥvivyādha hṛdi marmajño mātaṃgam iva tomaraiḥ  Ramsa rāmo bahubhir bāṇaiḥ kharakārmukaniḥsṛtaiḥviddho rudhirasiktāṅgo babhūva ruṣito bhṛśam  Ramsa dhanur dhanvināṃ śreṣṭhaḥ pragṛhya paramāhavemumoca parameṣvāsaḥ ṣaṭ śarān abhilakṣitān  Ramśirasy ekena bāṇena dvābhyāṃ bāhvor athārpayattribhiś candrārdhavaktraiś ca vakṣasy abhijaghāna ha  Ramtataḥ paścān mahātejā nārācān bhāskaropamānjighāṃsū rākṣasaṃ kruddhas trayodaśa śilāśitān  Ramtato sya yugam ekena caturbhiś caturo hayānṣaṣṭhena ca śiraḥ saṃkhye cicheda kharasāratheḥ  Ramtribhis triveṇuṃ balavān dvābhyām akṣaṃ mahābalaḥdvādaśena tu bāṇena kharasya saśaraṃ dhanuḥ  Ramchittvā vajranikāśena rāghavaḥ prahasann ivatrayodaśenendrasamo bibheda samare kharam  Ramprabhagnadhanvā viratho hatāśvo hatasārathiḥgadāpāṇir avaplutya tasthau bhūmau kharas tadā  Ramtat karma rāmasya mahārathasya sametya devāś ca maharṣayaś caapūjayan prāñjalayaḥ prahṛṣṭās tadā vimānāgragatāḥ sametāḥ  Ramkharaṃ tu virathaṃ rāmo gadāpāṇim avasthitammṛdupūrvaṃ mahātejāḥ paruṣaṃ vākyam abravīt  Ramgajāśvarathasambādhe bale mahati tiṣṭhatākṛtaṃ sudāruṇaṃ karma sarvalokajugupsitam  Ramudvejanīyo bhūtānāṃ nṛśaṃsaḥ pāpakarmakṛttrayāṇām api lokānām īśvaro pi na tiṣṭhati  Ramkarma lokaviruddhaṃ tu kurvāṇaṃ kṣaṇadācaratīkṣṇaṃ sarvajano hanti sarpaṃ duṣṭam ivāgatam  Ramlobhāt pāpāni kurvāṇaḥ kāmād vā yo na budhyatebhraṣṭaḥ paśyati tasyāntaṃ brāhmaṇī karakād iva  Ramvasato daṇḍakāraṇye tāpasān dharmacāriṇaḥkiṃ nu hatvā mahābhāgān phalaṃ prāpsyasi rākṣasa  Ramna ciraṃ pāpakarmāṇaḥ krūrā lokajugupsitāḥaiśvaryaṃ prāpya tiṣṭhanti śīrṇamūlā iva drumāḥ  Ramavaśyaṃ labhate kartā phalaṃ pāpasya karmaṇaḥghoraṃ paryāgate kāle drumaḥ puṣpam ivārtavam  Ramnacirāt prāpyate loke pāpānāṃ karmaṇāṃ phalamsaviṣāṇām ivānnānāṃ bhuktānāṃ kṣaṇadācara  Rampāpam ācaratāṃ ghoraṃ lokasyāpriyam icchatāmaham āsādito rājā prāṇān hantuṃ niśācara  Ramadya hi tvāṃ mayā muktāḥ śarāḥ kāñcanabhūṣaṇāḥvidārya nipatiṣyanti valmīkam iva pannagāḥ  Ramye tvayā daṇḍakāraṇye bhakṣitā dharmacāriṇaḥtān adya nihataḥ saṃkhye sasainyo nugamiṣyasi  Ramadya tvāṃ nihataṃ bāṇaiḥ paśyantu paramarṣayaḥnirayasthaṃ vimānasthā ye tvayā hiṃsitāḥ purā  Ramprahara tvaṃ yathākāmaṃ kuru yatnaṃ kulādhamaadya te pātayiṣyāmi śiras tālaphalaṃ yathā  Ramevam uktas tu rāmeṇa kruddhaḥ saṃraktalocanaḥpratyuvāca tato rāmaṃ prahasan krodhamūrchitaḥ  Ramprākṛtān rākṣasān hatvā yuddhe daśarathātmajaātmanā katham ātmānam apraśasyaṃ praśaṃsasi  Ramvikrāntā balavanto vā ye bhavanti nararṣabhāḥkathayanti na te kiṃcit tejasā svena garvitāḥ  Ramprākṛtās tv akṛtātmāno loke kṣatriyapāṃsanāḥnirarthakaṃ vikatthante yathā rāma vikatthase  Ramkulaṃ vyapadiśan vīraḥ samare ko bhidhāsyatimṛtyukāle hi samprāpte svayam aprastave stavam  Ramsarvathā tu laghutvaṃ te katthanena vidarśitamsuvarṇapratirūpeṇa tapteneva kuśāgninā  Ramna tu mām iha tiṣṭhantaṃ paśyasi tvaṃ gadādharamdharādharam ivākampyaṃ parvataṃ dhātubhiś citam  Ramparyāpto haṃ gadāpāṇir hantuṃ prāṇān raṇe tavatrayāṇām api lokānāṃ pāśahasta ivāntakaḥ  Ramkāmaṃ bahv api vaktavyaṃ tvayi vakṣyāmi na tv ahamastaṃ gaccheddhi savitā yuddhavighnas tato bhavet  Ramcaturdaśa sahasrāṇi rākṣasānāṃ hatāni tetvadvināśāt karomy adya teṣām aśrupramārjanam  Ramity uktvā paramakruddhas tāṃ gadāṃ paramāṅgadaḥkharaś cikṣepa rāmāya pradīptām aśaniṃ yathā  Ramkharabāhupramuktā sā pradīptā mahatī gadābhasma vṛkṣāṃś ca gulmāṃś ca kṛtvāgāt tatsamīpataḥ  Ramtām āpatantīṃ jvalitāṃ mṛtyupāśopamāṃ gadāmantarikṣagatāṃ rāmaś cicheda bahudhā śaraiḥ  Ramsā viśīrṇā śarair bhinnā papāta dharaṇītalegadāmantrauṣadhibalair vyālīva vinipātitā  Rambhittvā tu tāṃ gadāṃ bāṇai rāghavo dharmavatsalaḥsmayamānaḥ kharaṃ vākyaṃ saṃrabdham idam abravīt  Rametat te balasarvasvaṃ darśitaṃ rākṣasādhamaśaktihīnataro matto vṛthā tvam avagarjasi  Rameṣā bāṇavinirbhinnā gadā bhūmitalaṃ gatāabhidhānapragalbhasya tava pratyayaghātinī  Ramyat tvayoktaṃ vinaṣṭānām idam aśrupramārjanamrākṣasānāṃ karomīti mithyā tad api te vacaḥ  Ramnīcasya kṣudraśīlasya mithyāvṛttasya rakṣasaḥprāṇān apahariṣyāmi garutmān amṛtaṃ yathā  Ramadya te bhinnakaṇṭhasya phenabudbudabhūṣitamvidāritasya madbāṇair mahī pāsyati śoṇitam  Rampāṃsurūṣitasarvāṅgaḥ srastanyastabhujadvayaḥsvapsyase gāṃ samāśliṣya durlabhāṃ pramadām iva  Rampravṛddhanidre śayite tvayi rākṣasapāṃsanebhaviṣyanty aśaraṇyānāṃ śaraṇyā daṇḍakā ime  Ramjanasthāne hatasthāne tava rākṣasa maccharaiḥnirbhayā vicariṣyanti sarvato munayo vane  Ramadya viprasariṣyanti rākṣasyo hatabāndhavāḥbāṣpārdravadanā dīnā bhayād anyabhayāvahāḥ  Ramadya śokarasajñās tā bhaviṣyanti niśācaraanurūpakulāḥ patnyo yāsāṃ tvaṃ patir īdṛśaḥ  Ramnṛśaṃsaśīla kṣudrātman nityaṃ brāhmaṇakaṇṭakatvatkṛte śaṅkitair agnau munibhiḥ pātyate haviḥ  Ramtam evam abhisaṃrabdhaṃ bruvāṇaṃ rāghavaṃ raṇekharo nirbhartsayāmāsa roṣāt kharatarasvanaḥ  Ramdṛḍhaṃ khalv avalipto si bhayeṣv api ca nirbhayaḥvācyāvācyaṃ tato hi tvaṃ mṛtyuvaśyo na budhyase  Ramkālapāśaparikṣiptā bhavanti puruṣā hi yekāryākāryaṃ na jānanti te nirastaṣaḍindriyāḥ  Ramevam uktvā tato rāmaṃ saṃrudhya bhrukuṭiṃ tataḥsa dadarśa mahāsālam avidūre niśācaraḥ  Ramraṇe praharaṇasyārthe sarvato hy avalokayansa tam utpāṭayāmāsa saṃdṛśya daśanacchadam  Ramtaṃ samutkṣipya bāhubhyāṃ vinarditvā mahābalaḥrāmam uddiśya cikṣepa hatas tvam iti cābravīt  Ramtam āpatantaṃ bāṇaughaiś chittvā rāmaḥ pratāpavānroṣam āhārayat tīvraṃ nihantuṃ samare kharam  Ramjātasvedas tato rāmo roṣād raktāntalocanaḥnirbibheda sahasreṇa bāṇānāṃ samare kharam  Ramtasya bāṇāntarād raktaṃ bahu susrāva phenilamgireḥ prasravaṇasyeva toyadhārāparisravaḥ  Ramvihvalaḥ sa kṛto bāṇaiḥ kharo rāmeṇa saṃyugematto rudhiragandhena tam evābhyadravad drutam  Ramtam āpatantaṃ saṃrabdhaṃ kṛtāstro rudhirāplutamapāsarpat pratipadaṃ kiṃcit tvaritavikramaḥ  Ramtataḥ pāvakasaṃkāśaṃ vadhāya samare śaramkharasya rāmo jagrāha brahmadaṇḍam ivāparam  Ramsa tad dattaṃ maghavatā surarājena dhīmatāsaṃdadhe ca sa dharmātmā mumoca ca kharaṃ prati  Ramsa vimukto mahābāṇo nirghātasamaniḥsvanaḥrāmeṇa dhanur udyamya kharasyorasi cāpatat  Ramsa papāta kharo bhūmau dahyamānaḥ śarāgninārudreṇaiva vinirdagdhaḥ śvetāraṇye yathāndhakaḥ  Ramsa vṛtra iva vajreṇa phenena namucir yathābalo vendrāśanihato nipapāta hataḥ kharaḥ  Ramtato rājarṣayaḥ sarve saṃgatāḥ paramarṣayaḥsabhājya muditā rāmam idaṃ vacanam abruvan  Rametadarthaṃ mahātejā mahendraḥ pākaśāsanaḥśarabhaṅgāśramaṃ puṇyam ājagāma puraṃdaraḥ  Ramānītas tvam imaṃ deśam upāyena maharṣibhiḥeṣāṃ vadhārthaṃ krūrāṇāṃ rakṣasāṃ pāpakarmaṇām  Ramtad idaṃ naḥ kṛtaṃ kāryaṃ tvayā daśarathātmajasukhaṃ dharmaṃ cariṣyanti daṇḍakeṣu maharṣayaḥ  Rametasminn antare vīro lakṣmaṇaḥ saha sītayāgiridurgād viniṣkramya saṃviveśāśramaṃ sukhī  Ramtato rāmas tu vijayī pūjyamāno maharṣibhiḥpraviveśāśramaṃ vīro lakṣmaṇenābhivāditaḥ  Ramtaṃ dṛṣṭvā śatruhantāraṃ maharṣīṇāṃ sukhāvahambabhūva hṛṣṭā vaidehī bhartāraṃ pariṣasvaje  Ramtataḥ śūrpaṇakhā dṛṣṭvā sahasrāṇi caturdaśahatāny ekena rāmeṇa rakṣasāṃ bhīmakarmaṇām  Ramdūṣaṇaṃ ca kharaṃ caiva hataṃ triśirasaṃ raṇedṛṣṭvā punar mahānādaṃ nanāda jaladopamā  Ramsā dṛṣṭvā karma rāmasya kṛtam anyaiḥ suduṣkaramjagāma paramodvignā laṅkāṃ rāvaṇapālitām  Ramsā dadarśa vimānāgre rāvaṇaṃ dīptatejasamupopaviṣṭaṃ sacivair marudbhir iva vāsavam  Ramāsīnaṃ sūryasaṃkāśe kāñcane paramāsanerukmavedigataṃ prājyaṃ jvalantam iva pāvakam  Ramdevagandharvabhūtānām ṛṣīṇāṃ ca mahātmanāmajeyaṃ samare śūraṃ vyāttānanam ivāntakam  Ramdevāsuravimardeṣu vajrāśanikṛtavraṇamairāvataviṣāṇāgrair utkṛṣṭakiṇavakṣasam  Ramviṃśadbhujaṃ daśagrīvaṃ darśanīyaparicchadamviśālavakṣasaṃ vīraṃ rājalakṣmaṇalakṣitam  Ramsnigdhavaiḍūryasaṃkāśaṃ taptakāñcanakuṇḍalamsubhujaṃ śukladaśanaṃ mahāsyaṃ parvatopamam  Ramviṣṇucakranipātaiś ca śataśo devasaṃyugeāhatāṅgaṃ samastaiś ca devapraharaṇais tathā  Ramakṣobhyāṇāṃ samudrāṇāṃ kṣobhaṇaṃ kṣiprakāriṇamkṣeptāraṃ parvatāgrāṇāṃ surāṇāṃ ca pramardanam  Ramucchettāraṃ ca dharmāṇāṃ paradārābhimarśanamsarvadivyāstrayoktāraṃ yajñavighnakaraṃ sadā  Rampurīṃ bhogavatīṃ gatvā parājitya ca vāsukimtakṣakasya priyāṃ bhāryāṃ parājitya jahāra yaḥ  Ramkailāsaṃ parvataṃ gatvā vijitya naravāhanamvimānaṃ puṣpakaṃ tasya kāmagaṃ vai jahāra yaḥ  Ramvanaṃ caitrarathaṃ divyaṃ nalinīṃ nandanaṃ vanamvināśayati yaḥ krodhād devodyānāni vīryavān  Ramcandrasūryau mahābhāgāv uttiṣṭhantau paraṃtapaunivārayati bāhubhyāṃ yaḥ śailaśikharopamaḥ  Ramdaśavarṣasahasrāṇi tapas taptvā mahāvanepurā svayambhuve dhīraḥ śirāṃsy upajahāra yaḥ  Ramdevadānavagandharvapiśācapatagoragaiḥabhayaṃ yasya saṃgrāme mṛtyuto mānuṣād ṛte  Rammantrair abhiṣutaṃ puṇyam adhvareṣu dvijātibhiḥhavirdhāneṣu yaḥ somam upahanti mahābalaḥ  Ramāptayajñaharaṃ krūraṃ brahmaghnaṃ duṣṭacāriṇamkarkaśaṃ niranukrośaṃ prajānām ahite ratamrāvaṇaṃ sarvabhūtānāṃ sarvalokabhayāvaham  Ramrākṣasī bhrātaraṃ krūraṃ sā dadarśa mahābalamtaṃ divyavastrābharaṇaṃ divyamālyopaśobhitamrākṣasendraṃ mahābhāgaṃ paulastyakulanandanam  Ramtam abravīd dīptaviśālalocanaṃ pradarśayitvā bhayamohamūrchitāsudāruṇaṃ vākyam abhītacāriṇī mahātmanā śūrpaṇakhā virūpitā  Ramtataḥ śūrpaṇakhā dīnā rāvaṇaṃ lokarāvaṇamamātyamadhye saṃkruddhā paruṣaṃ vākyam abravīt  Rampramattaḥ kāmabhogeṣu svairavṛtto niraṅkuśaḥsamutpannaṃ bhayaṃ ghoraṃ boddhavyaṃ nāvabudhyase  Ramsaktaṃ grāmyeṣu bhogeṣu kāmavṛttaṃ mahīpatimlubdhaṃ na bahu manyante śmaśānāgnim iva prajāḥ  Ramsvayaṃ kāryāṇi yaḥ kāle nānutiṣṭhati pārthivaḥsa tu vai saha rājyena taiś ca kāryair vinaśyati  Ramayuktacāraṃ durdarśam asvādhīnaṃ narādhipamvarjayanti narā dūrān nadīpaṅkam iva dvipāḥ  Ramye na rakṣanti viṣayam asvādhīnā narādhipāḥte na vṛddhyā prakāśante girayaḥ sāgare yathā  Ramātmavadbhir vigṛhya tvaṃ devagandharvadānavaiḥayuktacāraś capalaḥ kathaṃ rājā bhaviṣyasi  Ramyeṣāṃ cāraś ca kośaś ca nayaś ca jayatāṃ varaasvādhīnā narendrāṇāṃ prākṛtais te janaiḥ samāḥ  Ramyasmāt paśyanti dūrasthān sarvān arthān narādhipāḥcāreṇa tasmād ucyante rājāno dīrghacakṣuṣaḥ  Ramayuktacāraṃ manye tvāṃ prākṛtaiḥ sacivair vṛtamsvajanaṃ ca janasthānaṃ hataṃ yo nāvabudhyase  Ramcaturdaśa sahasrāṇi rakṣasāṃ bhīmakarmaṇāmhatāny ekena rāmeṇa kharaś ca sahadūṣaṇaḥ  Ramṛṣīṇām abhayaṃ dattaṃ kṛtakṣemāś ca daṇḍakāḥdharṣitaṃ ca janasthānaṃ rāmeṇākliṣṭakarmaṇā  Ramtvaṃ tu lubdhaḥ pramattaś ca parādhīnaś ca rāvaṇaviṣaye sve samutpannaṃ bhayaṃ yo nāvabudhyase  Ramtīkṣṇam alpapradātāraṃ pramattaṃ garvitaṃ śaṭhamvyasane sarvabhūtāni nābhidhāvanti pārthivam  Ramatimāninam agrāhyam ātmasaṃbhāvitaṃ naramkrodhanaṃ vyasane hanti svajano pi narādhipam  Ramnānutiṣṭhati kāryāṇi bhayeṣu na bibheti cakṣipraṃ rājyāc cyuto dīnas tṛṇais tulyo bhaviṣyati  Ramśuṣkakāṣṭhair bhavet kāryaṃ loṣṭair api ca pāṃsubhiḥna tu sthānāt paribhraṣṭaiḥ kāryaṃ syād vasudhādhipaiḥ  Ramupabhuktaṃ yathā vāsaḥ srajo vā mṛditā yathāevaṃ rājyāt paribhraṣṭaḥ samartho pi nirarthakaḥ  Ramapramattaś ca yo rājā sarvajño vijitendriyaḥkṛtajño dharmaśīlaś ca sa rājā tiṣṭhate ciram  Ramnayanābhyāṃ prasupto pi jāgarti nayacakṣuṣāvyaktakrodhaprasādaś ca sa rājā pūjyate janaiḥ  Ramtvaṃ tu rāvaṇa durbuddhir guṇair etair vivarjitaḥyasya te viditaś cārai rakṣasāṃ sumahān vadhaḥ  Ramparāvamantā viṣayeṣu saṃgato na deśakālapravibhāgatattvavitayuktabuddhir guṇadoṣaniścaye vipannarājyo na cirād vipatsyate  Ramiti svadoṣān parikīrtitāṃs tayā samīkṣya buddhyā kṣaṇadācareśvaraḥdhanena darpeṇa balena cānvito vicintayāmāsa ciraṃ sa rāvaṇaḥ  Ramtataḥ śūrpaṇakhāṃ kruddhāṃ bruvatīṃ paruṣaṃ vacaḥamātyamadhye saṃkruddhaḥ paripapraccha rāvaṇaḥ  Ramkaś ca rāmaḥ kathaṃvīryaḥ kiṃrūpaḥ kiṃparākramaḥkimarthaṃ daṇḍakāraṇyaṃ praviṣṭaś ca suduścaram  Ramāyudhaṃ kiṃ ca rāmasya nihatā yena rākṣasāḥkharaś ca nihataḥ saṃkhye dūṣaṇas triśirās tathā  Ramity uktā rākṣasendreṇa rākṣasī krodhamūrchitātato rāmaṃ yathānyāyam ākhyātum upacakrame  Ramdīrghabāhur viśālākṣaś cīrakṛṣṇājināmbaraḥkandarpasamarūpaś ca rāmo daśarathātmajaḥ  Ramśakracāpanibhaṃ cāpaṃ vikṛṣya kanakāṅgadamdīptān kṣipati nārācān sarpān iva mahāviṣān  Ramnādadānaṃ śarān ghorān na muñcantaṃ mahābalamna kārmukaṃ vikarṣantaṃ rāmaṃ paśyāmi saṃyuge  Ramhanyamānaṃ tu tat sainyaṃ paśyāmi śaravṛṣṭibhiḥindreṇevottamaṃ sasyam āhataṃ tv aśmavṛṣṭibhiḥ  Ramrakṣasāṃ bhīmavīryāṇāṃ sahasrāṇi caturdaśanihatāni śarais tīkṣṇais tenaikena padātinā  Ramardhādhikamuhūrtena kharaś ca sahadūṣaṇaḥṛṣīṇām abhayaṃ dattaṃ kṛtakṣemāś ca daṇḍakāḥ  Ramekā kathaṃcin muktāhaṃ paribhūya mahātmanāstrīvadhaṃ śaṅkamānena rāmeṇa viditātmanā  Rambhrātā cāsya mahātejā guṇatas tulyavikramaḥanuraktaś ca bhaktaś ca lakṣmaṇo nāma vīryavān  Ramamarṣī durjayo jetā vikrānto buddhimān balīrāmasya dakṣiṇo bāhur nityaṃ prāṇo bahiścaraḥ  Ramrāmasya tu viśālākṣī dharmapatnī yaśasvinīsītā nāma varārohā vaidehī tanumadhyamā  Ramnaiva devī na gandharvī na yakṣī na ca kiṃnarītathārūpā mayā nārī dṛṣṭapūrvā mahītale  Ramyasya sītā bhaved bhāryā yaṃ ca hṛṣṭā pariṣvajetatijīvet sa sarveṣu lokeṣv api puraṃdarāt  Ramsā suśīlā vapuḥślāghyā rūpeṇāpratimā bhuvitavānurūpā bhāryā sā tvaṃ ca tasyās tathā patiḥ  Ramtāṃ tu vistīrṇajaghanāṃ pīnottuṅgapayodharāmbhāryārthe tu tavānetum udyatāhaṃ varānanām  Ramtāṃ tu dṛṣṭvādya vaidehīṃ pūrṇacandranibhānanāmmanmathasya śarāṇāṃ ca tvaṃ vidheyo bhaviṣyasi  Ramyadi tasyām abhiprāyo bhāryārthe tava jāyateśīghram uddhriyatāṃ pādo jayārtham iha dakṣiṇaḥ  Ramkuru priyaṃ tathā teṣāṃ rakṣasāṃ rākṣaseśvaravadhāt tasya nṛśaṃsasya rāmasyāśramavāsinaḥ  Ramtaṃ śarair niśitair hatvā lakṣmaṇaṃ ca mahārathamhatanāthāṃ sukhaṃ sītāṃ yathāvad upabhokṣyase  Ramrocate yadi te vākyaṃ mamaitad rākṣaseśvarakriyatāṃ nirviśaṅkena vacanaṃ mama rāghava  Ramniśamya rāmeṇa śarair ajihmagair hatāñ janasthānagatān niśācarānkharaṃ ca buddhvā nihataṃ ca dūṣaṇaṃ tvam adya kṛtyaṃ pratipattum arhasi  Ramtataḥ śūrpaṇakhāvākyaṃ tac chrutvā romaharṣaṇamsacivān abhyanujñāya kāryaṃ buddhvā jagāma ha  Ramtat kāryam anugamyātha yathāvad upalabhya cadoṣāṇāṃ ca guṇānāṃ ca sampradhārya balābalam  Ramiti kartavyam ity eva kṛtvā niścayam ātmanaḥsthirabuddhis tato ramyāṃ yānaśālāṃ jagāma ha  Ramyānaśālāṃ tato gatvā pracchanno rākṣasādhipaḥsūtaṃ saṃcodayāmāsa rathaḥ saṃyujyatām iti  Ramevam uktaḥ kṣaṇenaiva sārathir laghuvikramaḥrathaṃ saṃyojayāmāsa tasyābhimatam uttamam  Ramkāñcanaṃ ratham āsthāya kāmagaṃ ratnabhūṣitampiśācavadanair yuktaṃ kharaiḥ kanakabhūṣaṇaiḥ  Rammeghapratimanādena sa tena dhanadānujaḥrākṣasādhipatiḥ śrīmān yayau nadanadīpatim  Ramsa śvetavālavyasanaḥ śvetacchattro daśānanaḥsnigdhavaiḍūryasaṃkāśas taptakāñcanabhūṣaṇaḥ  Ramdaśāsyo viṃśatibhujo darśanīyaparicchadaḥtridaśārir munīndraghno daśaśīrṣa ivādrirāṭ  Ramkāmagaṃ ratham āsthāya śuśubhe rākṣasādhipaḥvidyunmaṇḍalavān meghaḥ sabalāka ivāmbare  Ramsaśailaṃ sāgarānūpaṃ vīryavān avalokayannānāpuṣpaphalair vṛkṣair anukīrṇaṃ sahasraśaḥ  Ramśītamaṅgalatoyābhiḥ padminībhiḥ samantataḥviśālair āśramapadair vedimadbhiḥ samāvṛtam  Ramkadalyāḍhakīsambādhaṃ nālikeropaśobhitamsālais tālais tamālaiś ca tarubhiś ca supuṣpitaiḥ  Ramatyantaniyatāhāraiḥ śobhitaṃ paramarṣibhiḥnāgaiḥ suparṇair gandharvaiḥ kiṃnaraiś ca sahasraśaḥ  Ramjitakāmaiś ca siddhaiś ca cāraṇaiś copaśobhitamājair vaikhānasair māṣair vālakhilyair marīcipaiḥ  Ramdivyābharaṇamālyābhir divyarūpābhir āvṛtamkrīḍāratividhijñābhir apsarobhiḥ sahasraśaḥ  Ramsevitaṃ devapatnībhiḥ śrīmatībhiḥ śriyā vṛtamdevadānavasaṃghaiś ca caritaṃ tv amṛtāśibhiḥ  Ramhaṃsakrauñcaplavākīrṇaṃ sārasaiḥ saṃpraṇāditamvaiḍūryaprastaraṃ ramyaṃ snigdhaṃ sāgaratejasā  Rampāṇḍurāṇi viśālāni divyamālyayutāni catūryagītābhijuṣṭāni vimānāni samantataḥ  Ramtapasā jitalokānāṃ kāmagāny abhisaṃpatangandharvāpsarasaś caiva dadarśa dhanadānujaḥ  Ramniryāsarasamūlānāṃ candanānāṃ sahasraśaḥvanāni paśyan saumyāni ghrāṇatṛptikarāṇi ca  Ramagarūṇāṃ ca mukhyānāṃ vanāny upavanāni catakkolānāṃ ca jātyānāṃ phalānāṃ ca sugandhinām  Rampuṣpāṇi ca tamālasya gulmāni maricasya camuktānāṃ ca samūhāni śuṣyamāṇāni tīrataḥ  Ramśaṅkhānāṃ prastaraṃ caiva pravālanicayaṃ tathākāñcanāni ca śailāni rājatāni ca sarvaśaḥ  Ramprasravāṇi manojñāni prasannāni hradāni cadhanadhānyopapannāni strīratnair āvṛtāni ca  Ramhastyaśvarathagāḍhāni nagarāṇy avalokayantaṃ samaṃ sarvataḥ snigdhaṃ mṛdusaṃsparśamārutam  Ramanūpaṃ sindhurājasya dadarśa tridivopamamtatrāpaśyat sa meghābhaṃ nyagrodham ṛṣibhir vṛtam  Ramsamantād yasya tāḥ śākhāḥ śatayojanam āyatāḥyasya hastinam ādāya mahākāyaṃ ca kacchapambhakṣārthaṃ garuḍaḥ śākhām ājagāma mahābalaḥ  Ramtasya tāṃ sahasā śākhāṃ bhāreṇa patagottamaḥsuparṇaḥ parṇabahulāṃ babhañjātha mahābalaḥ  Ramtatra vaikhānasā māṣā vālakhilyā marīcipāḥajā babhūvur dhūmrāś ca saṃgatāḥ paramarṣayaḥ  Ramteṣāṃ dayārthaṃ garuḍas tāṃ śākhāṃ śatayojanāmjagāmādāya vegena tau cobhau gajakacchapau  Ramekapādena dharmātmā bhakṣayitvā tad āmiṣamniṣādaviṣayaṃ hatvā śākhayā patagottamaḥpraharṣam atulaṃ lebhe mokṣayitvā mahāmunīn  Ramsa tenaiva praharṣeṇa dviguṇīkṛtavikramaḥamṛtānayanārthaṃ vai cakāra matimān matim  Ramayojālāni nirmathya bhittvā ratnagṛhaṃ varammahendrabhavanād guptam ājahārāmṛtaṃ tataḥ  Ramtaṃ maharṣigaṇair juṣṭaṃ suparṇakṛtalakṣaṇamnāmnā subhadraṃ nyagrodhaṃ dadarśa dhanadānujaḥ  Ramtaṃ tu gatvā paraṃ pāraṃ samudrasya nadīpateḥdadarśāśramam ekānte puṇye ramye vanāntare  Ramtatra kṛṣṇājinadharaṃ jaṭāvalkaladhāriṇamdadarśa niyatāhāraṃ mārīcaṃ nāma rākṣasam  Ramsa rāvaṇaḥ samāgamya vidhivat tena rakṣasātataḥ paścād idaṃ vākyam abravīd vākyakovidaḥ  Rammārīca śrūyatāṃ tāta vacanaṃ mama bhāṣataḥārto smi mama cārtasya bhavān hi paramā gatiḥ  Ramjānīṣe tvaṃ janasthānaṃ bhrātā yatra kharo mamadūṣaṇaś ca mahābāhuḥ svasā śūrpaṇakhā ca me  Ramtriśirāś ca mahātejā rākṣasaḥ piśitāśanaḥanye ca bahavaḥ śūrā labdhalakṣā niśācarāḥ  Ramvasanti manniyogena adhivāsaṃ ca rākṣasaḥbādhamānā mahāraṇye munīn ye dharmacāriṇaḥ  Ramcaturdaśa sahasrāṇi rakṣasāṃ bhīmakarmaṇāmśūrāṇāṃ labdhalakṣāṇāṃ kharacittānuvartinām  Ramte tv idānīṃ janasthāne vasamānā mahābalāḥsaṃgatāḥ param āyattā rāmeṇa saha saṃyuge  Ramtena saṃjātaroṣeṇa rāmeṇa raṇamūrdhanianuktvā paruṣaṃ kiṃcic charair vyāpāritaṃ dhanuḥ  Ramcaturdaśa sahasrāṇi rakṣasāṃ bhīmakarmaṇāmnihatāni śarais tīkṣṇair mānuṣeṇa padātinā  Ramkharaś ca nihataḥ saṃkhye dūṣaṇaś ca nipātitaḥhatvā triśirasaṃ cāpi nirbhayā daṇḍakāḥ kṛtāḥ  Rampitrā nirastaḥ kruddhena sabhāryaḥ kṣīṇajīvitaḥsa hantā tasya sainyasya rāmaḥ kṣatriyapāṃsanaḥ  Ramaśīlaḥ karkaśas tīkṣṇo mūrkho lubdho jitendriyaḥtyaktadharmas tv adharmātmā bhūtānām ahite rataḥ  Ramyena vairaṃ vināraṇye sattvam āśritya kevalamkarṇanāsāpahāreṇa bhaginī me virūpitā  Ramtasya bhāryāṃ janasthānāt sītāṃ surasutopamāmānayiṣyāmi vikramya sahāyas tatra me bhava  Ramtvayā hy ahaṃ sahāyena pārśvasthena mahābalabhrātṛbhiś ca surān yuddhe samagrān nābhicintaye  Ramtat sahāyo bhava tvaṃ me samartho hy asi rākṣasavīrye yuddhe ca darpe ca na hy asti sadṛśas tava  Rametadartham ahaṃ prāptas tvatsamīpaṃ niśācaraśṛṇu tat karma sāhāyye yat kāryaṃ vacanān mama  Ramsauvarṇas tvaṃ mṛgo bhūtvā citro rajatabindubhiḥāśrame tasya rāmasya sītāyāḥ pramukhe cara  Ramtvāṃ tu niḥsaṃśayaṃ sītā dṛṣṭvā tu mṛgarūpiṇamgṛhyatām iti bhartāraṃ lakṣmaṇaṃ cābhidhāsyati  Ramtatas tayor apāye tu śūnye sītāṃ yathāsukhamnirābādho hariṣyāmi rāhuś candraprabhām iva  Ramtataḥ paścāt sukhaṃ rāme bhāryāharaṇakarśiteviśrabdhaḥ prahariṣyāmi kṛtārthenāntarātmanā  Ramtasya rāmakathāṃ śrutvā mārīcasya mahātmanaḥśuṣkaṃ samabhavad vaktraṃ paritrasto babhūva ca  Ramsa rāvaṇaṃ trastaviṣaṇṇacetā mahāvane rāmaparākramajñaḥkṛtāñjalis tattvam uvāca vākyaṃ hitaṃ ca tasmai hitam ātmanaś ca  Ramtac chrutvā rākṣasendrasya vākyaṃ vākyaviśāradaḥpratyuvāca mahāprājño mārīco rākṣaseśvaram  Ramsulabhāḥ puruṣā rājan satataṃ priyavādinaḥapriyasya ca pathyasya vaktā śrotā ca durlabhaḥ  Ramna nūnaṃ budhyase rāmaṃ mahāvīryaṃ guṇonnatamayuktacāraś capalo mahendravaruṇopamam  Ramapi svasti bhavet tāta sarveṣāṃ bhuvi rakṣasāmapi rāmo na saṃkruddhaḥ kuryāl lokam arākṣasam  Ramapi te jīvitāntāya notpannā janakātmajāapi sītā nimittaṃ ca na bhaved vyasanaṃ mahat  Ramapi tvām īśvaraṃ prāpya kāmavṛttaṃ niraṅkuśamna vinaśyet purī laṅkā tvayā saha sarākṣasā  Ramtvadvidhaḥ kāmavṛtto hi duḥśīlaḥ pāpamantritaḥātmānaṃ svajanaṃ rāṣṭraṃ sa rājā hanti durmatiḥ  Ramna ca pitrā parityakto nāmaryādaḥ kathaṃcanana lubdho na ca duḥśīlo na ca kṣatriyapāṃsanaḥ  Ramna ca dharmaguṇair hīnaḥ kausalyānandavardhanaḥna ca tīkṣṇo hi bhūtānāṃ sarveṣāṃ ca hite rataḥ  Ramvañcitaṃ pitaraṃ dṛṣṭvā kaikeyyā satyavādinamkariṣyāmīti dharmātmā tataḥ pravrajito vanam  Ramkaikeyyāḥ priyakāmārthaṃ pitur daśarathasya cahitvā rājyaṃ ca bhogāṃś ca praviṣṭo daṇḍakāvanam  Ramna rāmaḥ karkaśas tāta nāvidvān nājitendriyaḥanṛtaṃ na śrutaṃ caiva naiva tvaṃ vaktum arhasi  Ramrāmo vigrahavān dharmaḥ sādhuḥ satyaparākramaḥrājā sarvasya lokasya devānām iva vāsavaḥ  Ramkathaṃ tvaṃ tasya vaidehīṃ rakṣitāṃ svena tejasāicchasi prasabhaṃ hartuṃ prabhām iva vivasvataḥ  Ramśarārciṣam anādhṛṣyaṃ cāpakhaḍgendhanaṃ raṇerāmāgniṃ sahasā dīptaṃ na praveṣṭuṃ tvam arhasi  Ramdhanurvyāditadīptāsyaṃ śarārciṣam amarṣaṇamcāpabāṇadharaṃ vīraṃ śatrusenāpahāriṇam  Ramrājyaṃ sukhaṃ ca saṃtyajya jīvitaṃ ceṣṭam Ramviśvāmitro tha dharmātmā madvitrasto mahāmuniḥsvayaṃ gatvā daśarathaṃ narendram idam abravīt  Ramayaṃ rakṣatu māṃ rāmaḥ parvakāle samāhitaḥmārīcān me bhayaṃ ghoraṃ samutpannaṃ nareśvara  Ramity evam ukto dharmātmā rājā daśarathas tadāpratyuvāca mahābhāgaṃ viśvāmitraṃ mahāmunim  Ramūnaṣoḍaśavarṣo yam akṛtāstraś ca rāghavaḥkāmaṃ tu mama yat sainyaṃ mayā saha gamiṣyativadhiṣyāmi muniśreṣṭha śatruṃ tava yathepsitam  Ramity evam uktaḥ sa munī rājānaṃ punar abravītrāmān nānyad balaṃ loke paryāptaṃ tasya rakṣasaḥ  Rambālo py eṣa mahātejāḥ samarthas tasya nigrahegamiṣye rāmam ādāya svasti te meghasaṃkāśas taptakāñcanakuṇḍalaḥbalī dattavaro darpād ājagāma tadāśramam  Ramtena dṛṣṭaḥ praviṣṭo haṃ sahasaivodyatāyudhaḥmāṃ tu dṛṣṭvā dhanuḥ sajyam asambhrāntaś cakāra ha  Ramavajānann ahaṃ mohād bhrāntacetanaḥpātito haṃ tadā tena gambhīre sāgarāmbhasiprāpya saṃjñāṃ cirāt tāta laṅkāṃ prati gataḥ purīm  Ramevam asmi tadā muktaḥ sahāyās te nipātitāḥakṛtāstreṇa rāmeṇa bālenākliṣṭakarmaṇā  Ramtan mayā vāryamāṇas tvaṃ yadi rāmeṇa vigrahamkariṣyasy āpadaṃ ghorāṃ kṣipraṃ prāpya naśiṣyasi  Ramkrīḍāratividhijñānāṃ samājotsavaśālināmrakṣasāṃ caiva saṃtāpam anarthaṃ cāhariṣyasi  Ramharmyaprāsādasambādhāṃ nānāratnavibhūṣitāmdrakṣyasi tvaṃ purīṃ laṅkāṃ vinaṣṭāṃ maithilīkṛte  Ramakurvanto pi pāpāni śucayaḥ pāpasaṃśrayātparapāpair vinaśyanti matsyā nāgahrade yathā  Ramdivyacandanadigdhāṅgān divyābharaṇabhūṣitāndrakṣyasy abhihatān bhūmau tava doṣāt tu rākṣasān  Ramhṛtadārān sadārāṃś ca daśa vidravato diśaḥhataśeṣān aśaraṇān drakṣyasi tvaṃ niśācarān  Ramśarajālaparikṣiptām agnijvālāsamāvṛtāmpradagdhabhavanāṃ laṅkāṃ drakṣyasi tvam asaṃśayam  Rampramadānāṃ sahasrāṇi tava rājan parigrahaḥbhava svadāranirataḥ svakulaṃ rakṣa rākṣasa  Rammānaṃ vṛddhiṃ Ramnihatya daṇḍakāraṇye tāpasān dharmacāriṇaḥrudhirāṇi pibaṃs teṣāṃ tathā māṃsāni bhakṣayan  Ramṛṣimāṃsāśanaḥ krūras trāsayan vanagocarāntadā rudhiramatto haṃ vyacaraṃ daṇḍakāvanam  Ramtadāhaṃ purāsamutkrāntas tato muktas tāv ubhau rākṣasau hatau  Ramśareṇa mukto rāmasya kathaṃcit prāpya jīvitamiha pravrājito yuktas tāpaso haṃ samāhitaḥ  Ramvṛkṣe vṛkṣe hi paśyāmi svapnagataṃ rāmam udbhramāmi vicetanaḥ  Ramrakārādīni nāmāni rāmatrastasya rāvaṇaratnāni ca rathāś caiva trāsaṃ saṃjanayanti me  Ramahaṃ tasya prabhāvajño na yuddhaṃ tena te kṣamamraṇe rāmeṇa Ramsaṃpṛṣṭena tu vaktavyaṃ sacivena vipaścitāudyatāñjalinā rājño ya icched bhūtim ātmanaḥ  Ramvākyam apratikūlaṃ tu mṛdupūrvaṃ śubhaṃ hitamupacāreṇa yuktaṃ ca vaktavyo vasudhādhipaḥ  Ramsāvamardaṃ tu daṇḍaṃ prasannatām  Ramtasmāt sarvāsv avasthāsu mānyāḥ pūjyāś ca pārthivāḥtvaṃ tu dharmam avijñāya kevalaṃ moham āsthitaḥ  Ramabhyāgataṃ māṃ daurātmyāt paruṣaṃ vadasīdṛśamguṇadoṣau na pṛcchāmi kṣamaṃ Rametat kāryam avaśyaṃ me balād api kariṣyasirājño hi pratikūlastho na jātu sukham edhate  Ramāsādya taṃ jīvitasaṃśayas te mṛtyur dhruvo hy adya mayā virudhyaetad yathāvat parigṛhya buddhyā yad atra Ramkenedam upadiṣṭaṃ te kṣudreṇāhitavādināyas tvām icchati naśyantaṃ svakṛtena niśācara  Ramvadhyāḥ khalu na hanyante sacivās tava rāvaṇaye tvām utpatham ārūḍhaṃ na nigṛhṇanti sarvaśaḥ  Ramamātyaiḥ na rākṣasāḥ  Ramnivāryamāṇas tu mayā hitaiṣiṇā na mṛṣyase vākyam idaṃ niśācaraparetakalpā hi gatāyuṣo narā hitaṃ na gṛhṇanti suhṛdbhir īritam  Ramevam uktvā tu paruṣaṃ mārīco rāvaṇaṃ tataḥgacchāvety Ramtathaiva tatra paśyantau pattanāni vanāni cagirīṃś ca saritaḥ sarvā rāṣṭrāṇi nagarāṇi ca  Ramsametya daṇḍakāraṇyaṃ rāghavasyāśramaṃ tataḥdadarśa sahamarīco rāvaṇo rākṣasādhipaḥ  Ramavatīrya rathāt
