kasya kāñcanam  Ramchattraṃ śataśalākaṃ ca divyamālyopaśobhitambhagnadaṇḍam idaṃ kasya bhūmau saumya nipātitam  Ramkāñcanoraśchadāś ceme piśācavadanāḥ kharāḥbhīmarūpā mahākāyāḥ kasya vā nihatā raṇe  Ramdīptapāvakasaṃkāśo dyutimān samaradhvajaḥapaviddhaś ca bhagnaś ca kasya sāṃgrāmiko rathaḥ  Ramrathākṣamātrā viśikhās tapanīyavibhūṣaṇāḥkasyeme bhihatā bāṇāḥ prakīrṇā ghorakarmaṇaḥ  Ramvairaṃ śataguṇaṃ paśya mamedaṃ jīvitāntakamsughorahṛdayaiḥ saumya rākṣasaiḥ kāmarūpibhiḥ  Ramhṛtā mṛtā vā sītā hi bhakṣitā vā tapasvinīna dharmas trāyate sītāṃ hriyamāṇāṃ mahāvane  Rambhakṣitāyāṃ hi vaidehyāṃ hṛtāyām api lakṣmaṇake hi loke priyaṃ kartuṃ śaktāḥ saumya mameśvarāḥ  Ramkartāram api lokānāṃ śūraṃ karuṇavedinamajñānād avamanyeran sarvabhūtāni lakṣmaṇa  Rammṛduṃ lokahite yuktaṃ dāntaṃ karuṇavedinamnirvīrya iti manyante nūnaṃ māṃ tridaśeśvarāḥ  Rammāṃ prāpya hi guṇo doṣaḥ saṃvṛttaḥ paśya lakṣmaṇaadyaiva sarvabhūtānāṃ rakṣasām abhavāya casaṃhṛtyaiva śaśijyotsnāṃ mahān sūrya ivoditaḥ  Ramnaiva yakṣā na gandharvā na piśācā na rākṣasāḥkiṃnarā vā manuṣyā vā sukhaṃ prāpsyanti lakṣmaṇa  Rammamāstrabāṇasampūrṇam ākāśaṃ paśya lakṣmaṇaniḥsampātaṃ kariṣyāmi hy adya trailokyacāriṇām  Ramsaṃniruddhagrahagaṇam āvāritaniśākaramvipranaṣṭānalamarudbhāskaradyutisaṃvṛtam  Ramvinirmathitaśailāgraṃ śuṣyamāṇajalāśayamdhvastadrumalatāgulmaṃ vipraṇāśitasāgaram  Ramna tāṃ kuśalinīṃ sītāṃ pradāsyanti mameśvarāḥasmin muhūrte saumitre mama drakṣyanti vikramam  Ramnākāśam utpatiṣyanti sarvabhūtāni lakṣmaṇamama cāpaguṇān muktair bāṇajālair nirantaram  Ramarditaṃ mama nārācair dhvastabhrāntamṛgadvijamsamākulam amaryādaṃ jagat paśyādya lakṣmaṇa  Ramākarṇapūrṇair iṣubhir jīvalokaṃ durāvaraiḥkariṣye maithilīhetor apiśācam arākṣasam  Rammama roṣaprayuktānāṃ sāyakānāṃ balaṃ surāḥdrakṣyanty adya vimuktānām amarṣād dūragāminām  Ramnaiva devā na daiteyā na piśācā na rākṣasāḥbhaviṣyanti mama krodhāt trailokye vipraṇāśite  Ramdevadānavayakṣāṇāṃ lokā ye rakṣasām apibahudhā nipatiṣyanti bāṇaughaiḥ śakulīkṛtāḥnirmaryādān imāṃl lokān kariṣyāmy adya sāyakaiḥ  Ramyathā jarā yathā mṛtyur yathā kālo yathā vidhiḥnityaṃ na pratihanyante sarvabhūteṣu lakṣmaṇatathāhaṃ krodhasaṃyukto na nivāryo smy asaṃśayam  Rampureva me cārudatīm aninditāṃ diśanti sītāṃ yadi nādya maithilīmsadevagandharvamanuṣyapannagaṃ jagat saśailaṃ parivartayāmy aham  Ramtapyamānaṃ tathā rāmaṃ sītāharaṇakarśitamlokānām abhave yuktaṃ saṃvartakam ivānalam  Ramvīkṣamāṇaṃ dhanuḥ sajyaṃ niḥśvasantaṃ muhur muhuḥhantukāmaṃ paśuṃ rudraṃ kruddhaṃ dakṣakratau yathā  Ramadṛṣṭapūrvaṃ saṃkruddhaṃ dṛṣṭvā rāmaṃ sa lakṣmaṇaḥabravīt prāñjalir vākyaṃ mukhena pariśuṣyatā  Rampurā bhūtvā mṛdur dāntaḥ sarvabhūtahite rataḥna krodhavaśam āpannaḥ prakṛtiṃ hātum arhasi  Ramcandre lakṣmīḥ prabhā sūrye gatir vāyau bhuvi kṣamāetac ca niyataṃ sarvaṃ tvayi cānuttamaṃ yaśaḥ  Ramna tu jānāmi kasyāyaṃ bhagnaḥ sāṃgrāmiko rathaḥkena vā kasya vā hetoḥ sāyudhaḥ saparicchadaḥ  Ramkhuranemikṣataś cāyaṃ sikto rudhirabindubhiḥdeśo nivṛttasaṃgrāmaḥ sughoraḥ pārthivātmaja  Ramekasya tu vimardo yaṃ na dvayor vadatāṃ varana hi vṛttaṃ hi paśyāmi balasya mahataḥ padam  Ramnaikasya tu kṛte lokān vināśayitum arhasiyuktadaṇḍā hi mṛdavaḥ praśāntā vasudhādhipāḥ  Ramsadā tvaṃ sarvabhūtānāṃ śaraṇyaḥ paramā gatiḥko nu dārapraṇāśaṃ te sādhu manyeta rāghava  Ramsaritaḥ sāgarāḥ śailā devagandharvadānavāḥnālaṃ te vipriyaṃ kartuṃ dīkṣitasyeva sādhavaḥ  Ramyena rājan hṛtā sītā tam anveṣitum arhasimaddvitīyo dhanuṣpāṇiḥ sahāyaiḥ paramarṣibhiḥ  Ramsamudraṃ ca viceṣyāmaḥ parvatāṃś ca vanāni caguhāś ca vividhā ghorā nalinīḥ pārvatīś ca ha  Ramdevagandharvalokāṃś ca viceṣyāmaḥ samāhitāḥyāvan nādhigamiṣyāmas tava bhāryāpahāriṇam  Ramna cet sāmnā pradāsyanti patnīṃ te tridaśeśvarāḥkosalendra tataḥ paścāt prāptakālaṃ kariṣyasi  Ramśīlena sāmnā vinayena sītāṃ nayena na prāpsyasi cen narendratataḥ samutsādaya hemapuṅkhair mahendravajrapratimaiḥ śaraughaiḥ  Ramtaṃ tathā śokasaṃtaptaṃ vilapantam anāthavatmohena mahatāviṣṭaṃ paridyūnam acetanam  Ramtataḥ saumitrir āśvāsya muhūrtād iva lakṣmaṇaḥrāmaṃ saṃbodhayāmāsa caraṇau cābhipīḍayan  Rammahatā tapasā rāma mahatā cāpi karmaṇārājñā daśarathenāsīl labdho mṛtam ivāmaraiḥ  Ramtava caiva guṇair baddhas tvadviyogān mahīpatiḥrājā devatvam āpanno bharatasya yathā śrutam  Ramyadi duḥkham idaṃ prāptaṃ kākutstha na sahiṣyaseprākṛtaś cālpasattvaś ca itaraḥ kaḥ sahiṣyati  Ramduḥkhito hi bhavāṃl lokāṃs tejasā yadi dhakṣyateārtāḥ prajā naravyāghra kva nu yāsyanti nirvṛtim  Ramlokasvabhāva evaiṣa yayātir nahuṣātmajaḥgataḥ śakreṇa sālokyam anayas taṃ samaspṛśat  Rammaharṣayo vasiṣṭhas tu yaḥ pitur naḥ purohitaḥahnā putraśataṃ jajñe tathaivāsya punar hatam  Ramyā ceyaṃ jagato mātā devī lokanamaskṛtāasyāś ca calanaṃ bhūmer dṛśyate satyasaṃśrava  Ramyau cemau jagatāṃ netre yatra sarvaṃ pratiṣṭhitamādityacandrau grahaṇam abhyupetau mahābalau  Ramsumahānty api bhūtāni devāś ca puruṣarṣabhana daivasya pramuñcanti sarvabhūtāni dehinaḥ  Ramśakrādiṣv api deveṣu vartamānau nayānayauśrūyete naraśārdūla na tvaṃ vyathitum arhasi  Ramnaṣṭāyām api vaidehyāṃ hṛtāyām api cānaghaśocituṃ nārhase vīra yathānyaḥ prākṛtas tathā  Ramtvadvidhā hi na śocanti satataṃ satyadarśinaḥsumahatsv api kṛcchreṣu rāmānirviṇṇadarśanāḥ  Ramtattvato hi naraśreṣṭha buddhyā samanucintayabuddhyā yuktā mahāprājñā vijānanti śubhāśubhe  Ramadṛṣṭaguṇadoṣāṇām adhṛtānāṃ ca karmaṇāmnāntareṇa kriyāṃ teṣāṃ phalam iṣṭaṃ pravartate  Rammām eva hi purā vīra tvam eva bahuśo nvaśāḥanuśiṣyāddhi ko nu tvām api sākṣād bṛhaspatiḥ  Rambuddhiś ca te mahāprājña devair api duranvayāśokenābhiprasuptaṃ te jñānaṃ saṃbodhayāmy aham  Ramdivyaṃ ca mānuṣaṃ caivam ātmanaś ca parākramamikṣvākuvṛṣabhāvekṣya yatasva dviṣatāṃ vadhe  Ramkiṃ te sarvavināśena kṛtena puruṣarṣabhatam eva tu ripuṃ pāpaṃ vijñāyoddhartum arhasi  Rampūrvajo py uktamātras tu lakṣmaṇena subhāṣitamsāragrāhī mahāsāraṃ pratijagrāha rāghavaḥ  Ramsaṃnigṛhya mahābāhuḥ pravṛddhaṃ kopam ātmanaḥavaṣṭabhya dhanuś citraṃ rāmo lakṣmaṇam abravīt  Ramkiṃ kariṣyāvahe vatsa kva vā gacchāva lakṣmaṇakenopāyena paśyeyaṃ sītām iti vicintaya  Ramtaṃ tathā paritāpārtaṃ lakṣmaṇo rāmam abravītidam eva janasthānaṃ tvam anveṣitum arhasi  Ramrākṣasair bahubhiḥ kīrṇaṃ nānādrumalatāyutamsantīha giridurgāṇi nirdarāḥ kandarāṇi ca  Ramguhāś ca vividhā ghorā nānāmṛgagaṇākulāḥāvāsāḥ kiṃnarāṇāṃ ca gandharvabhavanāni ca  Ramtāni yukto mayā sārdhaṃ tvam anveṣitum arhasitvadvidhā buddhisampannā mahātmāno nararṣabha  Ramāpatsu na prakampante vāyuvegair ivācalāḥity uktas tad vanaṃ sarvaṃ vicacāra salakṣmaṇaḥ  Ramkruddho rāmaḥ śaraṃ ghoraṃ saṃdhāya dhanuṣi kṣuramtataḥ parvatakūṭābhaṃ mahābhāgaṃ dvijottamam  Ramdadarśa patitaṃ bhūmau kṣatajārdraṃ jaṭāyuṣamtaṃ dṛṣṭvā giriśṛṅgābhaṃ rāmo lakṣmaṇam abravītanena sītā vaidehī bhakṣitā nātra saṃśayaḥ  Ramgṛdhrarūpam idaṃ vyaktaṃ rakṣo bhramati kānanambhakṣayitvā viśālākṣīm āste sītāṃ yathāsukhamenaṃ vadhiṣye dīptāgrair ghorair bāṇair ajihmagaiḥ  Ramity uktvābhyapatad gṛdhraṃ saṃdhāya dhanuṣi kṣuramkruddho rāmaḥ samudrāntāṃ cālayann iva medinīm  Ramtaṃ dīnadīnayā vācā saphenaṃ rudhiraṃ vamanabhyabhāṣata pakṣī tu rāmaṃ daśarathātmajam  Ramyām oṣadhim ivāyuṣmann anveṣasi mahāvanesā devī mama ca prāṇā rāvaṇenobhayaṃ hṛtam  Ramtvayā virahitā devī lakṣmaṇena ca rāghavahriyamāṇā mayā dṛṣṭā rāvaṇena balīyasā  Ramsītām abhyavapanno haṃ rāvaṇaś ca raṇe mayāvidhvaṃsitarathacchattraḥ pātito dharaṇītale  Rametad asya dhanur bhagnam etad asya śarāvaramayam asya raṇe rāma bhagnaḥ sāṃgrāmiko rathaḥ  Rampariśrāntasya me pakṣau chittvā khaḍgena rāvaṇaḥsītām ādāya vaidehīm utpapāta vihāyasamrakṣasā nihataṃ pūrvaṃ na māṃ hantuṃ tvam arhasi  Ramrāmas tasya tu vijñāya sītāsaktāṃ priyāṃ kathāmgṛdhrarājaṃ pariṣvajya ruroda sahalakṣmaṇaḥ  Ramekam ekāyane durge niḥśvasantaṃ kathaṃcanasamīkṣya duḥkhito rāmaḥ saumitrim idam abravīt  Ramrājyād bhraṃśo vane vāsaḥ sītā naṣṭā hato dvijaḥīdṛśīyaṃ mamālakṣmīr nirdahed api pāvakam  Ramsampūrṇam api ced adya pratareyaṃ mahodadhimso pi nūnaṃ mamālakṣmyā viśuṣyet saritāṃ patiḥ  Ramnāsty abhāgyataro loke matto smin sacarācareyeneyaṃ mahatī prāptā mayā vyasanavāgurā  Ramayaṃ pitṛvayasyo me gṛdhrarājo jarānvitaḥśete vinihato bhūmau mama bhāgyaviparyayāt  Ramity evam uktvā bahuśo rāghavaḥ sahalakṣmaṇaḥjaṭāyuṣaṃ ca pasparśa pitṛsnehaṃ nidarśayan  Ramnikṛttapakṣaṃ rudhirāvasiktaṃ taṃ gṛdhrarājaṃ parirabhya rāmaḥkva maithili prāṇasamā mameti vimucya vācaṃ nipapāta bhūmau  Ramrāmaḥ prekṣya tu taṃ gṛdhraṃ bhuvi raudreṇa pātitamsaumitriṃ mitrasampannam idaṃ vacanam abravīt  Rammamāyaṃ nūnam artheṣu yatamāno vihaṃgamaḥrākṣasena hataḥ saṃkhye prāṇāṃs tyajati dustyajān  Ramayam asya śarīre smin prāṇo lakṣmaṇa vidyatetathā svaravihīno yaṃ viklavaṃ samudīkṣate  Ramjaṭāyo yadi śaknoṣi vākyaṃ vyāharituṃ punaḥsītām ākhyāhi bhadraṃ te vadham ākhyāhi cātmanaḥ  Ramkiṃnimitto harat sītāṃ rāvaṇas tasya kiṃ mayāaparāddhaṃ tu yaṃ dṛṣṭvā rāvaṇena hṛtā priyā  Ramkathaṃ tac candrasaṃkāśaṃ mukham āsīn manoharamsītayā kāni coktāni tasmin kāle dvijottama  Ramkathaṃvīryaḥ kathaṃrūpaḥ kiṃkarmā sa ca rākṣasaḥkva cāsya bhavanaṃ tāta brūhi me paripṛcchataḥ  Ramtam udvīkṣyātha dīnātmā vilapantam anantaramvācātisannayā rāmaṃ jaṭāyur idam abravīt  Ramsā hṛtā rākṣasendreṇa rāvaṇena vihāyasāmāyām āsthāya vipulāṃ vātadurdinasaṃkulām  Rampariśrāntasya me tāta pakṣau chittvā niśācaraḥsītām ādāya vaidehīṃ prayāto dakṣiṇāmukhaḥ  Ramuparudhyanti me prāṇā dṛṣṭir bhramati rāghavapaśyāmi vṛkṣān sauvarṇān uśīrakṛtamūrdhajān  Ramyena yāti muhūrtena sītām ādāya rāvaṇaḥvipraṇaṣṭaṃ dhanaṃ kṣipraṃ tatsvāmī pratipadyate  Ramvindo nāma muhūrto sau sa ca kākutstha nābudhatjhaṣavad baḍiśaṃ gṛhya kṣipram eva vinaśyati  Ramna ca tvayā vyathā kāryā janakasya sutāṃ prativaidehyā raṃsyase kṣipraṃ hatvā taṃ rākṣasaṃ raṇe  Ramasaṃmūḍhasya gṛdhrasya rāmaṃ pratyanubhāṣataḥāsyāt susrāva rudhiraṃ mriyamāṇasya sāmiṣam  Ramputro viśravasaḥ sākṣād bhrātā vaiśravaṇasya caity uktvā durlabhān prāṇān mumoca patageśvaraḥ  Rambrūhi brūhīti rāmasya bruvāṇasya kṛtāñjaleḥtyaktvā śarīraṃ gṛdhrasya jagmuḥ prāṇā vihāyasam  Ramsa nikṣipya śiro bhūmau prasārya caraṇau tadāvikṣipya ca śarīraṃ svaṃ papāta dharaṇītale  Ramtaṃ gṛdhraṃ prekṣya tāmrākṣaṃ gatāsum acalopamamrāmaḥ subahubhir duḥkhair dīnaḥ saumitrim abravīt  Rambahūni rakṣasāṃ vāse varṣāṇi vasatā sukhamanena daṇḍakāraṇye vicīrṇam iha pakṣiṇā  Ramanekavārṣiko yas tu cirakālaṃ samutthitaḥso yam adya hataḥ śete kālo hi duratikramaḥ  Rampaśya lakṣmaṇa gṛdhro yam upakārī hataś ca mesītām abhyavapan no vai rāvaṇena balīyasā  Ramgṛdhrarājyaṃ parityajya pitṛpaitāmahaṃ mahatmama hetor ayaṃ prāṇān mumoca patageśvaraḥ  Ramsarvatra khalu dṛśyante sādhavo dharmacāriṇaḥśūrāḥ śaraṇyāḥ saumitre tiryagyonigateṣv api  Ramsītāharaṇajaṃ duḥkhaṃ na me saumya tathāgatamyathā vināśo gṛdhrasya matkṛte ca paraṃtapa  Ramrājā daśarathaḥ śrīmān yathā mama mahāyaśāḥpūjanīyaś ca mānyaś ca tathāyaṃ patageśvaraḥ  Ramsaumitre hara kāṣṭhāni nirmathiṣyāmi pāvakamgṛdhrarājaṃ didhakṣāmi matkṛte nidhanaṃ gatam  Ramnāthaṃ patagalokasya citām āropayāmy ahamimaṃ dhakṣyāmi saumitre hataṃ raudreṇa rakṣasā  Ramyā gatir yajñaśīlānām āhitāgneś ca yā gatiḥaparāvartināṃ yā ca yā ca bhūmipradāyinām  Rammayā tvaṃ samanujñāto gaccha lokān anuttamāngṛdhrarāja mahāsattva saṃskṛtaś ca mayā vraja  Ramevam uktvā citāṃ dīptām āropya patageśvaramdadāha rāmo dharmātmā svabandhum iva duḥkhitaḥ  Ramrāmo tha sahasaumitrir vanaṃ yātvā sa vīryavānsthūlān hatvā mahārohīn anu tastāra taṃ dvijam  Ramrohimāṃsāni coddhṛtya peśīkṛtvā mahāyaśāḥśakunāya dadau rāmo ramye haritaśādvale  Ramyat tat pretasya martyasya kathayanti dvijātayaḥtat svargagamanaṃ tasya kṣipraṃ rāmo jajāpa ha  Ramtato godāvarīṃ gatvā nadīṃ naravarātmajauudakaṃ cakratus tasmai gṛdhrarājāya tāv ubhau  Ramsa gṛdhrarājaḥ kṛtavān yaśaskaraṃ suduṣkaraṃ karma raṇe nipātitaḥmaharṣikalpena ca saṃskṛtas tadā jagāma puṇyāṃ gatim ātmanaḥ śubhām  Ramkṛtvaivam udakaṃ tasmai prasthitau rāghavau tadāavekṣantau vane sītāṃ paścimāṃ jagmatur diśam  Ramtāṃ diśaṃ dakṣiṇāṃ gatvā śaracāpāsidhāriṇauaviprahatam aikṣvākau panthānaṃ pratipedatuḥ  Ramgulmair vṛkṣaiś ca bahubhir latābhiś ca praveṣṭitamāvṛtaṃ sarvato durgaṃ gahanaṃ ghoradarśanam  Ramvyatikramya tu vegena gṛhītvā dakṣiṇāṃ diśamsubhīmaṃ tan mahāraṇyaṃ vyatiyātau mahābalau  Ramtataḥ paraṃ janasthānāt trikrośaṃ gamya rāghavaukrauñcāraṇyaṃ viviśatur gahanaṃ tau mahaujasau  Ramnānāmeghaghanaprakhyaṃ prahṛṣṭam iva sarvataḥnānāvarṇaiḥ śubhaiḥ puṣpair mṛgapakṣigaṇair yutam  Ramdidṛkṣamāṇau vaidehīṃ tad vanaṃ tau vicikyatuḥtatra tatrāvatiṣṭhantau sītāharaṇakarśitau  Ramlakṣmaṇas tu mahātejāḥ sattvavāñ śīlavāñ śuciḥabravīt prāñjalir vākyaṃ bhrātaraṃ dīptatejasam  Ramspandate me dṛḍhaṃ bāhur udvignam iva me manaḥprāyaśaś cāpy aniṣṭāni nimittāny upalakṣaye  Ramtasmāt sajjībhavārya tvaṃ kuruṣva vacanaṃ hitammamaiva hi nimittāni sadyaḥ śaṃsanti sambhramam  Rameṣa vañculako nāma pakṣī paramadāruṇaḥāvayor vijayaṃ yuddhe śaṃsann iva vinardati  Ramtayor anveṣator evaṃ sarvaṃ tad vanam ojasāsaṃjajñe vipulaḥ śabdaḥ prabhañjann iva tad vanam  Ramsaṃveṣṭitam ivātyarthaṃ gahanaṃ mātariśvanāvanasya tasya śabdo bhūd divam āpūrayann iva  Ramtaṃ śabdaṃ kāṅkṣamāṇas tu rāmaḥ kakṣe sahānujaḥdadarśa sumahākāyaṃ rākṣasaṃ vipulorasam  Ramāsedatus tatas tatra tāv ubhau pramukhe sthitamvivṛddham aśirogrīvaṃ kabandham udare mukham  Ramromabhir nicitais tīkṣṇair mahāgirim ivocchritamnīlameghanibhaṃ raudraṃ meghastanitaniḥsvanam  Rammahāpakṣmeṇa piṅgena vipulenāyatena caekenorasi ghoreṇa nayanenāśudarśinā  Rammahādaṃṣṭropapannaṃ taṃ lelihānaṃ mahāmukhambhakṣayantaṃ mahāghorān ṛkṣasiṃhamṛgadvipān  Ramghorau bhujau vikurvāṇam ubhau yojanam āyataukarābhyāṃ vividhān gṛhya ṛkṣān pakṣigaṇān mṛgān  Ramākarṣantaṃ vikarṣantam anekān mṛgayūthapānsthitam āvṛtya panthānaṃ tayor bhrātroḥ prapannayoḥ  Ramatha tau samatikramya krośamātre dadarśatuḥmahāntaṃ dāruṇaṃ bhīmaṃ kabandhaṃ bhujasaṃvṛtam  Ramsa mahābāhur atyarthaṃ prasārya vipulau bhujaujagrāha sahitāv eva rāghavau pīḍayan balāt  Ramkhaḍginau dṛḍhadhanvānau tigmatejau mahābhujaubhrātarau vivaśaṃ prāptau kṛṣyamāṇau mahābalau  Ramtāv uvāca mahābāhuḥ kabandho dānavottamaḥkau yuvāṃ vṛṣabhaskandhau mahākhaḍgadhanurdharau  Ramghoraṃ deśam imaṃ prāptau mama bhakṣāv upasthitauvadataṃ kāryam iha vāṃ kimarthaṃ cāgatau yuvām  Ramimaṃ deśam anuprāptau kṣudhārtasyeha tiṣṭhataḥsabāṇacāpakhaḍgau ca tīkṣṇaśṛṅgāv ivarṣabhaumamāsyam anusaṃprāptau durlabhaṃ jīvitaṃ punaḥ  Ramtasya tadvacanaṃ śrutvā kabandhasya durātmanaḥuvāca lakṣmaṇaṃ rāmo mukhena pariśuṣyatā  Ramkṛcchrāt kṛcchrataraṃ prāpya dāruṇaṃ satyavikramavyasanaṃ jīvitāntāya prāptam aprāpya tāṃ priyām  Ramkālasya sumahad vīryaṃ sarvabhūteṣu lakṣmaṇatvāṃ ca māṃ ca naravyāghra vyasanaiḥ paśya mohitaunātibhāro sti daivasya sarvabhūteṣu lakṣmaṇa  Ramśūrāś ca balavantaś ca kṛtāstrāś ca raṇājirekālābhipannāḥ sīdanti yathā vālukasetavaḥ  Ramiti bruvāṇo dṛḍhasatyavikramo mahāyaśā dāśarathiḥ pratāpavānavekṣya saumitrim udagravikramaṃ sthirāṃ tadā svāṃ matim ātmanākarot  Ramtau tu tatra sthitau dṛṣṭvā bhrātarau rāmalakṣmaṇaubāhupāśaparikṣiptau kabandho vākyam abravīt  Ramtiṣṭhataḥ kiṃ nu māṃ dṛṣṭvā kṣudhārtaṃ kṣatriyarṣabhauāhārārthaṃ tu saṃdiṣṭau daivena gatacetasau  Ramtac chrutvā lakṣmaṇo vākyaṃ prāptakālaṃ hitaṃ tadāuvācārtisamāpanno vikrame kṛtaniścayaḥ  Ramtvāṃ ca māṃ ca purā tūrṇam ādatte rākṣasādhamaḥtasmād asibhyām asyāśu bāhū chindāvahai gurū  Ramtatas tau deśakālajñau khaḍgābhyām eva rāghavauachindatāṃ susaṃhṛṣṭau bāhū tasyāṃsadeśayoḥ  Ramdakṣiṇo dakṣiṇaṃ bāhum asaktam asinā tataḥcicheda rāmo vegena savyaṃ vīras tu lakṣmaṇaḥ  Ramsa papāta mahābāhuś chinnabāhur mahāsvanaḥkhaṃ ca gāṃ ca diśaś caiva nādayañ jalado yathā  Ramsa nikṛttau bhujau dṛṣṭvā śoṇitaughapariplutaḥdīnaḥ papraccha tau vīrau kau yuvām iti dānavaḥ  Ramiti tasya bruvāṇasya lakṣmaṇaḥ śubhalakṣaṇaḥśaśaṃsa tasya kākutsthaṃ kabandhasya mahābalaḥ  Ramayam ikṣvākudāyādo rāmo nāma janaiḥ śrutaḥasyaivāvarajaṃ viddhi bhrātaraṃ māṃ ca lakṣmaṇam  Ramasya devaprabhāvasya vasato vijane vanerakṣasāpahṛtā bhāryā yām icchantāv ihāgatau  Ramtvaṃ tu ko vā kimarthaṃ vā kabandha sadṛśo vaneāsyenorasi dīptena bhagnajaṅgho viceṣṭase  Ramevam uktaḥ kabandhas tu lakṣmaṇenottaraṃ vacaḥuvāca paramaprītas tad indravacanaṃ smaran  Ramsvāgataṃ vāṃ naravyāghrau diṣṭyā paśyāmi cāpy ahamdiṣṭyā cemau nikṛttau me yuvābhyāṃ bāhubandhanau  Ramvirūpaṃ yac ca me rūpaṃ prāptaṃ hy avinayād yathātan me śṛṇu naravyāghra tattvataḥ śaṃsatas tava  Rampurā rāma mahābāho mahābalaparākramarūpam āsīn mamācintyaṃ triṣu lokeṣu viśrutamyathā somasya śakrasya sūryasya ca yathā vapuḥ  Ramso haṃ rūpam idaṃ kṛtvā lokavitrāsanaṃ mahatṛṣīn vanagatān rāma trāsayāmi tatas tataḥ  Ramtataḥ sthūlaśirā nāma maharṣiḥ kopito mayāsaṃcinvan vividhaṃ vanyaṃ rūpeṇānena dharṣitaḥ  Ramtenāham uktaḥ prekṣyaivaṃ ghoraśāpābhidhāyināetad eva nṛśaṃsaṃ te rūpam astu vigarhitam  Ramsa mayā yācitaḥ kruddhaḥ śāpasyānto bhaved itiabhiśāpakṛtasyeti tenedaṃ bhāṣitaṃ vacaḥ  Ramyadā chittvā bhujau rāmas tvāṃ dahed vijane vanetadā tvaṃ prāpsyase rūpaṃ svam eva vipulaṃ śubham  Ramśriyā virājitaṃ putraṃ danos tvaṃ viddhi lakṣmaṇaindrakopād idaṃ rūpaṃ prāptam evaṃ raṇājire  Ramahaṃ hi tapasogreṇa pitāmaham atoṣayamdīrgham āyuḥ sa me prādāt tato māṃ vibhramo spṛśat  Ramdīrgham āyur mayā prāptaṃ kiṃ me śakraḥ kariṣyatiity evaṃ buddhim āsthāya raṇe śakram adharṣayam  Ramtasya bāhupramuktena vajreṇa śataparvaṇāsakthinī ca śiraś caiva śarīre saṃpraveśitam  Ramsa mayā yācyamānaḥ sann ānayad yamasādanampitāmahavacaḥ satyaṃ tad astv iti mamābravīt  Ramanāhāraḥ kathaṃ śakto bhagnasakthiśiromukhaḥvajreṇābhihataḥ kālaṃ sudīrgham api jīvitum  Ramevam uktas tu me śakro bāhū yojanam āyatauprādād āsyaṃ ca me kukṣau tīkṣṇadaṃṣṭram akalpayat  Ramso haṃ bhujābhyāṃ dīrghābhyāṃ samākṛṣya vanecarānsiṃhadvipamṛgavyāghrān bhakṣayāmi samantataḥ  Ramsa tu mām abravīd indro yadā rāmaḥ salakṣmaṇaḥchetsyate samare bāhū tadā svargaṃ gamiṣyasi  Ramsa tvaṃ rāmo si bhadraṃ te nāham anyena rāghavaśakyo hantuṃ yathātattvam evam uktaṃ maharṣiṇā  Ramahaṃ hi matisācivyaṃ kariṣyāmi nararṣabhamitraṃ caivopadekṣyāmi yuvābhyāṃ saṃskṛto gninā  Ramevam uktas tu dharmātmā danunā tena rāghavaḥidaṃ jagāda vacanaṃ lakṣmaṇasyopaśṛṇvataḥ  Ramrāvaṇena hṛtā sītā mama bhāryā yaśasvinīniṣkrāntasya janasthānāt saha bhrātrā yathāsukham  Ramnāmamātraṃ tu jānāmi na rūpaṃ tasya rakṣasaḥnivāsaṃ vā prabhāvaṃ vā vayaṃ tasya na vidmahe  Ramśokārtānām anāthānām evaṃ viparidhāvatāmkāruṇyaṃ sadṛśaṃ kartum upakāre ca vartatām  Ramkāṣṭhāny ānīya śuṣkāṇi kāle bhagnāni kuñjaraiḥbhakṣyāmas tvāṃ vayaṃ vīra śvabhre mahati kalpite  Ramsa tvaṃ sītāṃ samācakṣva yena vā yatra vā hṛtākuru kalyāṇam atyarthaṃ yadi jānāsi tattvataḥ  Ramevam uktas tu rāmeṇa vākyaṃ danur anuttamamprovāca kuśalo vaktuṃ vaktāram api rāghavam  Ramdivyam asti na me jñānaṃ nābhijānāmi maithilīmyas tāṃ jñāsyati taṃ vakṣye dagdhaḥ svaṃ rūpam āsthitaḥ  Ramadagdhasya hi vijñātuṃ śaktir asti na me prabhorākṣasaṃ taṃ mahāvīryaṃ sītā yena hṛtā tava  Ramvijñānaṃ hi mahad bhraṣṭaṃ śāpadoṣeṇa rāghavasvakṛtena mayā prāptaṃ rūpaṃ lokavigarhitam  Ramkiṃ tu yāvan na yāty astaṃ savitā śrāntavāhanaḥtāvan mām avaṭe kṣiptvā daha rāma yathāvidhi  Ramdagdhas tvayāham avaṭe nyāyena raghunandanavakṣyāmi tam ahaṃ vīra yas taṃ jñāsyati rākṣasam  Ramtena sakhyaṃ ca kartavyaṃ nyāyyavṛttena rāghavakalpayiṣyati te prītaḥ sāhāyyaṃ laghuvikramaḥ  Ramna hi tasyāsty avijñātaṃ triṣu lokeṣu rāghavasarvān parisṛto lokān purā vai kāraṇāntare  Ramevam uktau tu tau vīrau kabandhena nareśvaraugiripradaram āsādya pāvakaṃ visasarjatuḥ  Ramlakṣmaṇas tu maholkābhir jvalitābhiḥ samantataḥcitām ādīpayāmāsa sā prajajvāla sarvataḥ  Ramtac charīraṃ kabandhasya ghṛtapiṇḍopamaṃ mahatmedasā pacyamānasya mandaṃ dahati pāvakaḥ  Ramsa vidhūya citām āśu vidhūmo gnir ivotthitaḥaraje vāsasī bibhran mālāṃ divyāṃ mahābalaḥ  Ramtataś citāyā vegena bhāsvaro virajāmbaraḥutpapātāśu saṃhṛṣṭaḥ sarvapratyaṅgabhūṣaṇaḥ  Ramvimāne bhāsvare tiṣṭhan haṃsayukte yaśaskareprabhayā ca mahātejā diśo daśa virājayan  Ramso ntarikṣagato rāmaṃ kabandho vākyam abravītśṛṇu rāghava tattvena yathā sīmām avāpsyasi  Ramrāma ṣaḍ yuktayo loke yābhiḥ sarvaṃ vimṛśyateparimṛṣṭo daśāntena daśābhāgena sevyate  Ramdaśābhāgagato hīnas tvaṃ rāma sahalakṣmaṇaḥyat kṛte vyasanaṃ prāptaṃ tvayā dārapradharṣaṇam  Ramtad avaśyaṃ tvayā kāryaḥ sa suhṛt suhṛdāṃ varaakṛtvā na hi te siddhim ahaṃ paśyāmi cintayan  Ramśrūyatāṃ rāma vakṣyāmi sugrīvo nāma vānaraḥbhrātrā nirastaḥ kruddhena vālinā śakrasūnunā  Ramṛṣyamūke girivare pampāparyantaśobhitenivasaty ātmavān vīraś caturbhiḥ saha vānaraiḥ  Ramvayasyaṃ taṃ kuru kṣipram ito gatvādya rāghavaadrohāya samāgamya dīpyamāne vibhāvasau  Ramna ca te so vamantavyaḥ sugrīvo vānarādhipaḥkṛtajñaḥ kāmarūpī ca sahāyārthī ca vīryavān  Ramśaktau hy adya yuvāṃ kartuṃ kāryaṃ tasya cikīrṣitamkṛtārtho vākṛtārtho vā kṛtyaṃ tava kariṣyati  Ramsa ṛkṣarajasaḥ putraḥ pampām aṭati śaṅkitaḥbhāskarasyaurasaḥ putro vālinā kṛtakilbiṣaḥ  Ramsaṃnidhāyāyudhaṃ kṣipram ṛṣyamūkālayaṃ kapimkuru rāghava satyena vayasyaṃ vanacāriṇam  Ramsa hi sthānāni sarvāṇi kārtsnyena kapikuñjaraḥnaramāṃsāśināṃ loke naipuṇyād adhigacchati  Ramna tasyāviditaṃ loke kiṃcid asti hi rāghavayāvat sūryaḥ pratapati sahasrāṃśur ariṃdama  Ramsa nadīr vipulāñ śailān giridurgāṇi kandarānanviṣya vānaraiḥ sārdhaṃ patnīṃ te dhigamiṣyati  Ramvānarāṃś ca mahākāyān preṣayiṣyati rāghavadiśo vicetuṃ tāṃ sītāṃ tvadviyogena śocatīm  Ramsa meruśṛṅgāgragatām aninditāṃ praviśya pātālatale pi vāśritāmplavaṃgamānāṃ pravaras tava priyāṃ nihatya rakṣāṃsi punaḥ pradāsyati  Ramnidarśayitvā rāmāya sītāyāḥ pratipādanevākyam anvartham arthajñaḥ kabandhaḥ punar abravīt  Rameṣa rāma śivaḥ panthā yatraite puṣpitā drumāḥpratīcīṃ diśam āśritya prakāśante manoramāḥ  Ramjambūpriyālapanasāḥ plakṣanyagrodhatindukāḥaśvatthāḥ karṇikārāś ca cūtāś cānye ca pādapāḥ  Ramtān āruhyāthavā bhūmau pātayitvā ca tān balātphalāny amṛtakalpāni bhakṣayantau gamiṣyathaḥ  Ramcaṅkramantau varān deśāñ śailāc chailaṃ vanād vanamtataḥ puṣkariṇīṃ vīrau pampāṃ nāma gamiṣyathaḥ  Ramaśarkarām avibhraṃśāṃ samatīrtham aśaivalāmrāma saṃjātavālūkāṃ kamalotpalaśobhitām  Ramtatra haṃsāḥ plavāḥ krauñcāḥ kurarāś caiva rāghavavalgusvarā nikūjanti pampāsalilagocarāḥ  Ramnodvijante narān dṛṣṭvā vadhasyākovidāḥ śubhāḥghṛtapiṇḍopamān sthūlāṃs tān dvijān bhakṣayiṣyathaḥ  Ramrohitān vakratuṇḍāṃś ca nalamīnāṃś ca rāghavapampāyām iṣubhir matsyāṃs tatra rāma varān hatān  Ramnistvakpakṣān ayastaptān akṛśān ekakaṇṭakāntava bhaktyā samāyukto lakṣmaṇaḥ sampradāsyati  Rambhṛśaṃ te khādato matsyān pampāyāḥ puṣpasaṃcayepadmagandhi śivaṃ vāri sukhaśītam anāmayam  Ramuddhṛtya sa tadākliṣṭaṃ rūpyasphaṭikasaṃnibhamatha puṣkaraparṇena lakṣmaṇaḥ pāyayiṣyati  Ramsthūlān giriguhāśayyān varāhān vanacāriṇaḥapāṃ lobhād upāvṛttān vṛṣabhān iva nardataḥrūpānvitāṃś ca pampāyāṃ drakṣyasi tvaṃ narottama  Ramsāyāhne vicaran rāma viṭapīnmālyadhāriṇaḥśītodakaṃ ca pampāyāṃ dṛṣṭvā śokaṃ vihāsyasi  Ramsumanobhiś citāṃs tatra tilakān naktamālakānutpalāni ca phullāni paṅkajāni ca rāghava  Ramna tāni kaścin mālyāni tatrāropayitā naraḥmataṃgaśiṣyās tatrāsann ṛṣayaḥ susamāhitaḥ  Ramteṣāṃ bhārābhitaptānāṃ vanyam āharatāṃ guroḥye prapetur mahīṃ tūrṇaṃ śarīrāt svedabindavaḥ  Ramtāni mālyāni jātāni munīnāṃ tapasā tadāsvedabindusamutthāni na vinaśyanti rāghava  Ramteṣām adyāpi tatraiva dṛśyate paricāriṇīśramaṇī śabarī nāma kākutstha cirajīvinī  Ramtvāṃ tu dharme sthitā nityaṃ sarvabhūtanamaskṛtamdṛṣṭvā devopamaṃ rāma svargalokaṃ gamiṣyati  Ramtatas tad rāma pampāyās tīram āśritya paścimamāśramasthānam atulaṃ guhyaṃ kākutstha paśyasi  Ramna tatrākramituṃ nāgāḥ śaknuvanti tam āśramamṛṣes tasya mataṃgasya vidhānāt tac ca kānanam  Ramtasmin nandanasaṃkāśe devāraṇyopame vanenānāvihagasaṃkīrṇe raṃsyase rāma nirvṛtaḥ  Ramṛṣyamūkas tu pampāyāḥ purastāt puṣpitadrumaḥsuduḥkhārohaṇo nāma śiśunāgābhirakṣitaḥudāro brahmaṇā caiva pūrvakāle vinirmitaḥ  Ramśayānaḥ puruṣo rāma tasya śailasya mūrdhaniyat svapne labhate vittaṃ tat prabuddho dhigacchati  Ramna tv enaṃ viṣamācāraḥ pāpakarmādhirohatitatraiva praharanty enaṃ suptam ādāya rākṣasāḥ  Ramtato pi śiśunāgānām ākrandaḥ śrūyate mahānkrīḍatāṃ rāma pampāyāṃ mataṃgāraṇyavāsinām  Ramsiktā rudhiradhārābhiḥ saṃhatya paramadvipāḥpracaranti pṛthak kīrṇā meghavarṇās tarasvinaḥ  Ramte tatra pītvā pānīyaṃ vimalaṃ śītam avyayamnivṛttāḥ saṃvigāhante vanāni vanagocarāḥ  Ramrāma tasya tu śailasya mahatī śobhate guhāśilāpidhānā kākutstha duḥkhaṃ cāsyāḥ praveśanam  Ramtasyā guhāyāḥ prāgdvāre mahāñ śītodako hradaḥbahumūlaphalo ramyo nānānagasamāvṛtaḥ  Ramtasyāṃ vasati sugrīvaś caturbhiḥ saha vānaraiḥkadācicchikhare tasya parvatasyāvatiṣṭhate  Ramkabandhas tv anuśāsyaivaṃ tāv ubhau rāmalakṣmaṇausragvī bhāskaravarṇābhaḥ khe vyarocata vīryavān  Ramtaṃ tu khasthaṃ mahābhāgaṃ kabandhaṃ rāmalakṣmaṇauprasthitau tvaṃ vrajasveti vākyam ūcatur antikāt  Ramgamyatāṃ kāryasiddhyartham iti tāv abravīc ca saḥsuprītau tāv anujñāpya kabandhaḥ prasthitas tadā  Ramsa tat kabandhaḥ pratipadya rūpaṃ vṛtaḥ śriyā bhāskaratulyadehaḥnidarśayan rāmam avekṣya khasthaḥ sakhyaṃ kuruṣveti tadābhyuvāca  Ramtau kabandhena taṃ mārgaṃ pampāyā darśitaṃ vaneātasthatur diśaṃ gṛhya pratīcīṃ nṛvarātmajau  Ramtau śaileṣv ācitānekān kṣaudrakalpaphaladrumānvīkṣantau jagmatur draṣṭuṃ sugrīvaṃ rāmalakṣmaṇau  Ramkṛtvā ca śailapṛṣṭhe tu tau vāsaṃ raghunandanaupampāyāḥ paścimaṃ tīraṃ rāghavāv upatasthatuḥ  Ramtau puṣkariṇyāḥ pampāyās tīram āsādya paścimamapaśyatāṃ tatas tatra śabaryā ramyam āśramam  Ramtau tam āśramam āsādya drumair bahubhir āvṛtamsuramyam abhivīkṣantau śabarīm abhyupeyatuḥ  Ramtau tu dṛṣṭvā tadā siddhā samutthāya kṛtāñjaliḥpādau jagrāha rāmasya lakṣmaṇasya ca dhīmataḥ  Ramtām uvāca tato rāmaḥ śramaṇīṃ saṃśitavratāmkaccit te nirjitā vighnāḥ kaccit te vardhate tapaḥ  Ramkaccit te niyataḥ kopa āhāraś ca tapodhanekaccit te niyamāḥ prāptāḥ kaccit te manasaḥ sukhamkaccit te guruśuśrūṣā saphalā cārubhāṣiṇi  Ramrāmeṇa tāpasī pṛṣṭā sā siddhā siddhasaṃmatāśaśaṃsa śabarī vṛddhā rāmāya pratyupasthitā  Ramcitrakūṭaṃ tvayi prāpte vimānair atulaprabhaiḥitas te divam ārūḍhā yān ahaṃ paryacāriṣam  Ramtaiś cāham uktā dharmajñair mahābhāgair maharṣibhiḥāgamiṣyati te rāmaḥ supuṇyam imam āśramam  Ramsa te pratigrahītavyaḥ saumitrisahito tithiḥtaṃ ca dṛṣṭvā varāṃl lokān akṣayāṃs tvaṃ gamiṣyasi  Rammayā tu vividhaṃ vanyaṃ saṃcitaṃ puruṣarṣabhatavārthe puruṣavyāghra pampāyās tīrasambhavam  Ramevam uktaḥ sa dharmātmā śabaryā śabarīm idamrāghavaḥ prāha vijāne tāṃ nityam abahiṣkṛtām  Ramdanoḥ sakāśāt tattvena prabhāvaṃ te mahātmanaḥśrutaṃ pratyakṣam icchāmi saṃdraṣṭuṃ yadi manyase  Rametat tu vacanaṃ śrutvā rāmavaktrād viniḥsṛtamśabarī darśayāmāsa tāv ubhau tad vanaṃ mahat  Rampaśya meghaghanaprakhyaṃ mṛgapakṣisamākulammataṃgavanam ity eva viśrutaṃ raghunandana  Ramiha te bhāvitātmāno guravo me mahādyutejuhavāṃścakrire tīrthaṃ mantravan mantrapūjitam  Ramiyaṃ pratyaksthalī vedī yatra te me susatkṛtāḥpuṣpopahāraṃ kurvanti śramād udvepibhiḥ karaiḥ  Ramteṣāṃ tapaḥprabhāvena paśyādyāpi raghūttamadyotayanti diśaḥ sarvāḥ śriyā vedyo tulaprabhāḥ  Ramaśaknuvadbhis tair gantum upavāsaśramālasaiḥcintite bhyāgatān paśya sametān sapta sāgarān  Ramkṛtābhiṣekais tair nyastā valkalāḥ pādapeṣv ihaadyāpi na viśuṣyanti pradeśe raghunandana  Ramkṛtsnaṃ vanam idaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ śrotavyaṃ ca śrutaṃ tvayātad icchāmy abhyanujñātā tyaktum etat kalevaram  Ramteṣām icchāmy ahaṃ gantuṃ samīpaṃ bhāvitātmanāmmunīnām āśramo yeṣām ahaṃ ca paricāriṇī  Ramdharmiṣṭhaṃ tu vacaḥ śrutvā rāghavaḥ sahalakṣmaṇaḥanujānāmi gaccheti prahṛṣṭavadano bravīt  Ramanujñātā tu rāmeṇa hutvātmānaṃ hutāśanejvalatpāvakasaṃkāśā svargam eva jagāma sā  Ramyatra te sukṛtātmāno viharanti maharṣayaḥtat puṇyaṃ śabarī sthānaṃ jagāmātmasamādhinā  Ramdivaṃ tu tasyāṃ yātāyāṃ śabaryāṃ svena karmaṇālakṣmaṇena saha bhrātrā cintayāmāsa rāghavaḥ  Ramcintayitvā tu dharmātmā prabhāvaṃ taṃ mahātmanāmhitakāriṇam ekāgraṃ lakṣmaṇaṃ rāghavo bravīt  Ramdṛṣṭo yam āśramaḥ saumya bahvāścaryaḥ kṛtātmanāmviśvastamṛgaśārdūlo nānāvihagasevitaḥ  Ramsaptānāṃ ca samudrāṇām eṣu tīrtheṣu lakṣmaṇaupaspṛṣṭaṃ ca vidhivat pitaraś cāpi tarpitāḥ  Rampranaṣṭam aśubhaṃ yat tat kalyāṇaṃ samupasthitamtena tv etat prahṛṣṭaṃ me mano lakṣmaṇa samprati  Ramhṛdaye hi naravyāghra śubham āvirbhaviṣyatitad āgaccha gamiṣyāvaḥ pampāṃ tāṃ priyadarśanām  Ramṛśyamūko girir yatra nātidūre prakāśateyasmin vasati dharmātmā sugrīvo ṃśumataḥ sutaḥnityaṃ vālibhayāt trastaś caturbhiḥ saha vānaraiḥ  Ram abhitvare ca taṃ draṣṭuṃ sugrīvaṃ vānararṣabhamtadadhīnaṃ hi me saumya sītāyāḥ parimārgaṇam  Ramiti bruvāṇaṃ taṃ rāmaṃ saumitrir idam abravītgacchāvas tvaritaṃ tatra mamāpi tvarate manaḥ  Ramāśramāt tu tatas tasmān niṣkramya sa viśāṃ patiḥājagāma tataḥ pampāṃ lakṣmaṇena sahābhibhūḥ  Ramsamīkṣamāṇaḥ puṣpāḍhyaṃ sarvato vipuladrumamkoyaṣṭibhiś cārjunakaiḥ śatapattraiś ca kīcakaiḥetaiś cānyaiś ca vividhair nāditaṃ tad vanaṃ mahat  Ramsa rāmo vividhān vṛkṣān sarāṃsi vividhāni capaśyan kāmābhisaṃtapto jagāma paramaṃ hradam  Ramsa tām āsādya vai rāmo dūrād udakavāhinīmmataṃgasarasaṃ nāma hradaṃ samavagāhata  Ramsa tu śokasamāviṣṭo rāmo daśarathātmajaḥviveśa nalinīṃ pampāṃ paṅkajaiś ca samāvṛtām  Ramtilakāśokapuṃnāgabakuloddālakāśinīmramyopavanasambādhāṃ padmasaṃpīḍitodakām  Ramsphaṭikopamatoyāḍhyāṃ ślakṣṇavālukasaṃtatāmmatsyakacchapasambādhāṃ tīrasthadrumaśobhitām  Ramsakhībhir iva yuktābhir latābhir anuveṣṭitāmkiṃnaroragagandharvayakṣarākṣasasevitāmnānādrumalatākīrṇāṃ śītavārinidhiṃ śubhām  Rampadmaiḥ saugandhikais tāmrāṃ śuklāṃ kumudamaṇḍalaiḥnīlāṃ kuvalayoddhātair bahuvarṇāṃ kuthām iva  Ramaravindotpalavatīṃ padmasaugandhikāyutāmpuṣpitāmravaṇopetāṃ barhiṇodghuṣṭanāditām  Ramsa tāṃ dṛṣṭvā tataḥ pampāṃ rāmaḥ saumitriṇā sahavilalāpa ca tejasvī kāmād daśarathātmajaḥ  Ramtilakair bījapūraiś ca vaṭaiḥ śukladrumais tathāpuṣpitaiḥ karavīraiś ca puṃnāgaiś ca supuṣpitaiḥ  Rammālatīkundagulmaiś ca bhaṇḍīrair niculais tathāaśokaiḥ saptaparṇaiś ca ketakair atimuktakaiḥanyaiś ca vividhair vṛkṣaiḥ pramadevopaśobhitām  Ramasyās tīre tu pūrvoktaḥ parvato dhātumaṇḍitaḥṛśyamūka iti khyātaś citrapuṣpitakānanaḥ  Ramharir ṛkṣarajonāmnaḥ putras tasya mahātmanaḥadhyāste taṃ mahāvīryaḥ sugrīva iti viśrutaḥ  Ramsugrīvam abhigaccha tvaṃ vānarendraṃ nararṣabhaity uvāca punar vākyaṃ lakṣmaṇaṃ satyavikramam  Ramtato mahad vartma ca dūrasaṃkramaṃ krameṇa gatvā pravilokayan vanamdadarśa pampāṃ śubhadarśakānanām anekanānāvidhapakṣisaṃkulām
